综合 Letterboxd 评分、国际电影节奖项/首映信息和片型排序。点击卡片底部可跳转 MIFF 购票页或 Letterboxd。

#1格拉迪瓦 La Gradiva必看20 🎬 LB 4.06 长片
2026 · 145 分钟 · 剧情 · 新锐视野 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Marine Atlan · 法国、意大利
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文戛纳影评人周大奖｜澳大利亚首映
一位中学女教师带领二十名巴黎学生前往庞贝古城遗址，青春期的情感与矛盾在异国旅途中悄然滋长。被孤立的优等生苏珊娜在旁默默观察，幻想着自己能否融入这场情感漩涡。影片以细腻视角描摹青少年的内心动荡。
▸导演玛琳·阿特兰以摄影师身份获凯撒奖提名，本片为其长片处女作，画面细腻、光影斑斓，将意大利风光与青春情愫巧妙融合。▸改编自文学经典《格拉迪瓦》及弗洛伊德相关分析，赋予青春题材更深哲思，展现欲望与自我觉醒的复杂交错。▸荣获戛纳影评人周大奖，真实刻画青少年心理与群体动态，打破对青春的刻板印象，是当下欧洲青春片中的独特之作。

#2芭芭拉永存 Barbara Forever必看20 🎬 LB 3.96 长片
2026 · 102 分钟 · 纪录片 · 电影之梦 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Brydie O'Connor · 美国
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文柏林电影节泰迪熊奖、圣丹斯电影节最佳剪辑奖
本片通过珍贵档案和个人影像，追溯先锋女同志导演芭芭拉·哈默的艺术人生。她以大胆创新的镜头语言挑战主流视角，成为酷儿电影史上的重要人物。
▸导演布莱迪·奥康纳巧妙融合哈默本人的影像资料与访谈，使观众得以近距离感受这位酷儿电影先驱的真实声音与独特视角。▸影片不仅呈现了哈默的代表作片段，还深入探讨她对女性身份与性别表达的持续探索，展现酷儿影像的历史变革。▸荣获柏林电影节泰迪熊奖及圣丹斯最佳剪辑奖，艺术性与社会意义兼具，是理解酷儿电影发展不可错过的档案级纪录片。
MIFFLetterboxd
#3苍鹭 Blue Heron必看20 🎬 LB 3.93 长片
2025 · 90 分钟 · 剧情 · 新锐视野 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Sophy Romvari · 加拿大、匈牙利
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文洛迦诺电影节最佳首作奖、多伦多电影节加拿大新发现奖
在90年代的温哥华岛，匈牙利移民家庭的女孩萨莎在兄弟们的陪伴下成长，家中麻烦不断的哥哥让她童年蒙上阴影。成年后，萨莎作为电影人，翻看旧录像和回忆，试图理解自己成长的轨迹。本片以细腻视角展现家庭、记忆与自我认知。
▸导演Sophy Romvari以自传式手法，融合家庭影像与现实，呈现独特的情感质地，继短片《还在处理》后首度长片亮相，展现新锐女性导演的敏锐洞察力。▸影片以温柔但深刻的方式探讨移民家庭的成长与创伤，节奏舒缓，气氛真挚，适合在电影节大银幕上细细体会。▸荣获洛迦诺电影节最佳首作奖及多伦多电影节加拿大新发现奖，获国际影评人高度评价，被誉为“继《晒后假期》后最动人的成长电影”。

#4忧伤少女 Sad Girlz必看20 🎬 LB 3.90 长片
2026 · 90 分钟 · 剧情 · 学校单元 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Fernanda Tovar · 墨西哥
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文柏林电影节获奖作品｜澳大利亚首映
两位十六岁的墨西哥少女兼游泳队友，在一次聚会后经历创伤事件，友情与成长面临考验。她们尝试用现代科技和神秘方式寻求答案，探索青春期的复杂情感与自我认知。
▸导演费尔南达·托瓦尔以细腻、自然主义的影像风格，展现青春创伤与友谊的真实触感，阳光下的墨西哥日常令人印象深刻。▸影片巧妙融合现代元素如ChatGPT与塔罗牌，呈现当代青少年面对困境时的多元选择与心理变化。▸两位年轻演员表演真挚动人，情感张力十足，带来极具共鸣的观影体验，是MIFF学校单元不可错过的成长故事。

#5失落之地 Lost Land必看20 🎬 LB 3.86 长片
2025 · 99 分钟 · 剧情 · 亚太单元 · 维州首映 · 导演 Akio Fujimoto · 日本、法国、德国、Malaysia
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文威尼斯电影节地平线单元评审团特别奖
九岁女孩索米拉和四岁的弟弟沙菲被突然带离孟加拉难民营，踏上前往马来西亚的未知旅程。影片以孩童视角，展现他们在迁徙中的困惑与坚韧，聚焦罗兴亚族群的生存困境，兼具现实主义与情感力量。
▸日本导演藤本明男与罗兴亚真实家庭深度合作，历时多年打造首部全罗兴亚语电影，展现罕见的民族视角。▸采用纪实与虚构融合的手法，摄影师北川义男以沉浸式影像捕捉儿童流亡过程的真实情感，观众将身临其境感受动荡与不安。▸荣获威尼斯电影节地平线单元评审团特别奖，影片以细腻笔触关注全球被忽视的人道危机，是亚洲太平洋单元不可错过的震撼之作。

#6玫瑰 Rose必看20 🎬 LB 3.85 长片
2026 · 93 分钟 · 剧情 · 主打佳片 · 维州首映 · 导演 Markus Schleinzer · 德国、奥地利
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文柏林电影节最佳主角银熊奖、维州首映
在十七世纪德国，身负弹伤的士兵“玫瑰”继承农庄并逐渐融入村庄生活，却隐藏着以男性身份伪装的秘密。随着婚姻与家庭压力逼近，她的真实身份面临揭露，故事探讨性别、身份与生存。
▸德国奥斯卡提名女星桑德拉·惠勒（《坠落的解剖》）奉献银熊奖获奖表演，展现复杂心理与历史人物的挣扎。▸导演Markus Schleinzer以真实历史为灵感，结合民间传说和性别跨越主题，呈现独特视角与深刻人物刻画。▸影片以冷峻写实的影像风格，重现三十年战争时期的欧洲乡村，带来沉浸式观影体验，适合在MIFF大银幕欣赏。

#7苍蝇 Flies必看20 🎬 LB 3.84 长片
2026 · 99 分钟 · 剧情、喜剧 · 拉丁美洲 · 维州首映 · 导演 Fernando Eimbcke · 墨西哥
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文柏林电影节主竞赛评审团奖、读者评审团奖
墨西哥老年女性奥尔加因经济困境不得不出租房间，迎来单亲父亲图利奥和九岁儿子克里斯蒂安。两人因家人患癌暂居奥尔加家，冷漠的奥尔加逐渐与乐观的孩子建立起温情联系。本片以幽默与温情交织，展现陌生人间的相互治愈。
▸导演费尔南多·艾姆布克以黑白影像打造出独特都市氛围，巧妙性别反转经典“陌生人携童同行”模式，带来新鲜视角。▸片中表演自然细腻，尤其是奥尔加与克里斯蒂安之间的情感变化，令人动容。▸曾获柏林电影节两项大奖，幽默与深刻并存，兼具社会现实与个人成长，适合喜欢拉美电影和温情喜剧的观众在MIFF大银幕体验。

#8獸兵衛忍風帖 Ninja Scroll必看20 🎬 LB 3.84 长片
1993 · 99 分钟 · 剧情、惊悚、奇幻 · 经典修复 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Yoshiaki Kawajiri · 日本
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文柏林电影节公开复活；导演参与4K修复；澳洲首映
浪人兽兵卫在战国乱世邂逅女忍者胧和神秘密探，三人联手对抗八名拥有超凡能力的恶忍，踏上生死未卜的险途。本片融合动作、奇幻与悬疑元素，展现忍者世界的残酷与魅力。
▸导演川尻善昭亲自参与修复，4K胶片动画重现1990年代日本动画巅峰，画面细节与色彩震撼升级，极具收藏与观赏价值。▸动作场面以极致的暴力美学和流畅的忍者对决著称，怪异角色与超现实设定令人目不暇接，是后世多部电影与动画的灵感源泉。▸曾于柏林电影节公开复活，MIFF澳洲首映，经典之作与《阿基拉》《攻壳机动队》齐名，值得大银幕重温其影响力与视觉冲击。

#9枯叶 Dry Leaf必看20 🎬 LB 3.83 长片
2025 · 186 分钟 · 剧情、实验 · 实验影像 · 维州首映 · 导演 Alexandre Koberidze · 德国、Georgia
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文洛迦诺电影节主竞赛特别提及奖、国际影评人费比西奖
年轻摄影师丽莎在拍摄格鲁吉亚各地破旧足球场时神秘失踪，父亲伊拉克利与同事列万踏上充满魔幻现实色彩的寻女之旅。影片以实验性的叙事方式，展现家庭情感与人生迷途。
▸导演亚历山大·科贝里泽继《我们仰望天空时会看到什么？》后，再次以独特视角探索格鲁吉亚人文与乡村风貌，延续其诗意与幽默。▸全片采用索尼爱立信老款手机拍摄，画面呈现像素化美学，赋予乡村景致抽象而新奇的视觉体验，极具实验电影魅力。▸演员阵容中导演父亲亲自出演，角色设定大胆——部分人物“隐形”，在现实与幻想之间自由游走，观众将体验一场独特的公路与家庭故事。

#10懦夫 Coward必看20 🎬 LB 3.79 长片
2026 · 120 分钟 · 剧情、Historical · 主打佳片 · 维州首映 · 导演 Lukas Dhont · 法国、比利时、荷兰
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文戛纳电影节双最佳男演员奖｜维州首映
1916年，第一次世界大战西线战壕中，两位性格迥异的年轻士兵皮埃尔与弗朗西斯在战火与压力下，因合作军中剧团而产生微妙情愫。本片通过隐秘的情感描绘，展现战争中的人性挣扎与自我认同。
▸《亲密》导演卢卡斯·栋特最新力作，以细腻视角探索男同性恋情在极端环境下的觉醒与挣扎。▸两位主演在戛纳电影节斩获最佳男演员奖，表演层次丰富，情感表达极具感染力。▸影片巧妙融合历史战争与青春成长元素，戏剧团体与战壕生活交错，展现独特舞台美学与视觉风格，是大银幕不可错过的观影体验。

#11哈酱，摇摆你的舞步！ Ha-Chan, Shake Your Booty!必看20 🎬 LB 3.72 长片
2026 · 122 分钟 · 喜剧 · 北美单元 · 维州首映 · 导演 Josef Kubota Wladyka · 美国
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文圣丹斯电影节最佳导演奖；维州首映
中年舞者哈酱在东京与丈夫共舞，却因突如其来的失去而陷入低谷。九个月后，家人鼓励她重返舞厅，并遇到充满魅力的新教练。影片以魔幻现实主义手法，展现她在舞蹈与人生间重拾自我与快乐。
▸导演Josef Kubota Wladyka以独特视角将悲伤题材与喜剧、魔幻现实主义巧妙融合，带来耳目一新的观影体验。▸奥斯卡提名演员菊地凛子出演哈酱，以精湛表演和舞技诠释情感转变，阵容还包括知名演员Edda、Guerra、You、吉田洋，跨语言、跨文化碰撞更丰富。▸影片在Sundance获最佳导演奖，精妙舞蹈编排、鲜明美术设计与欢快流行配乐相得益彰，让观众沉浸于多彩舞厅与人生起伏。

#12米诺陶 Minotaur必看20 🎬 LB 3.71 长片
2026 · 141 分钟 · 剧情、惊悚、犯罪 · 主打佳片 · 维州首映 · 导演 Andrey Zvyagintsev · Russia
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文2026年戛纳电影节评审团大奖；MIFF维州首映
富有的企业CEO格列布被迫为俄乌战争征募员工，正值妻子与年轻艺术家偷情，事业与家庭危机交织，逼近一场令人震惊的对决。本片以尖锐视角揭示现代俄罗斯的腐败与道德失落，兼具心理惊悚与社会批判。
▸安德烈·萨金采夫时隔十年重返大银幕，继《无爱可诉》后再度以独特视角审视当代俄罗斯，影片在流亡法国期间创作，愤怒与精准兼具。▸以经典犯罪题材为骨架，融合政治讽刺与男性心理剖析，影像冷峻细腻，幽默感辛辣，展现导演对社会与人性的深刻洞察。▸荣获2026年戛纳电影节评审团大奖，成为年度影坛焦点，MIFF首映机会难得，适合关注国际时政与高质量艺术电影的观众。

#13百万之一 One in a Million必看20 🎬 LB 3.69 长片
2026 · 102 分钟 · 纪录片 · 纪录片单元 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Jack MacInnes, Itab Azzam · 美国、英国
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文圣丹斯电影节纪录片竞赛观众奖、最佳导演奖；澳大利亚首映
本片记录叙利亚女孩伊斯拉从11岁逃离阿勒颇，到在德国科隆成长为成年人的十年历程。她在异国他乡面对语言、文化和家庭传统的冲突，展现难民身份下的成长与坚韧。
▸导演伊塔布·阿扎姆本人是叙利亚人，与主角家庭建立深厚情感，带来极为亲密真实的视角。▸历时十年拍摄，捕捉难民少女在欧洲的成长与归乡，展现战争、迁徙与家庭的复杂影响。▸荣获圣丹斯纪录片竞赛观众奖和最佳导演奖，影片兼具情感力量与社会深度，是不可错过的难民题材力作。

#14不速之客 The Incomer必看20 🎬 LB 3.68 长片
2026 · 102 分钟 · 喜剧 · 主打佳片 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Louis Paxton · 英国
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文圣丹斯电影节NEXT单元创新奖；澳大利亚首映
在苏格兰偏远岛屿上，成年兄妹伊拉与桑迪过着与世隔绝的生活。一次外来官员的到访打破了他们的平静，三人之间展开一场荒诞又温情的喜剧较量，探索孤独、归属与家庭的边界。
▸导演Louis Paxton以苏格兰童年记忆为灵感，巧妙融合荒诞幽默与地方神话，呈现独特的影像风格与地域氛围。▸主演Gayle Rankin（《龙之家族》）奉献大胆精彩的表演，配合Grant O’Rourke、Domhnall Gleeson等实力演员，角色鲜明，化学反应十足。▸荣获圣丹斯电影节NEXT单元创新奖，代表新锐导演的独特视角与创作活力，是不可错过的年度喜剧新声。

#15黑神与白魔 Black God, White Devil必看20 🎬 LB 3.77 长片
1964 · 120 分钟 · 剧情 · Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels · 导演 Glauber Rocha · 巴西
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文1964年戛纳电影节竞赛片，获国际影评人费比西奖
在1940年代巴西旱原，农场工人曼努埃尔因杀害老板被迫与妻子逃亡，两人卷入宗教叛乱与暴力冲突之中。影片以政治寓言和史诗气质，展现边缘人物对抗压迫的悲剧命运。

#1格拉迪瓦 La Gradiva必看20 🎬 LB 4.06 长片
2026 · 145 分钟 · 剧情 · 新锐视野 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Marine Atlan · 法国、意大利
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文戛纳影评人周大奖｜澳大利亚首映
一位中学女教师带领二十名巴黎学生前往庞贝古城遗址，青春期的情感与矛盾在异国旅途中悄然滋长。被孤立的优等生苏珊娜在旁默默观察，幻想着自己能否融入这场情感漩涡。影片以细腻视角描摹青少年的内心动荡。
英文原文简介Passionate but put-upon teacher Madame Mercier (Antonia Buresi, Rodeo , MIFF 2022) shepherds 20 of her students from Paris to Naples, where they will visit the sites devastated by Mount Vesuvius two millennia prior. Being in such close quarters for an extended period heightens the high schoolers’ extant dynamics. Boisterous Toni yearns for his best friend James, who canoodles with his classmate Angela, herself vexed by masculine insensitivity. Meanwhile, ostracised star pupil Suzanne observes and fantasises about how she might become embroiled. Surrounded by scenes of calamity, the teenagers confront the crises within themselves. Inspired by Wilhelm Jensen’s novella Gradiva: A Pompeiian Fancy and Sigmund Freud’s analysis of it, César-nominated cinematographer Marine Atlan’s searing full-length debut is a rare work that dramatises the turmoil of adolescence without recycling tired tropes about caprice or rebellion. Juxtaposing the transitory nature of youth with the timelessness of Pompeii’s ruins, Atlan also captures the human penchant for concealing emotions and their inevitable eruption when surface and substance no longer coincide. Glorious, sun-dappled cinematography enriches the film’s illuminating studies of each character, while the naturalistic performances of its breakout cast bring authenticity and verve to this visionary coming-of-age tale.
▸导演玛琳·阿特兰以摄影师身份获凯撒奖提名，本片为其长片处女作，画面细腻、光影斑斓，将意大利风光与青春情愫巧妙融合。▸改编自文学经典《格拉迪瓦》及弗洛伊德相关分析，赋予青春题材更深哲思，展现欲望与自我觉醒的复杂交错。▸荣获戛纳影评人周大奖，真实刻画青少年心理与群体动态，打破对青春的刻板印象，是当下欧洲青春片中的独特之作。

#2芭芭拉永存 Barbara Forever必看20 🎬 LB 3.96 长片
2026 · 102 分钟 · 纪录片 · 电影之梦 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Brydie O'Connor · 美国
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文柏林电影节泰迪熊奖、圣丹斯电影节最佳剪辑奖
本片通过珍贵档案和个人影像，追溯先锋女同志导演芭芭拉·哈默的艺术人生。她以大胆创新的镜头语言挑战主流视角，成为酷儿电影史上的重要人物。
英文原文简介Fearless Los Angeles–born artist Barbara Hammer was 30 years old and married to a man when she first heard the word “lesbian”. This life-changing discovery would, in turn, lead to the expansion of the vocabulary of queer cinema itself. Across her prolific career from her groundbreaking 1974 short Dyketactics through to her feature-length breakout Nitrate Kisses (MIFF 1993) and beyond – works variously composed of frankly sensual depictions of friends and lovers and cinematic images from a bygone era – Hammer’s filmography was as playful as it was relentless in decentring the heterosexual gaze. Brydie O’Connor’s energising tribute to this LGBTQIA+ icon artfully weaves together footage from the director’s personal archive with clips from her films, all accompanied by commentary from Hammer herself – with some sections recorded shortly before her passing in 2019 – as well as from Florrie Burke, the filmmaker’s widow. Winner of a Teddy Award at the 2026 Berlinale along with a prize for editing at Sundance, Barbara Forever looks to the future of queer filmmaking by honouring one of its greatest revolutionaries.
▸导演布莱迪·奥康纳巧妙融合哈默本人的影像资料与访谈，使观众得以近距离感受这位酷儿电影先驱的真实声音与独特视角。▸影片不仅呈现了哈默的代表作片段，还深入探讨她对女性身份与性别表达的持续探索，展现酷儿影像的历史变革。▸荣获柏林电影节泰迪熊奖及圣丹斯最佳剪辑奖，艺术性与社会意义兼具，是理解酷儿电影发展不可错过的档案级纪录片。

#3苍鹭 Blue Heron必看20 🎬 LB 3.93 长片

英文原文洛迦诺电影节最佳首作奖、多伦多电影节加拿大新发现奖

英文原文简介Eight-year-old Sasha (Eylul Guven) is growing up surrounded by brothers, one of a sprawling Hungarian immigrant family on Vancouver Island in the 1990s. The big family’s attention is captured by troubled elder brother Jeremy (Edik Beddoes), whose rebellious behaviour seems like a cry for help. Years later, now a filmmaker, Sasha (Amy Zimmer) combs through old home videos and bittersweet memories, trying to make sense of her formative years. Earning comparisons to Charlotte Wells’s beloved Aftersun (MIFF 2022), Blue Heron won the Swatch First Feature Award upon its premiere at Locarno and was crowned Best Canadian Discovery at TIFF. Sophy Romvari has directed a number of celebrated shorts including 2020’s Still Processing , effectively an autobiographical companion to Blue Heron ; her hugely impressive, affecting debut feature further confirms her as a major emerging voice in cinema.
▸导演Sophy Romvari以自传式手法，融合家庭影像与现实，呈现独特的情感质地，继短片《还在处理》后首度长片亮相，展现新锐女性导演的敏锐洞察力。▸影片以温柔但深刻的方式探讨移民家庭的成长与创伤，节奏舒缓，气氛真挚，适合在电影节大银幕上细细体会。▸荣获洛迦诺电影节最佳首作奖及多伦多电影节加拿大新发现奖，获国际影评人高度评价，被誉为“继《晒后假期》后最动人的成长电影”。

#5失落之地 Lost Land必看20 🎬 LB 3.86 长片
2025 · 99 分钟 · 剧情 · 亚太单元 · 维州首映 · 导演 Akio Fujimoto · 日本、法国、德国、Malaysia
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文威尼斯电影节地平线单元评审团特别奖
九岁女孩索米拉和四岁的弟弟沙菲被突然带离孟加拉难民营，踏上前往马来西亚的未知旅程。影片以孩童视角，展现他们在迁徙中的困惑与坚韧，聚焦罗兴亚族群的生存困境，兼具现实主义与情感力量。
英文原文简介When nine-year-old Somira and her four-year-old brother Shafi (played by real-life siblings Shomira Rias Uddin and Muhammad Shofik Rias Uddin) find themselves suddenly and inexplicably ripped from their lives in a Bangladeshi refugee camp, all they are told is that they going to find an uncle in Malaysia. Thus begins an uncertain, hazardous journey over days and then weeks – over land and by sea – that will take everything the siblings have to give and then some. As the first ever film spoken entirely in Rohingya, Lost Land approaches Somira and Shafi’s story with an intimate realism that invites audiences to do more than merely bear witness: the film envelops us in the children’s confusion and determination, embodying the instability of their lives on the move. Japanese director Akio Fujimoto spent years working with Rohingya people to bring this story to life, and he does so with tender empathy, while Yoshio Kitagawa’s beautifully immersive cinematography aids the film’s authenticity and emotional weight. Lost Land is a profound and poignant document of the human lives at the heart of a too-often-overlooked humanitarian crisis.
▸日本导演藤本明男与罗兴亚真实家庭深度合作，历时多年打造首部全罗兴亚语电影，展现罕见的民族视角。▸采用纪实与虚构融合的手法，摄影师北川义男以沉浸式影像捕捉儿童流亡过程的真实情感，观众将身临其境感受动荡与不安。▸荣获威尼斯电影节地平线单元评审团特别奖，影片以细腻笔触关注全球被忽视的人道危机，是亚洲太平洋单元不可错过的震撼之作。

#6玫瑰 Rose必看20 🎬 LB 3.85 长片
2026 · 93 分钟 · 剧情 · 主打佳片 · 维州首映 · 导演 Markus Schleinzer · 德国、奥地利
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文柏林电影节最佳主角银熊奖、维州首映
在十七世纪德国，身负弹伤的士兵“玫瑰”继承农庄并逐渐融入村庄生活，却隐藏着以男性身份伪装的秘密。随着婚姻与家庭压力逼近，她的真实身份面临揭露，故事探讨性别、身份与生存。
英文原文简介From the battlefields of the Thirty Years’ War, a soldier arrives in a small German village carrying a document proving his inheritance of a local farm. Facially scarred by a bullet wound, this mysterious figure proves himself to be hardworking and brave, and slowly but surely insinuates himself into the community. But the soldier has a secret: he is, in fact, a woman named Rose masquerading as a man. When she is married off to a neighbour’s daughter – with children expected from the union – Rose’s deception is put to the test. Sandra Hüller, the Academy Award–nominated star of Anatomy of a Fall (MIFF 2023), gives a tour-de-force performance as Rose that earned her the Silver Bear for Best Leading Performance at this year’s Berlinale. Taking real-world inspiration from the notorious case of Martin Guerre, as well as hundreds of historical accounts of gender transgression, Markus Schleinzer’s ( Angelo , MIFF 2019) third feature is a fascinating fictional character study.
▸德国奥斯卡提名女星桑德拉·惠勒（《坠落的解剖》）奉献银熊奖获奖表演，展现复杂心理与历史人物的挣扎。▸导演Markus Schleinzer以真实历史为灵感，结合民间传说和性别跨越主题，呈现独特视角与深刻人物刻画。▸影片以冷峻写实的影像风格，重现三十年战争时期的欧洲乡村，带来沉浸式观影体验，适合在MIFF大银幕欣赏。

英文原文柏林电影节主竞赛评审团奖、读者评审团奖
墨西哥老年女性奥尔加因经济困境不得不出租房间，迎来单亲父亲图利奥和九岁儿子克里斯蒂安。两人因家人患癌暂居奥尔加家，冷漠的奥尔加逐渐与乐观的孩子建立起温情联系。本片以幽默与温情交织，展现陌生人间的相互治愈。
英文原文简介Finally admitting she’s in financial dire straits, elderly sourpuss Olga rents out the spare room in her Mexico City apartment. Heeding her ad are Tulio and his nine-year-old son Cristian, who need lodgings as the mum of the family receives cancer treatment at the nearby hospital. At first, Olga begrudges them, hesitant to have a child in her living quarters. But as Tulio ventures out to look for work, she finds herself traversing the city alone with Cristian, whose wide-eyed optimism begins to melt her frosty exterior. Receiving the Competition Prize of the Ecumenical Jury and the Berliner Morgenpost Readers’ Jury Award at the Berlinale, Fernando Eimbcke’s fifth feature is a disarmingly winsome portrait of two people who come together despite – or perhaps because of – tragic circumstances. Shot in evocative black-and-white, Flies gender-flips the dynamic of films such as Alice in the Cities (MIFF 1975) and Paper Moon in its tale of an unwilling adult thrown together by fate with a child who is not their own, while the film’s humour is droll without dismissing the weightier themes at play: mortality, imminent grief, and the irreversibility of both time and loss of innocence. Anchored on powerhouse performances from Teresita Sánchez ( Tótem , MIFF 2023) and first-timer Bastian Escobar, Flies portrays the alchemy between the resignation of old age and the curiosity of youth that, in combination, paves the way for healing.
▸导演费尔南多·艾姆布克以黑白影像打造出独特都市氛围，巧妙性别反转经典“陌生人携童同行”模式，带来新鲜视角。▸片中表演自然细腻，尤其是奥尔加与克里斯蒂安之间的情感变化，令人动容。▸曾获柏林电影节两项大奖，幽默与深刻并存，兼具社会现实与个人成长，适合喜欢拉美电影和温情喜剧的观众在MIFF大银幕体验。

#8獸兵衛忍風帖 Ninja Scroll必看20 🎬 LB 3.84 长片
1993 · 99 分钟 · 剧情、惊悚、奇幻 · 经典修复 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Yoshiaki Kawajiri · 日本
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文柏林电影节公开复活；导演参与4K修复；澳洲首映
浪人兽兵卫在战国乱世邂逅女忍者胧和神秘密探，三人联手对抗八名拥有超凡能力的恶忍，踏上生死未卜的险途。本片融合动作、奇幻与悬疑元素，展现忍者世界的残酷与魅力。
英文原文简介In Edo period Japan, wandering ronin Jubei winds up in a village tyrannised by an iron giant; there, he saves the female ninja Kagero, who decides to join him. Crossing paths with Dakuan, a government spy, they are informed that Jubei must confront the Eight Devils of Kimon – a band of malevolent super-ninja hell-bent on overthrowing the shogunate. As the trio set out to vanquish evil, they quickly learn that it’s kill or be killed. First released in 1993, this legendary Animate Film production sits alongside Akira and Ghost in the Shell as a classic of its genre – one whose influence is evident in titles such as The Matrix , Kill Bill and Scott Pilgrim vs. the World (MIFF 2005). Restored in 4K with the involvement of director Yoshiaki Kawajiri and publicly revived at this year’s Berlinale, this cel-animated wonder is renowned for its action sequences featuring both visceral brutality and virtuosic movement. Expect cutthroat scuffles for power, raunchy sex scenes and plentiful larger-than-life creatures including a snake lady, a living hornet’s nest and a gay assassin who kills with near-invisible electric wires!
▸导演川尻善昭亲自参与修复，4K胶片动画重现1990年代日本动画巅峰，画面细节与色彩震撼升级，极具收藏与观赏价值。▸动作场面以极致的暴力美学和流畅的忍者对决著称，怪异角色与超现实设定令人目不暇接，是后世多部电影与动画的灵感源泉。▸曾于柏林电影节公开复活，MIFF澳洲首映，经典之作与《阿基拉》《攻壳机动队》齐名，值得大银幕重温其影响力与视觉冲击。

#9枯叶 Dry Leaf必看20 🎬 LB 3.83 长片
2025 · 186 分钟 · 剧情、实验 · 实验影像 · 维州首映 · 导演 Alexandre Koberidze · 德国、Georgia
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文洛迦诺电影节主竞赛特别提及奖、国际影评人费比西奖
年轻摄影师丽莎在拍摄格鲁吉亚各地破旧足球场时神秘失踪，父亲伊拉克利与同事列万踏上充满魔幻现实色彩的寻女之旅。影片以实验性的叙事方式，展现家庭情感与人生迷途。
英文原文简介When sports photographer Lisa vanished, she was working on an assignment documenting ramshackle football fields across the country. She has left behind a letter for her parents in Tbilisi instructing them not to follow her – a request that her father, Irakli (played by the filmmaker’s own father, David Koberidze), disregards. He attempts to retrace her cross-country path together with her colleague Levan – who, like many of the characters in this gentle and transfixing saga, happens to be invisible – but theirs is destined to be a sublimely digressive quest, punctuated by curious encounters. Shot entirely on an old Sony Ericsson camera phone and unfolding across an epic timescale, Alexandre Koberidze’s latest feature – winner of both a Competition Special Mention and the FIPRESCI Prize at Locarno Film Festival – combines the sense of melancholic whimsy that distinguished his previous feature, What Do We See When We Look at the Sky? (MIFF 2021), with its daring formal gambit, giving its images of the Georgian countryside a surprising, pixelated beauty at times verging on abstraction.
▸导演亚历山大·科贝里泽继《我们仰望天空时会看到什么？》后，再次以独特视角探索格鲁吉亚人文与乡村风貌，延续其诗意与幽默。▸全片采用索尼爱立信老款手机拍摄，画面呈现像素化美学，赋予乡村景致抽象而新奇的视觉体验，极具实验电影魅力。▸演员阵容中导演父亲亲自出演，角色设定大胆——部分人物“隐形”，在现实与幻想之间自由游走，观众将体验一场独特的公路与家庭故事。

#10懦夫 Coward必看20 🎬 LB 3.79 长片
2026 · 120 分钟 · 剧情、Historical · 主打佳片 · 维州首映 · 导演 Lukas Dhont · 法国、比利时、荷兰
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文戛纳电影节双最佳男演员奖｜维州首映
1916年，第一次世界大战西线战壕中，两位性格迥异的年轻士兵皮埃尔与弗朗西斯在战火与压力下，因合作军中剧团而产生微妙情愫。本片通过隐秘的情感描绘，展现战争中的人性挣扎与自我认同。
英文原文简介Lukas Dhont’s stirring latest film – which won its leads a pair of Best Actor prizes at Cannes – depicts a clandestine romance between two young men that blooms in the trenches of WWI. It’s 1916, and Pierre and Francis have been conscripted to fight on the Western Front. Nicknamed “Quiet Mouse”, the former is a handsome, brawny farmer who struggles to express himself; the latter, a tailor’s son, is flamboyant and creative. Francis is enlisted to direct a theatre troupe that will entertain the soldiers, a role that includes cross-dressing as the female lead. When Pierre is tasked with assisting the troupe, the pair’s opposing qualities draw them together – and collaboration evolves into something more.
▸《亲密》导演卢卡斯·栋特最新力作，以细腻视角探索男同性恋情在极端环境下的觉醒与挣扎。▸两位主演在戛纳电影节斩获最佳男演员奖，表演层次丰富，情感表达极具感染力。▸影片巧妙融合历史战争与青春成长元素，戏剧团体与战壕生活交错，展现独特舞台美学与视觉风格，是大银幕不可错过的观影体验。

#11哈酱，摇摆你的舞步！ Ha-Chan, Shake Your Booty!必看20 🎬 LB 3.72 长片
2026 · 122 分钟 · 喜剧 · 北美单元 · 维州首映 · 导演 Josef Kubota Wladyka · 美国
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文圣丹斯电影节最佳导演奖；维州首映
中年舞者哈酱在东京与丈夫共舞，却因突如其来的失去而陷入低谷。九个月后，家人鼓励她重返舞厅，并遇到充满魅力的新教练。影片以魔幻现实主义手法，展现她在舞蹈与人生间重拾自我与快乐。
英文原文简介Middle-aged Haru and her husband Luis are serious about ballroom, performing the rumba, tango and paso doble in competitions all over Tokyo. But after enduring a catastrophic loss, Haru loses her spark. Nine months on, her sister and her cousin decide something must change, so they cajole her back into the studio. Enter: sexy new dance instructor Fedir (complete with open marriage!), who might just pull Haru out of her rut. Josef Kubota Wladyka’s third feature is a refreshing spin on the grief drama, while Oscar nominee Rinko Kikuchi ( Kumiko, the Treasure Hunter , MIFF 2014) – as balletic on the dance floor as she is in her portrayal of emotional overload – delivers an affecting, multifaceted performance. Also starring Alejandro Edda, Alberto Guerra, You ( Nobody Knows , MIFF 2004) and Yoh Yoshida ( Like Father, Like Son , MIFF 2013), the film deftly moves between languages (English, Spanish, Japanese) and tones (melodramatic, soap-operatic, surrealist) – all of which are buoyed by magnificent choreography, vibrant production design and a joyous pop soundtrack. Dedicated to Wladyka’s dancer mother, Ha-Chan, Shake Your Booty! shows that when life gets tough, all it takes is to get back on your feet.
▸导演Josef Kubota Wladyka以独特视角将悲伤题材与喜剧、魔幻现实主义巧妙融合，带来耳目一新的观影体验。▸奥斯卡提名演员菊地凛子出演哈酱，以精湛表演和舞技诠释情感转变，阵容还包括知名演员Edda、Guerra、You、吉田洋，跨语言、跨文化碰撞更丰富。▸影片在Sundance获最佳导演奖，精妙舞蹈编排、鲜明美术设计与欢快流行配乐相得益彰，让观众沉浸于多彩舞厅与人生起伏。

#12米诺陶 Minotaur必看20 🎬 LB 3.71 长片
2026 · 141 分钟 · 剧情、惊悚、犯罪 · 主打佳片 · 维州首映 · 导演 Andrey Zvyagintsev · Russia
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文2026年戛纳电影节评审团大奖；MIFF维州首映
富有的企业CEO格列布被迫为俄乌战争征募员工，正值妻子与年轻艺术家偷情，事业与家庭危机交织，逼近一场令人震惊的对决。本片以尖锐视角揭示现代俄罗斯的腐败与道德失落，兼具心理惊悚与社会批判。
英文原文简介In the immediate wake of his nation’s invasion of Ukraine, wealthy company CEO Gleb is directed to provide cannon fodder for Russia’s war machine. As he is ‘volunteering’ men to be drafted from within his employee pool, he learns that his wife Galina is having an affair with a handsome young artist. This intersection of Gleb’s professional and private crises becomes a trigger point for a shocking showdown. After recovering from a near-fatal coma in 2021, dissident Russian director Andrey Zvyagintsev ( Loveless , MIFF 2017) has returned to reinterpret Claude Chabrol’s 1969 classic The Unfaithful Wife as a staunchly contemporary study of masculinity, both personal and political. His life in exile in France has only sharpened his fury at the current state of his fatherland, which is directed with exquisite precision not just at Putin and his cronies but also at the everyday collaborators, deliberate or accidental, who proliferate in the shadow of war. Shot in Latvia, Minotaur is a merciless thriller for our present times, with a crisp and cunning eye for detail and a savage streak of wry humour – a pièce de résistance in more ways than one.
▸安德烈·萨金采夫时隔十年重返大银幕，继《无爱可诉》后再度以独特视角审视当代俄罗斯，影片在流亡法国期间创作，愤怒与精准兼具。▸以经典犯罪题材为骨架，融合政治讽刺与男性心理剖析，影像冷峻细腻，幽默感辛辣，展现导演对社会与人性的深刻洞察。▸荣获2026年戛纳电影节评审团大奖，成为年度影坛焦点，MIFF首映机会难得，适合关注国际时政与高质量艺术电影的观众。

#13百万之一 One in a Million必看20 🎬 LB 3.69 长片
2026 · 102 分钟 · 纪录片 · 纪录片单元 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Jack MacInnes, Itab Azzam · 美国、英国
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文圣丹斯电影节纪录片竞赛观众奖、最佳导演奖；澳大利亚首映
本片记录叙利亚女孩伊斯拉从11岁逃离阿勒颇，到在德国科隆成长为成年人的十年历程。她在异国他乡面对语言、文化和家庭传统的冲突，展现难民身份下的成长与坚韧。
英文原文简介When we meet Israa, she’s 11 years old, hustling to help make money for her family. A refugee from Aleppo, Syria, she has only just embarked on a journey across countries, cultures and bureaucratic barriers to find asylum in Europe. Once she settles into her adopted home of Cologne, however, life offers different challenges: a new language and culture to learn, and newfound Western freedoms clashing with her family’s traditions. Finally returning to Aleppo a decade later as an adult and witnessing the devastation that lingers, Israa reflects that, for all the immediate hardships of war, “it’s not as hard as what comes after”. Across 2015 and 2016, at the height of the Syrian Civil War, over one million refugees entered Germany; but the story didn’t end there. Filmed over 10 years, this astonishing documentary – its emotional foundation built on the close relationship between Israa’s family and its directors, husband-and-wife team Jack MacInnes and Itab Azzam (herself born in Syria) – zooms in to relate one of those accounts in intimate detail. Both a narrative of displacement and assimilation and a shrine to the resilience of Syrian culture, this is a moving portrait of life flourishing in the wake of destruction.
▸导演伊塔布·阿扎姆本人是叙利亚人，与主角家庭建立深厚情感，带来极为亲密真实的视角。▸历时十年拍摄，捕捉难民少女在欧洲的成长与归乡，展现战争、迁徙与家庭的复杂影响。▸荣获圣丹斯纪录片竞赛观众奖和最佳导演奖，影片兼具情感力量与社会深度，是不可错过的难民题材力作。

#14不速之客 The Incomer必看20 🎬 LB 3.68 长片
2026 · 102 分钟 · 喜剧 · 主打佳片 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Louis Paxton · 英国
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文圣丹斯电影节NEXT单元创新奖；澳大利亚首映
在苏格兰偏远岛屿上，成年兄妹伊拉与桑迪过着与世隔绝的生活。一次外来官员的到访打破了他们的平静，三人之间展开一场荒诞又温情的喜剧较量，探索孤独、归属与家庭的边界。
英文原文简介Adult siblings Isla and Sandy have lived their entire lives on a remote and otherwise uninhabited Orkney island. Decades ago, before he died, their father warned them about “incomers” from the mainland; thus, apart from hunting seabirds and communing with imaginary beasts, the siblings spend their days training to fend off invaders. But when awkward government official Daniel is dispatched to evict the pair, nothing goes quite to plan. Winning the Innovator Award in Sundance’s NEXT program for new filmmaking talent, The Incomer heralds writer/director Louis Paxton as an excitingly fresh voice in cinema. With a keen eye for the picturesque vistas of the northern Scottish environment where he spent his childhood and shot this film, Paxton mines the mysterious magic of the landscape – its beauty, decay and embedded mythology – as a key part of his storytelling, hilariously brought to life by a superb cast. House of the Dragon ’s Gayle Rankin deserves special mention for the audacity of her performance as Isla, but Grant O’Rourke ( Outlander ), Domhnall Gleeson, John Hannah and Michelle Gomez are also magnificent. With quirky wit and heartwarming pathos, The Incomer is a smart and absurd crowdpleaser about the importance of remaining true to oneself.
▸导演Louis Paxton以苏格兰童年记忆为灵感，巧妙融合荒诞幽默与地方神话，呈现独特的影像风格与地域氛围。▸主演Gayle Rankin（《龙之家族》）奉献大胆精彩的表演，配合Grant O’Rourke、Domhnall Gleeson等实力演员，角色鲜明，化学反应十足。▸荣获圣丹斯电影节NEXT单元创新奖，代表新锐导演的独特视角与创作活力，是不可错过的年度喜剧新声。

#15黑神与白魔 Black God, White Devil必看20 🎬 LB 3.77 长片
1964 · 120 分钟 · 剧情 · Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels · 导演 Glauber Rocha · 巴西
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文1964年戛纳电影节竞赛片，获国际影评人费比西奖
在1940年代巴西旱原，农场工人曼努埃尔因杀害老板被迫与妻子逃亡，两人卷入宗教叛乱与暴力冲突之中。影片以政治寓言和史诗气质，展现边缘人物对抗压迫的悲剧命运。
英文原文简介In the 1940s, during a drought in the Brazilian sertão , or hinterlands, fed-up ranch hand Manuel (Geraldo Del Rey) kills his deceitful boss and goes on the lam with his wife Rosa (Yóna Magalhães). Together, they venture to the holy site of Monte Santo, where, now outlaws, they align themselves with the violent, self-proclaimed holy man Sebastião (Lídio Silva), who is leading a revolt against wealthy landowners. The mercenary Antônio das Mortes (Maurício do Valle), hired by the church and rich locals, is sent to kill Sebastião – and, in turn, the bandit Corisco (Othon Bastos) is out to stop Antônio. Causing a sensation at Cannes when it premiered in Competition in 1964, Black God, White Devil won the FIPRESCI Prize and further established the career of director Glauber Rocha, who was only 25 years old at the time. A sweeping, urgent political allegory suffused with mythmaking and history, Rocha’s second film was described by Luis Buñuel as “the most beautiful thing I have seen in a decade, filled with a savage poetry”. “Rocha’s hectic drama is, in effect, a political western that rages at Brazil’s governmental corruption and plutocratic oppression [with] raw, grand, urgent images.” – The New Yorker
▸巴西新电影运动代表作，由25岁导演格劳贝尔·罗查执导，融合西部片与政治寓言，影像风格大胆、充满诗意与狂野。▸全新4K修复版，重现1964年戛纳竞赛片的震撼视听，极具历史与美学价值。▸演员表演极具张力，叙事层层推进，揭示宗教、阶级与暴力交织的社会现实，是不可错过的南美电影经典。

#16守望高山 To Hold a Mountain必看20 🎬 LB 3.67 长片
2026 · 105 分钟 · 纪录片 · 纪录片单元 · 维州首映 · 导演 Petar Glomazić, Biljana Tutorov · 法国、Montenegro、Serbia、Slovenia
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文圣丹斯电影节纪录片竞赛大奖
在黑山的辛亚耶维纳高原，牧羊人加拉坚守家园，带领女儿和邻居抵抗外来势力，展现女性在困境中团结与坚韧的力量。影片以诗意影像描绘她与土地的深厚情感，探讨爱与坚持的主题。
英文原文简介In Montenegro’s starkly beautiful Sinjajevina alpine range, middle-aged Mileva “Gara” Jovanović herds sheep, milks cows, makes delicious cheese and laughs with her friends, all the while raising adoring teenager Nada to be kind and resilient. Women here have endured generations of patriarchal violence, and Gara works hard to hold her precious space of care and community. As NATO forces plan to exploit these high rolling pastures for military training, Gara stands her ground over a seven-year period, rallying her neighbours to repel repeated incursions into the land and life she holds dear. The winner of the top prize in Sundance 2026’s documentary competition is uplifting enough as a portrayal of staunch matriarchal activism. But directors Biljana Tutorov and Petar Glomazić are striving to capture something loftier: the mountain of love, grief and determination that Gara holds inside. Gently, elegantly, the film falls in rhythm with her steadfast seasonal labour; it’s beguilingly alert to the expressive power of sensory textures in the manner of Return to Dust (MIFF 2022), Honeyland (MIFF 2019) and In the Land of Wolves (MIFF 2018). Building an emotional cartography all its own, To Hold a Mountain traces the contours of the pure bonds between people and place.
▸荣获2026年圣丹斯纪录片竞赛大奖，导演比利亚娜·图托罗夫与佩塔尔·格洛马齐奇以细腻视角，真实记录女性对家园的守护与抗争。▸影片采用自然主义影像风格，巧妙捕捉高原季节变迁与生活质感，观众能沉浸式体验牧羊人的日常与情感。▸主题关注女性在传统社会中的抗争与团结，既有社会现实深度，也有温暖的人文关怀，适合喜欢《隐入尘烟》《蜂蜜之地》的观众。

#17不忠的妻子 The Unfaithful Wife必看20 🎬 LB 3.76 长片
1969 · 98 分钟 · 剧情、惊悚、犯罪、悬疑 · 锋利现实 · 导演 Claude Chabrol · 法国
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文启发了多部获奖电影，影响力深远
巴黎保险经理查尔斯怀疑妻子海伦出轨，逐渐陷入猜忌与偏执，家庭表面的平静被暗流撕裂。这部法国家庭悬疑片，以冷峻风格展现婚姻、信任与道德边界的复杂纠葛。
英文原文简介In this exquisitely calibrated homage to Hitchcock, Parisian insurance executive Charles Desvallées (Michel Bouquet, Night and Fog , MIFF 1966) begins to suspect that his wife Hélène (Stéphane Audran) is having an affair, sending him into an escalating state of paranoia – and towards a plan that will rupture the bourgeois calm of their existence. With its chilly surfaces, precision staging and dark humour, this deliciously deviant drama finds the great Claude Chabrol ( A Story of Women , MIFF 1989; The Butcher , MIFF 1973) on signature form, with the filmmaker’s then-wife Audran ( The Discreet Charm of the Bourgeoisie , MIFF 2000; Les Biches ) delivering a glamourous, emotionally opaque performance that’s ripe with depth and mystery. Critically acclaimed but initially unsuccessful with audiences, The Unfaithful Wife has gone on to become one of Chabrol’s most enduring and influential works, serving as the inspiration for both Adrian Lyne’s Unfaithful and Andrey Zvyagintsev’s recent Cannes Grand Prix winner Minotaur (MIFF 2026).
▸法国新浪潮大师克洛德·夏布洛尔精妙致敬希区柯克，冷静精准的镜头与黑色幽默让悬疑气氛层层递进。▸斯特凡娜·奥德朗的表演极具神秘感，情感深沉却难以捉摸，为角色赋予独特魅力。▸本片影响深远，启发了《不忠》和戈尔吉亚夫塞夫新作《弥诺陶洛斯》，在MIFF重温经典，见证其对现代犯罪电影的启发。

英文原文柏林电影节最佳处女作奖；澳大利亚首映
在无名战区的持续轰炸下，普通人日复一日地为生存而奋斗，不仅要躲避炮火，还要寻找食物、温暖和片刻的安宁。影片以幽默和坚韧展现战争中的人性与希望，充满现实关怀与戏剧张力。
英文原文简介In an unidentified war zone under constant attack, life for locals must go on. Survival doesn’t just mean dodging bombs and sniper fire, but also trying to find food, warmth, a cigarette or the time and privacy to have sex. While former filmmaker Arafat scavenges for food and medicine, a group of young friends break into his boarded-up video store, debating whether to burn the old videotapes to make a fire or just trade memories of their favourite movies. Long-time human rights activist Abdallah Alkhatib was born in Syria’s Yarmouk refugee camp, one of the largest settlements of displaced Palestinians; his 2021 documentary Little Palestine: Diary of a Siege chronicled life in Yarmouk and its fall during the Syrian civil war. Here, drawing from his own experiences of living under fire, he builds a drama that is at once urgent, defiant and unexpectedly funny. The recipient of the Best First Feature award at Berlin this year, Chronicles From the Siege delivers a searing portrait of lives that refuse to be overlooked.
▸导演Abdallah Alkhatib以自身难民经历，将真实的战争生活转化为富有情感的剧情片，延续其纪录片《小巴勒斯坦》的深刻视角。▸影片巧妙融合紧张氛围与幽默元素，通过角色在困境中对旧电影的回忆和争论，展现人们对文化与记忆的坚持。▸荣获柏林电影节最佳处女作奖，国际首映，展现当代阿拉伯电影的独特声音，是MIFF不可错过的中东题材力作。

When Iris ends up in a police station, the only one to bail her out is her estranged father, Aris (Christos Passalis, Dogtooth , MIFF 2009), unexpectedly back in town and in her life. These two misfits soon find that they’re a lot alike, striking a deal to work – or more specifically, hustle – together. With echoes of Peter Bogdanovich’s 1973 classic Paper Moon and recent MIFF favourites Aftersun (MIFF 2022) and Scrapper (MIFF 2023), Myrsini Aristidou’s impressive debut is a poignant riff on the young-father/daughter dynamic as well as a study of two charismatic, complicated characters. #20阿妹 Ah Girl必看20 🎬 LB 3.63 长片

英文原文鹿特丹电影节青年评审奖获奖；澳大利亚首映
故事发生在90年代的新加坡，七岁的阿妹和妹妹阿田在父母离婚的动荡中，寄居祖父母家。面对父母的不确定与承诺，她努力守护妹妹，同时逐渐意识到家庭的异常，体验成长的困惑与无助。
英文原文简介In 90s Singapore, seven-year-old Swee Swee – or “Ah Girl”, as her family calls her – is trying to understand what’s going on in her world. Living with her grandparents as her parents go through a separation, she’s looking out for her younger sister, Ah Tian, and searching for some sense of stability. Instead, her erratic, often-absent mother is prone to making unrealistic promises of an imagined future together, while her father – dating a string of potential new partners – is wondering if the kids should go live with an aunt and uncle in Australia. Torn between competing adults and growing increasingly curious about the world, Ah Girl begins to realise that her family life isn’t normal, and that adults can’t be relied on. As Ah Girl and Ah Tian respectively, newcomers Ong Xuan Jing and Sydney Wong give two of the most incredible child-actor performances you’ll ever see, emotions alive across their tiny faces. Shooting her two leads in close-up and anchoring the entire narrative from a child’s perspective, writer/director Ang Geck Geck Priscilla upends all the familiar tropes of the divorce drama. “Children shouldn’t care about adult problems,” Ah Girl is told; but what she realises is that, as a kid, you’re going to be dragged through the problems of adults no matter how much you try to avoid them. As she retorts: “All adults are liars.”
▸导演洪可可以儿童视角大胆颠覆传统家庭剧，采用近距离拍摄，让观众沉浸于阿妹的内心世界。▸两位新晋童星翁宣静与黄诗迪的表演极具感染力，细腻展现孩子在家庭变故中的情感波动，极为动人。▸本片以新加坡90年代的家庭生活为背景，展现亚洲社会中离婚家庭的独特困境与文化差异，极具地域特色，在MIFF大银幕上尤为值得一看。

英文原文There was no plan – most of these civil resisters didn’t even know one another – but they showed up instinctively nonetheless to bear witness and defend what was morally right.
这是一部2026年英国纪录片长片。导演：Felipe Bustos Sierra。MIFF 信息：纪录片单元、维州首映。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、音乐与表演。
英文原文简介On 13 May 2021, as the first day of Eid-ul-Fitr dawned, a Home Office immigration raid targeted an ordinary residential street in Pollokshields, Glasgow, bundling two local men into a van. But their neighbours wouldn’t let it leave; one protester flung his body under the van and hugged the axle. Word travelled quickly: soon, more than 2000 ordinary people had dropped their morning cuppas, walked out of work meetings and abandoned their daily routines to converge on Kenmure Street. There was no plan – most of these civil resisters didn’t even know one another – but they showed up instinctively nonetheless to bear witness and defend what was morally right. Haunted by his own decision to stay home that morning – “I didn’t see the hope everyone on Kenmure Street did” – Scotland-based Chilean-Belgian director Felipe Bustos Sierra commemorates this day of spontaneous solidarity as a moment-by-moment mosaic of crowdsourced testimonies, archival fragments and self-aware dramatisations by actors Emma Thompson (also an executive producer on the film alongside Hugh Bonneville) and Kate Dickie ( The Witch , MIFF 2015). Winning a Special Jury Award for Civil Resistance at Sundance 2026, this heartening film is a timely reminder that we never need permission to stop legalised injustice.

英文原文简介Seventeen-year-old Robert is trying his best to make ends meet. But as a Congolese refugee in Bangui, in the Central African Republic, the odds are stacked against him. His parents have been jailed for the ‘crime’ of being refugees, and Robert must look after his four younger siblings. He’s also got his final exams to worry about. He copes by writing songs and lyrics, in the process holding on to his dream of making it as a musician. Based on director Rafiki Fariala’s own experiences, Congo Boy is the first Central African film to screen at Cannes, where it received a standing ovation along with charismatic star Bradley Fiomona’s Un Certain Regard Best Actor prize. Leading a stellar cast of non-professionals who add a further layer of authenticity to the story, Fiomona shines through Robert’s poignant interactions with his siblings and his thrilling skills on the mic, showcasing a rousing soundtrack of tunes written by Fariala. Shot on location in Bangui, Congo Boy is a paean to the indomitable human spirit and an undeniable pleasure to boot.

But when Nour announces she’s getting married, Gloria has to look at her own life, from past mistakes to future hopes. Premiering in competition in Berlin, Dao is a joyous follow-up to the director’s Silver Bear–winning social-realist drama Félicité (MIFF 2017), marking a triumphant return to narrative filmmaking after his drawn-from-the-archive documentary portrait of jazz legend Thelonious Monk, Rewind & Play (MIFF 2022).

#26Variations on a Theme🎬 LB 3.60 长片
2026 · 65 分钟 · 剧情 · 非洲与中东 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Devon Delmar, Jason Jacobs · 荷兰、Qatar、South Africa
🏆 获奖、威尼斯、鹿特丹、首映
英文原文Rotterdam’s Tiger Award winner riffs on the many lives of villagers in a lyrical docufiction fable of a forgotten South African mountain community. | Jacobs and Devon Delmar won Rotterdam’s top prize for this follow-up to their Venice-premiering 2024 debut Carissa , confirming them as vital new voices in South African – and global – cinema.
这是一部2026年荷兰、Qatar、South Africa剧情长片。导演：Devon Delmar, Jason Jacobs。MIFF 信息：非洲与中东、澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、记忆与历史、恐怖 / 超自然。
英文原文简介Hettie is a goatherd in South Africa’s remote Kamiesberg mountains. On the eve of her 80th birthday, she’s offered long-overdue reparations for her father’s military service in World War II. The only problem: it’s a scam. As Hettie and her neighbours wait for money that will never come, other villagers search for diamonds, watch rugby, play dominoes or slip into memories. Surrounded by ghosts of past conflicts, in a rural hamlet forgotten by South African society, they are victims of forces large and small – but each has their own rich inner life. Staged as a series of ‘variations’, this hybrid docufiction takes a literary approach, narrating the thoughts of its subjects in a voiceover by co-director Jason Jacobs. His real-life grandmother plays the leading role of Hettie, and that intimacy is at the centre of an achingly empathetic film blessed with cultural specificity, lyrical imagery and an evocative score by Mikhaila Alyssa Smith. Jacobs and Devon Delmar won Rotterdam’s top prize for this follow-up to their Venice-premiering 2024 debut Carissa , confirming them as vital new voices in South African – and global – cinema.

#27Dorian Gray in the Mirror of the Yellow Press🎬 LB 3.67 长片

英文原文简介As Dr. Mabuse, Delphine Seyrig is the high-femme head of an international media empire. Seeking to boost circulation figures, she has a cunning plan: create a character for her readers to fall in love with, and then ruin him before their very eyes. Dorian Gray (Veruschka von Lehndorff) is just the dandy: young, rich and handsome. Pliable and immaculately dressed, he takes courses in art history and literature; attends philanthropic meetings; and journeys out on memorable trips to the opera, the Press Ball and much further to the underworld. As Dr. Mabuse’s creation begins to take hold in society, a battle of wills emerges. In the third and final film in her ‘Berlin Trilogy’ (following 1979’s Ticket of No Return and 1981’s Freak Orlando ), Ulrike Ottinger borrows loosely from both Oscar Wilde’s 1890 Gothic horror The Picture of Dorian Gray and Norbert Jacques’s infamous Dr. Mabuse character – by way of Fritz Lang’s film series – with a great sense of queer irony to create a delicious satire of ego and capitalism. Ottinger’s own striking production design is complemented by Gisela Storch’s gender-crossing costuming and memorable performances from the two leads, along with frequent collaborator Tabea Blumenschein as Dorian Gray’s love interest.
Letterboxd 3.67/5；剧情、实验、奇幻 / Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels。推荐理由：亲密关系、记忆与历史、恐怖 / 超自然。奖项/展映线索：柏林电影节

英文原文简介Amid the sunny splendour of 1980s coastal China, six-year-old tomboy Juan enjoys a sweet life: going to school, swimming, playing soccer, flying kites, getting into fights. But soon things are thrown into flux: her widowed mother remarries, then falls pregnant. Because families are only permitted to have a single child, Juan is quickly adopted out to an older couple in the city. A decade later, against the backdrop of the changing cultural landscape of the 1990s, a now-teenage Juan looks for a place that feels like home. When she finds that her factory work only amplifies her dislocation, she finally takes the plunge and seeks contact with her birth family. Zou Jing ( Lili Alone , MIFF 2021) sets her beautiful, difficult drama against the real-life phenomenon of mass adoption in China that followed the 1979 establishment of the one-child policy. Gorgeously shot by DOP Liang Zhongqiang and featuring stirring performances by newcomer Cao Ruofan and Li Gengxi ( Resurrection , MIFF 2025) – who embody the film’s protagonist as a child and young adult respectively – A Girl Unknown earned acclaim on the Croisette, taking home three Cannes Critics’ Week awards.

#29Elephants in the Fog🎬 LB 3.57 长片

英文原文简介On the fringes of the village of Thori, near a forest inhabited by wild elephants, live a community of Kinnar women united by a vow of chastity. They often perform sacred rites for the villagers, but their third-gender status brings both reverence and ridicule. One of the Kinnar matriarchs, Pirati, has fallen for a local man and dreams of eloping with him to Delhi. But when her adoptive daughter Apsara disappears and the townsfolk refuse to help, she’s faced with an impossible decision. Receiving a seven-minute standing ovation at Cannes, Elephants in the Fog is the first Nepali feature ever selected for the festival’s Un Certain Regard section, where it won the Jury Prize. The feature directorial debut of Shambhala (MIFF 2024) and The Black Hen (MIFF 2016) co-writer Abinash Bikram Shah, it’s at once a riveting crime saga and a robust dramatisation of threats to trans rights across South Asia. Real-world LGBTQIA+ activist Puspa Thing Lama embodies Pirati’s defiant fortitude with an authenticity born of lived experience, while the on-location cinematography by Noé Bach ( Animalia , MIFF 2023) permeates proceedings with an otherworldly, almost menacing air.

When that story fails to connect with an audience, Li retreats to a remote inn in wintertime. There, she strikes up an unlikely friendship with the taciturn owner, Benzo (Shinichi Tsutsumi), who says he rates films based on “how well they depict human sadness”. Following his impressive previous pictures Small, Slow but Steady and All the Long Nights , rising Japanese auteur Sho Miyake received Locarno’s top honour (plus an additional prize from the Junior Jury) for this tender exploration of human aches and interpersonal dynamics. 英文原文简介For Bruno in 1990s Mexico City, life is exuberant. He’s celebrating his 11th birthday with a gender-swap costume party, and he spends many frivolous days – watching porn, acting in the school play, sneaking onto the set of Baz Luhrmann’s Romeo + Juliet – with his best friend and crush Vladimir. But things take a turn when he and his mother receive news that his father has HIV. Thirty years later, Bruno confronts the memories and revelations of this watershed in his childhood. A film that is, in the director’s words, “not faithful to facts, but to emotional memory”, award-winning documentarian Bruno Santamaría Razo’s fiction debut ingeniously blurs boundaries in both excavating and reimagining the past. Initially born from interviews with family members, the resulting work plays with remembrance and representation, interweaving dramatic recreations with talking-head footage, animation and even educational AIDS videos from the era. Newcomer Jade Reyes is a revelation, playing Santamaría Razo’s younger self with a wide-eyed ebullience that is matched by Fernando Hernández García’s warm, at times whimsical 16mm cinematography. What emerges is a visionary account of grief, growth and the affirming power of storytelling.

As the couple move from Ankara to Istanbul with their 13-year-old daughter, relationships begin to fray and ethics become compromised, the hostility of the Turkish regime infecting the family dynamic. Winner of the Berlin International Film Festival’s top prize, İlker Çatak’s follow-up to The Teachers’ Lounge is an all-too-timely depiction of state-administered suppression of artists and intellectuals, reflecting how authoritarian regimes erode the humanity of those under their boot. Shooting in Germany so as to preserve his own artistic freedom – with intertitles announcing from the outset that Berlin is serving as Ankara and Hamburg as Istanbul – Çatak uses his domestic drama as a spur for greater conversations about the rise of censorship and anti-art regimes.

Instead, they drive right into a chaotic firefight involving US marines, which kills Mariam’s husband and two sons. Twelve years later, Mariam – now living in the US with her daughter – receives a request from an American journalist she met in hospital after the shooting: one of the marines wants to meet her. Adapting a 2012 New Yorker article by Pulitzer Prize–winning combat journalist Dexter Filkins, Reed Van Dyk’s ( DeKalb Elementary , MIFF 2017) debut feature astutely avoids centring the grip of PTSD on the US soldier (played by a career-best Boyd Holbrook) over his victims’ years of anguish; instead, this complex, layered narrative explores civilian trauma and veteran guilt as mutually inextricable violences of war. Hiam Abbass ( Gaza Mon Amour , MIFF 2021; Succession ) is breathtakingly restrained as Mariam; Kenneth Branagh, meanwhile, brings gravitas to his performance as a fictionalised Filkins. While its kinetic in medias res action sequences are visceral, Atonement finds heartbreaking power in its compassionate portrayal of shared humanity.

As Marija evicts Vytas in favour of a refugee family and Vytas moves back in with his Russophile parents, the former couple must navigate their new individualities – are they good people? Andrius Blaževičius’s wry film offers a masterclass in visual storytelling: it’s little wonder he walked away from Sundance with the World Cinema Dramatic section’s Directing Award. With precision, he threads the tension between comfort and conflict through every strand of the story’s DNA, continually testing Vytas’s and Marija’s moral convictions. Marius Repšys’s and Žygimantė Elena Jakštaitė’s outstanding performances underscore the ironies of their actions, while the deadpan script, off-kilter score and coolly detached cinematography combine to solidify a sense of growing unease that makes How to Divorce During the War both timely and universally resonant.

英文原文简介“Disorientation is part of the journey. Welcome to Lebanon.” So pronounces Do You Love Me , which jams on Lebanese collective memory in ways both joyous and harrowing. Stitching together still photos, home movies, old celluloid, TV clips, radio broadcasts and podcasts, this free-associative portrait of life in Beirut is filled with acts of humanity and inhumanity. From garbage strikes to bomb strikes, news reports to pop-cultural ephemera, this wild ride through the archives is an act of resistance filled with singing and dancing. Lebanon has no national archive, so filmmaker and interdisciplinary artist Lana Daher set out to make her own. Combing through 20,000 hours of footage drawn from across seven decades, Daher and co-writer/editor Qutaiba Barhamji – whose previous editing work has included Four Daughters , Smoke Sauna Sisterhood (both MIFF 2023) and the Oscar-nominated The Voice of Hind Rajab – forgo talking heads, voiceovers and explanatory intertitles. Instead, their exuberant supercut is shot through with energy, daring and an undeniable sense of humour.

英文原文This César Best Documentary–winning French box-office smash, with a score featuring Warren Ellis, is a stunning visual and aural immersion into the misty Vosges mountains. | Award-winning wildlife photographer and filmmaker Vincent Munier joins his 12-year-old son and father, environmentalist Michel Munier, on a journey through the forest in search of the endangered bird.
这是一部2025年法国纪录片长片。导演：Vincent Munier。MIFF 信息：自然世界、维州首映。核心看点：家庭关系、成长与青春、亲密关系、政治与社会现实、记忆与历史、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Three generations of nature lovers set out to find the western capercaillie amid the densely wooded and visually spectacular Vosges, a French mountain range close to the German border. Award-winning wildlife photographer and filmmaker Vincent Munier joins his 12-year-old son and father, environmentalist Michel Munier, on a journey through the forest in search of the endangered bird. But even though the capercaillie might be rare here, other wildlife are not. Munier’s camera captures bears, deer, owls and more, in all their visual and sonic glory. After winning awards in the National History Museum Wildlife Photographer of the Year competition three years in a row in his youth, Vincent Munier has in recent times also turned his hand to the moving image. His first feature documentary, The Velvet Queen , charted his quest to find the elusive snow leopard; Whispers in the Woods brings him back to where he grew up, and to a far more personal quest. While Munier’s images are extraordinary, what sets this film apart is how they combine with the sound design (which also scored a César) to highlight the unique aural vibrations of these woods – all underscored by Warren Ellis, Dom La Nena and Rosemary Standley’s score, which itself earned a Lumière Award for Best Music. An exquisite love letter to family and to the wonderful world we live in, Whispers in the Woods is best experienced on the big screen.

英文原文简介Whizzing through Tehran on his bicycle, Amir is preoccupied by a decision he’s been avoiding. His plan is to emigrate to Italy to join his girlfriend, Tara, who has already moved there to study; but he remains torn between staying in the city he’s known all his life and leaving it all behind for a new adventure. As he awaits visa approval, Amir visits his uncle, plays poker with his buddies and replays memories from his relationship with Tara. Meanwhile, his life-changing decision looms, and the distance between him and Tara weighs heavier on his heart. Writer/director Amir Azizi won two awards at the Venice International Film Festival – including the top prize in the festival’s Giornate degli Autori section – for this humanistic portrayal of a young man at a crossroads. Spotlighting the beauty in the everyday, Inside Amir poignantly captures a side of Tehran that we rarely see depicted, as well as a feeling that will resonate with anyone who’s ever moved far from home.

英文原文简介In October 2009 in northern Argentina, members of the Diaguita community of Los Chuschagasta attempted to resist eviction from their native land. In the confrontation that followed, 68-year-old resident Javier Chocobar was shot dead and two others were wounded – a crime that was captured on video, but only taken to court after a decade-long process of protest and agitation. Even now, justice for Chocobar’s people remains hard to come by. Winner of Best Film at the 2025 BFI London Film Festival, the first feature-length documentary from acclaimed filmmaker Lucrecia Martel ( The Headless Woman ) serves as an unexpected companion piece to her satirical colonialist parable Zama (MIFF 2018). At once true-crime story, legal drama and big-picture portrait of Argentina, Landmarks offers not only an indictment of systemic shortcomings but also a deeper exploration of her nation’s centuries-long history of colonial settlement, land grabs and silencing of its Indigenous populations.

#43Weighed but Found Wanting🎬 LB 3.88 长片

🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文A pioneering work of the Second Golden Age of Philippine Cinema, set in the province where director Lino Brocka ( Manila in the Claws of Light , MIFF 2013) grew up, Wei...
这是一部1974年菲律宾剧情长片。导演：Lino Brocka。MIFF 信息：经典修复、澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、成长与青春、政治与社会现实。
英文原文简介Junior is the only son of Cesar, a lawyer, a failed politician and the richest man in town. This wealth has afforded Junior an ultra-comfortable life – one he spends with his similarly well-off friends and girlfriend. After a series of upsetting discoveries, however, Junior distances himself from this privileged bubble, eventually finding solace in his friendships with leper Berto and ‘village idiot’ Kuala. But the teenager soon learns that beneath the strictures of small-town respectability lurks all manner of ruthlessness. A pioneering work of the Second Golden Age of Philippine Cinema, set in the province where director Lino Brocka ( Manila in the Claws of Light , MIFF 2013) grew up, Weighed but Found Wanting offers a contemporary twist on the biblical account of hubris, hypocrisy and judgement its title references. Released at the peak of Ferdinand Marcos’s ghastly martial-law regime, it was a critical and commercial success, winning six FAMAS Awards and launching the career of “King of Philippine Drama” Christopher de Leon, who debuted here alongside luminaries Eddie Garcia and Lolita Rodriguez. With echoes of Fellini, Bogdanovich and José Rizal’s magnum opus Noli Me Tángere , Brocka’s masterpiece champions empathy and anti-establishment principles during a period of large-scale repression; now, in one of the film’s first international screenings – this brand-new 4K restoration having recently premiered at Il Cinema Ritrovato – it can be discovered afresh.

英文原文简介Bouchra, a coyote, is a New York–based Moroccan filmmaker in the throes of creating a semi-autobiographical feature. Unable to access the inspiration she seeks, she decides to call her mother, Aïcha, who lives in Casablanca, to address the topic they’ve left untouched for almost a decade: Bouchra’s sexuality. Despite staying in touch, mother and daughter have never discussed Bouchra’s same-sex relationships, nor her ‘out’ life in the US. As the filmmaker starts devising storyboards, we’re pulled into a genre-defying hybrid work that blends memory, fantasy and metafiction. Winning the top queer prize at the Chicago International Film Festival, Bouchra recalls directors Orian Barki and Meriem Bennani’s 2020 miniseries 2 Lizards in its evocation of a hyperreal world where animals act and interact like humans. Blending live action, photogrammetry and 3D scanning, it uses actual snippets of conversation between Bennani and her mother to launch into confabulation, with Bouchra’s film-within-a-film offering a medium for catharsis, conjecture and wish fulfilment. Empathetic and visionary, Bouchra meditates on the act of mediation itself – how cinema, just like discussions held across distance and time, necessarily hinges on our version of the truth.

英文原文Sharing the Best Director Prize at Cannes, this sublime time-hopping triptych recounts three men’s experiences of love, legacy and the unending fight for queer liberation.

In 1932, Carlos attempts to gain membership to an exclusive casino but is rejected due to rumours about his homosexuality. And in 2017, historian Alberto inherits a gift from his estranged grandfather that exacerbates tensions with his mother. Across the decades, these men’s stories interweave and bleed into one another, revealing threads that connect them in profound, unexpected ways. Associate-produced by Pedro Almodóvar ( Bitter Christmas , MIFF 2026) and featuring supporting turns by Penélope Cruz, Glenn Close and Julio Torres ( Problemista , MIFF 2024), the arrestingly poetic second feature from directorial duo Javier Ambrossi and Javier Calvo depicts how each generation faces its own forms of prejudice. Yet as much as it lays bare the present’s debts to the past, the film also challenges our notions of linear time, its dazzling collisions of image and sound coming together as palimpsests of personal and societal memory. Inspired by Federico García Lorca’s unfinished stageplay of the same name, La Bola Negra is a sweeping meditation on the battles we wage for ideology and belonging.

Once together, the pair feel the heat not just of the production’s Canary Islands setting but also of the tensions that simmer between them. The plot line of the latest feature from Goya Award–winning director Rodrigo Sorogoyen ( The Beasts ; Mother , MIFF 2018) may evoke Sentimental Value , but it trades in Joachim Trier’s optimistic take on filial reconciliation for a far more scorching account of familial messiness. Alongside questions of nepotism, ulterior motives and creative exploitation, The Beloved makes ingenious use of myriad film stocks – from sombre black-and-white to shaky, vibrant handheld; from 16mm to 35mm to digital – to convey differing mental states, circumstances and slants on the past. Matching Javier Bardem’s career-best performance as a morally murky agent of patriarchal power, Victoria Luengo ( Bitter Christmas , MIFF 2026) portrays Emilia’s guardedness and resentment with sophisticated grace.

#50Waking Hours🎬 LB 3.26 长片
2025 · 78 分钟 · 纪录片、实验 · 纪录新视野 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Filippo Foscarini, Federico Cammarata · 意大利
🏆 获奖、威尼斯
英文原文A nocturnal descent into the lives of Afghan people smugglers living in the forests of the Balkan route, this Venice award winner is a profound, immersive experience.
这是一部2025年意大利纪录片、实验长片。导演：Filippo Foscarini, Federico Cammarata。MIFF 信息：纪录新视野、澳洲首映。核心看点：政治与社会现实、恐怖 / 超自然。
英文原文简介In the darkness of a forest in northern Serbia, right by the border of Hungary, Afghan passeurs gather around a flickering fire: smoking, baking bread and discussing the best corridors for smuggling people across the border. As gunshots resound in the distance and loudspeakers blast periodic warnings from the Hungarian side, these tiny figures linger in the shadow of the European Union. Taking place almost entirely in darkness – illuminated only by firelight, torches, phones and distant passing headlights – this immersive, experiential work of direct cinema takes us into the world of the men who facilitate safe passage along the Balkan route. Seeing the work of their often-reviled subjects as “a response to and a consequence of Europe’s exclusionary policies”, Italian directors Federico Cammarata and Filippo Foscarini covertly film from a distance, danger forever in the air. With its nocturnal imagery and heightened quality of sound, Waking Hours plays almost like a slow-burning horror movie: plunging viewers into an unsettling night; cultivating a sense of mounting fear; asking us to imagine what’s lurking outside the frame.
Letterboxd 3.26/5；纪录片、实验 / 纪录新视野 / 澳洲首映。推荐理由：政治与社会现实、恐怖 / 超自然。奖项/展映线索：获奖、威尼斯

#51Everybody Digs Bill Evans🎬 LB 3.23 长片

🏆 银熊奖、导演奖、获奖、柏林电影节
英文原文In a virtuosic riff on a biopic standard, this Silver Bear–winning ensemble piece plays on the emotions of the people surrounding an anguished US jazz piano icon. | British documentarian Grant Gee ( Joy Division ) won the Berlinale’s Silver Bear for Best Director with this fiction debut, whose jaunty title – borrowed from an early Evans album – belies its deeper themes.
这是一部2026年英国、爱尔兰剧情、音乐长片。导演：Grant Gee。MIFF 信息：音乐电影、澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、音乐与表演。
英文原文简介June 1961: the Bill Evans Trio have just live-recorded a New York residency that will spawn two celebrated jazz albums. Ten days later, a car crash kills bassist Scott LaFaro at just 25. Devastated, Evans can’t even touch a piano. He stays with his brother Harry, sister-in-law Pat and adoring niece Debby; shoots heroin with his girlfriend Ellaine; and journeys silently, scarily inward. Bill’s depressive black hole starts to claim Harry – a music conservatory teacher who envies his kid brother’s genius – and even shadows their working-class parents’ sunny Florida retirement. British documentarian Grant Gee ( Joy Division ) won the Berlinale’s Silver Bear for Best Director with this fiction debut, whose jaunty title – borrowed from an early Evans album – belies its deeper themes. In elegant black-and-white, the film seeks its lost subject in negative space, emulating his subtle style; impressionistic montages shimmer like harmonic chords and slide across chronologies like modal progressions. Playing both Evans and his compositions, frequent Joachim Trier collaborator Anders Danielsen Lie ( The Worst Person in the World , MIFF 2021) is magnetically quiet, while Bill Pullman and Laurie Metcalf are in career-best form as Bill’s parents.

Desperate to fix their relationship, they visit twin TikTok love gurus Tilly and Tilly, whose mysterious counsel reminds the couple how and why they fell for each other. It also unlocks something else, with earth-shattering repercussions … literally. Cheekily interpreting the real-world implications of Rhonda Byrne’s pseudoscientific self-help hit The Secret , first-time feature director Graham Parkes creates a wonderfully witty, lived-in love story with a supernatural through-line that’s as hilarious as it is horrifying. Utilising ingenious split-screen techniques and capturing the stunning vistas of the Pacific Northwest, Parkes and cinematographer Christopher Ripley ensure the film looks incredible, while Lewis Pullman ( The Testament of Ann Lee ) and Maya Hawke ( Once Upon a Time in Hollywood , MIFF 2019; Stranger Things ) are phenomenal as Charlie and Julia, exuding chemistry while anchoring every emotional heartbeat and delivering every punchline to perfection. With a supporting cast that includes Randall Park, Kate Berlant and Jon Hamm as himself in a brilliantly executed recurring bit, Wishful Thinking is a boldly original, funny and insightful study of the wonderful delusion at the heart of all love: that its exhilarating highs and heartbreaking lows can change the world.
Letterboxd 3.72/5；剧情、喜剧、爱情、奇幻 / 主打佳片 / 澳洲首映。推荐理由：家庭关系、亲密关系、政治与社会现实、恐怖 / 超自然。奖项/展映线索：获奖

英文原文简介When P.K. Mahanandia was a baby, an astrologer predicted he’d marry a woman from outside India. But how? Mahanandia was Dalit – the lowest, poorest caste. Then, in 1975, Swedish backpacker Lotta von Schedvin paid the gentle, curious 23-year-old to sketch her portrait on a Delhi street, and soon fell for him. After two magical months together, von Schedvin returned home – but for Mahanandia, it wasn’t over. With his last $80, he bought a secondhand Raleigh bicycle and pedalled off on the hippie trail on what would become a 6000-mile quest. The Proclaimers would’ve given up long before … but, for this Tour de Romance, artistic talent and the kindness of many strangers were more than enough fuel to keep the wheels turning. Documentarian Orlando von Einsiedel ( Evelyn , MIFF 2019) is always looking for the best aspects of humanity, whether it be among gorilla-protecting Congolese rangers in Virunga (MIFF 2014) or Syria’s volunteer civil defenders in his 2016 Oscar-winning short The White Helmets . Here, he weaves the couple’s photos, letters and heartfelt interviews through beguilingly vintage-textured re-enactments of their courtship and Mahanandia’s odyssey, adding unscripted interactions with some of the colourful characters the director meets while filming along his subject’s original route. Be prepared to fall head over handlebars for these dreamers.

Tamara Kotevska’s previous portrait of farming in rural North Macedonia, Honeyland (co-directed with Ljubomir Stefanov, MIFF 2019), received Oscar nominations for both Best Documentary and Best International Feature Film. The Tale of Silyan , which premiered at Venice and won Best Feature Documentary at the International Documentary Association Awards, is equally impressive: a unique modern-day folktale filled with heart, humour and spectacular cinematography.

In the painful aftermath of Adrian’s death, McElwee turned to his archive, in search of what he and his camera might have missed. Eventually, Carla confesses something about the specific circumstances of the accident, leaving Thomas shattered. This revelation leads both Thomas and Carla to share intimate conversations with friends and loved ones about the fragility of romantic relationships and the impossibility of ever truly knowing someone – even those with whom we share a life. Two-time Silver Bear–winning filmmaker Angela Schanelec ( I Was at Home, But , MIFF 2019) returns with another characteristically austere, defiantly minimalist work that’s fascinated with the psychology of modern relationships but resists easy interpretation – the kind of filmmaking that will appeal to fans of directors like Hong Sang-soo, Aki Kaurismäki and Éric Rohmer. Shot on 35mm by regular Radu Jude collaborator Marius Panduru ( Diary of a Chambermaid , MIFF 2026), the Berlinale Competition–selected film is constructed from formally controlled tableau-like sequences, each deeply attuned to the beauty of everyday life, whether it be a brass band playing in a park as it begins to rain or a group of friends performing a dance to a Leonard Cohen song.

英文原文简介The date 22 June 1986 is etched into the collective mythologies of two nations and football fans around the globe. The FIFA World Cup quarter-final match played that day between arch rivals England and Argentina is infamous for the contentious “hand of god” goal from Diego Maradona, followed minutes later by his “goal of the century”. But it’s not just the golden boy’s feats that set the match apart; geopolitical tensions that had been brewing for years had only recently boiled over in the deadly Falklands War, and fans on both sides viewed this game through a prism of revenge. Forty years later, directors Juan Cabral and Santiago Franco reinvestigate this historic moment in exhilarating detail, echoing the structure of the game and thoughtfully reflecting on the historical, cultural and sociopolitical context that gave it so much charge. Cathartic interviews with former on-field opponents including Gary Lineker, Peter Shilton, Ricardo Giusti, Jorge Burruchaga and Julio Olarticoechea, shot in exquisite monochrome, are juxtaposed against lively archival footage of the match in vivid colour, all framed in the same boxy 4:3 ratio through which that day’s audiences viewed the action on their TV sets. Whether you’ve seen the match 100 times or never, The Match makes for a suspenseful, riveting and ultimately moving watch.

Much like Pain and Glory (MIFF 2019), Pedro Almodóvar’s latest Competition headliner at Cannes – where it shared the Soundtrack Award – is an ingenious piece of self-portraiture that interrogates creativity and its impediments. The enthralling film-within-a-film explodes onto the screen with the director’s signature vivid colours and sumptuous settings, which are enhanced by the piquant soundtrack by long-time collaborator Alberto Iglesias. 英文原文Legendary fashion photographer and photojournalist William Klein exploded into narrative filmmaking with this Prix Jean Vigo–winning mockumentary, now a cult record of groovy 1960s mod fashion.

英文原文简介Trailed by a gormless French film crew through Paris, American model Polly (played by director William Klein’s favourite model, Dorothy McGowan) is a mod Alice weaving her way through a stylishly shambolic Wonderland. Right from the famous opening sequence – a runway show in a Gaudi-esque colosseum in which fashionistas coo over models encased in sheet metal – Klein is fascinated with fashion’s theatre of the absurd. His satirical eye finds something solemn, even religious, in the banal pronouncements of fashion editors and the nonsensical questions of TV interviewers, while Polly seems bemused to find herself an object of worship for trend-hungry teens and lecherous men. Two years before he would make the unnerving American satire Mr. Freedom , Klein skewers the rarefied world of Parisian haute couture and its hangers-on from his privileged position as one of the most subversive photographers to appear in American Vogue . With his sights on the commercialisation of the ‘60s “youthquake”, he mashes up the French New Wave with Beatles caper A Hard Day’s Night , using playful animation that anticipates Monty Python’s Flying Circus .

英文原文简介If a winner of major contemporary poetry awards were ever simultaneously a pop-cultural icon, Mary Oliver is it. Openly queer but fiercely private, Oliver – who died in 2019, aged 83 – was an American mystic, enamoured by the transcendental natural beauty she encountered on her daily walks through Provincetown’s woods and wilds. Influenced by Whitman, Thoreau, Keats and Emerson, and often compared with Dickinson and Rumi, Oliver’s celebrated nature poems have inspired ordinary folk for generations. Now, in this documentary on the poet’s life, director Sasha Waters respectfully shows us the woman behind the words adored by millions, exploring Oliver’s lonely and sometimes traumatic childhood as well as her salvation: in love, in nature and in writing. Friends and admirers including Stephen Colbert, Lucy Dacus, John Waters, Steve Buscemi and Helena Bonham Carter share memories and read favourite poems, while previously unseen photos, prose, essays and correspondence offer insights into Oliver’s inner world. Interspersed with stunning visuals of the landscapes that so inspired her, the film offers a tender, authentic and enlivening study of her life, loves and letters.

英文原文简介Idle during the 2023 Writers Guild of America strike, documentarian John Wilson attends a workshop on how to make Hallmark Christmas rom-com movies. Inspired by his apartment building’s crumbling foundations, he tests this aspirational, escapist formula on the world’s love affair with concrete. Unsurprisingly, Wilson struggles to pitch his idea to prospective investors – and, fretting that he might be falling through the industry’s cracks, he takes a pilgrimage from the celebrity handprints outside LA’s Chinese Theatre to the dome atop Rome’s ancient Pantheon and more, finding surprising insights along the way. Fans of HBO comedy series How To With John Wilson will rejoice that the director’s Sundance-premiering debut feature continues along his curious perambulation. But whether you want eccentric tales embedded in urban history or are hard-set on formalist documentaries like Architecton (MIFF 2024), Wilson delivers it all in slabs. As entertainment grows gimmickier and ever more disposable, The History of Concrete offers a rich, hearteningly humane meditation on life and death, on the things we either leave in ruins or care enough to fix.

🏆 获奖
英文原文Karlovy Vary’s Crystal Globe winner is an enchanting portrait of solitude and free-spirited abandon following eccentric twin brothers living in the Czech wilderness. | Informed by the eponymous book by journalist Aleš Palán and showered with three Czech Lion Awards as well as the top prize at the Karlovy Vary International Film Festival, Better Go Mad in the Wild is a dreamy and poetic...
这是一部2025年Slovakia、Czechia纪录片长片。导演：Miro Remo。MIFF 信息：纪录片单元、澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介In a farmstead deep in the Šumavan Mountains, situated near Czechia’s western borders with Austria and Germany, live identical twins František and Ondřej Klišík. Now in their sixties, the brothers exist in bucolic bliss: drinking, bickering, swimming in glacial lakes and wandering – sometimes in the nude – through nearby forests. On other occasions, they commune with the animals in their midst: their chickens and cows; their dog Joint; and their majestic bull Nandy, whose voiceover recounts the brothers’ storied pasts and current concerns. Informed by the eponymous book by journalist Aleš Palán and showered with three Czech Lion Awards as well as the top prize at the Karlovy Vary International Film Festival, Better Go Mad in the Wild is a dreamy and poetic glimpse into a life of wilful seclusion. Produced over a five-year period, during which director Miro Remo and his crew spent 60 days with the twins, it leverages its hybrid form – not quite essay film or observational documentary – to transport viewers to a world both elemental and unmoored from modern society. It’s a stunning work propelled by emotion and tone, joining František and Ondřej as they muse on mortality, their misadventures and the dreams keeping their maverick ways alive.
Letterboxd 3.60/5；纪录片 / 纪录片单元 / 澳洲首映。推荐理由：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、纪录片视角。奖项/展映线索：获奖

#66Palimpsest: The Story of a Name🎬 LB 3.60 长片
2025 · 109 分钟 · 纪录片 · 纪录片单元 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Mary Stephen · 法国、中国台湾、中国香港
🏆 获奖
英文原文Stephen’s latest film, which received two Golden Horse Awards, proves a richly personal new entry in an oeuvre dedicated to the exploration of identity across borders.
这是一部2025年法国、中国台湾、中国香港纪录片长片。导演：Mary Stephen。MIFF 信息：纪录片单元、澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、记忆与历史。
英文原文简介“All my life I’ve been asked about my family name,” reflects Mary Stephen ( Justocoeur , MIFF 1981). She was born in British Hong Kong to Hilda and Henry Stephen, respectively known in earlier life as Chan Tik-Fong and Hilda Yik. Like their filmmaker daughter, both parents had a creative streak: she wrote poetry, while he was an avid amateur filmmaker and journal keeper, documenting their family life extensively. Poring over her father’s records, Stephen, as the film’s narrator, uncovers all manner of likely tall tales – including a claim of an Indigenous Australian grandfather – and meditates upon the mechanisms and functions of such mythologisation. Together with her parents, Stephen emigrated to Montreal at age 15 before moving to Paris, where she would establish herself as the editor of some of Éric Rohmer’s most cherished films, including A Tale of Winter and A Summer’s Tale . Her own directorial work, largely unseen for decades, has recently enjoyed a much-deserved revival thanks to the restoration of her dreamy 1978 debut, Shades of Silk (MIFF 2026). Stephen’s latest film, which received two Golden Horse Awards, proves a richly personal new entry in an oeuvre dedicated to the exploration of identity across borders.

#67美狄亚 (古希腊悲剧) Medea🎬 LB 3.69 长片
1969 · 111 分钟 · 剧情、实验 · Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels · 导演 Pier Paolo Pasolini · 法国、德国、意大利
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文High priestess Medea, the granddaughter of the Greek sun god Helios, has her life fatefully ruptured when Jason and the Argonauts arrive on her homeland of Colchis to steal the Golden Fleece.
这是一部1969年法国、德国、意大利剧情、实验长片。导演：Pier Paolo Pasolini。MIFF 信息：Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels。核心看点：家庭关系、亲密关系、政治与社会现实、记忆与历史。
英文原文简介High priestess Medea, the granddaughter of the Greek sun god Helios, has her life fatefully ruptured when Jason and the Argonauts arrive on her homeland of Colchis to steal the Golden Fleece. Together, she and Jason abscond to Corinth, where she attempts to relinquish her spiritual past and subsume herself in the role of dutiful wife and mother to their two sons. When Jason abandons her to follow a more politically beneficial marriage, Medea is driven to a shocking act of vengeance. In this visually stunning adaptation of Euripides’s canonical work, Pier Paolo Pasolini infuses the mythical tragedy with biting colonial allegory. A close friend of the visionary director, the legendary Maria Callas – dressed in brilliant costumes by Piero Tosi, who had previously worked with her on opera productions – delivers a powerhouse performance of diva proportions in the title role. The dramatic landscapes of Türkiye’s Central Anatolian region are further emphasised by the production design of Dante Ferretti, who worked on eight of Pasolini’s films before his Oscar-winning Hollywood career.
Letterboxd 3.69/5；剧情、实验 / Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels。推荐理由：家庭关系、亲密关系、政治与社会现实、记忆与历史。奖项/展映线索：有电影节展映/奖项线索

#68Middle of the Night🎬 LB 3.69 长片
1959 · 118 分钟 · 剧情 · Kim Novak: Hollywood Heretic · 导演 Delbert Mann · 美国
🏆 获奖
英文原文Jerry Kingsley (played by two-time Academy Award winner Fredric March), a recently bereaved Manhattan textiles manufacturer, is encouraged by all around him to take a new wife.
这是一部1959年美国剧情长片。导演：Delbert Mann。MIFF 信息：Kim Novak: Hollywood Heretic。核心看点：家庭关系、亲密关系、政治与社会现实、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Jerry Kingsley (played by two-time Academy Award winner Fredric March), a recently bereaved Manhattan textiles manufacturer, is encouraged by all around him to take a new wife. What his family and buddies don’t expect is that the 56-year-old man’s affections will land on Betty Preisser (Kim Novak), the 24-year-old divorced receptionist who works at his factory. Even as the two tentatively pursue this May–December romance, they soon grasp the complexities of sharing the relationship with their families and friends. Marilyn Monroe had originally campaigned to play Betty after seeing the Broadway production on which the film was based, but the role instead went to Novak, keen to prove her acting chops and break free of the bombshell image Columbia Pictures had created for her. Adapted for the screen by playwright Paddy Chayefsky ( Marty ) and shot in striking black-and-white, the emotional performances from March and Novak – who cites it as her favourite turn – devastate. Premiering in Competition at the 1959 Cannes Film Festival, where Novak’s appearance on the Croisette was among the event’s most documented, Middle of the Night is a deeply human and compassionate portrait of people reaching for connection in a world determined to judge them for it.

#69The Dreamed Adventure🎬 LB 3.09 长片
2026 · 167 分钟 · 剧情、惊悚 · 主打佳片 · 维州首映 · 导演 Valeska Grisebach · 法国、德国、奥地利、Bulgaria
🏆 评审团奖、获奖、戛纳
英文原文Almost a decade after Western , Valeska Grisebach returns with this similarly rough-hewn, simmering tale of border town intrigue that claimed the Cannes Jury Prize. | Awarded the Jury Prize at Cannes, The Dreamed Adventure is as sinewy, assured and enigmatic as Said, played by the striking non-professional actor Syule...
这是一部2026年法国、德国、奥地利、Bulgaria剧情、惊悚长片。导演：Valeska Grisebach。MIFF 信息：主打佳片、维州首映。核心看点：政治与社会现实、悬疑 / 犯罪张力。
英文原文简介The ostensibly sleepy town of Svilengrad sits on the Bulgarian border, with Türkiye to the east and Greece to the south. The laconic Said has hardly been there a day when his car is stolen. Not that it appears to bother him unduly – this rangy former local is an unruffled sort, returned, it seems, to broker a shady fuel deal. A chance encounter reunites him with Veska, an old acquaintance who’s in town helming an archaeological dig. Her attraction to Said sees her venture dangerously deep into Svilengrad’s boozy, machismo-laden underworld. Awarded the Jury Prize at Cannes, The Dreamed Adventure is as sinewy, assured and enigmatic as Said, played by the striking non-professional actor Syuleyman Letifov ( Western , MIFF 2017), while the brilliant Yana Radeva gradually takes centre stage in the film as Veska. In this sprawling, arid noir, the latent threat of violence charges even minor gestures, whether it be the pouring of another drink, the lighting of another cigarette or the simple act of leaning back in a plastic lawn chair. It’s a subtly masterful work, well worth the long wait.
