#70Whispers in May🎬 LB 3.58 长片
2026 · 95 分钟 · 纪录片、剧情 · 学校单元 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Dongnan Chen · 中国香港、荷兰、瑞典、韩国
🏆 获奖
英文原文The winner of the main prize at CPH:DOX, this impressionistic hybrid documentary follows a teenage girl on a quest to find a ceremonial skirt.
这是一部2026年中国香港、荷兰、瑞典、韩国纪录片、剧情长片。导演：Dongnan Chen。MIFF 信息：学校单元、澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、成长与青春、亲密关系、政治与社会现实、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Fourteen-year-old Qihuo has just had her first period. In her Nuosu community in south-west China’s remote, mountainous Liangshan district, this milestone signals that she is ready to work in the factories – and, even, for arranged marriage. Tradition also calls for menarche to be commemorated with a “skirt-changing” ceremony, in which garments signifying childhood are replaced. With her parents both working miles away from their village, Qihuo shares her secret with her two best friends; and, together, the girls set out across the mountains to find her a new skirt. Described by director Dongnan Chen as a “reluctant coming-of-age film”, Whispers in May is a poignant documentary – created collaboratively with its protagonists – that could easily be mistaken for a fictional work. As the girls traverse the rugged landscape, trawl through fabrics at local markets and get their palms read by fortune tellers, we witness this precious and fleeting moment of their lives between childhood and adulthood, between freedom and responsibility. In awarding this dreamlike time capsule, the CPH:DOX jury praised it as “a modern-day fairytale that heeds monsters and factories, alike”.

#71The Man With the Golden Arm🎬 LB 3.67 长片
1955 · 119 分钟 · 剧情 · Kim Novak: Hollywood Heretic · 导演 Otto Preminger · 美国
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文A landmark of postwar American cinema, 1955 classic The Man With the Golden Arm takes an unflinching look at the psychological impacts of addiction with a startling candour that shattered Hollywood taboos at the time.
这是一部1955年美国剧情长片。导演：Otto Preminger。MIFF 信息：Kim Novak: Hollywood Heretic。核心看点：家庭关系、亲密关系、政治与社会现实、音乐与表演。
英文原文简介A landmark of postwar American cinema, 1955 classic The Man With the Golden Arm takes an unflinching look at the psychological impacts of addiction with a startling candour that shattered Hollywood taboos at the time. After a stint getting clean in prison, aspiring jazz drummer Frankie Machine (Frank Sinatra, From Here to Eternity ) returns to Chicago’s chaotic backstreets, where he struggles to rebuild his life within the constraints of a manipulative marriage and the suffocating pull of old habits, battling the allure of heroin. Columbia Pictures agreed to loan Kim Novak to United Artists after Otto Preminger specifically requested to cast her in the role of Molly Novotny, Frankie’s sympathetic girlfriend; it proved to be a breakthrough role for her. Sinatra likewise delivers a career-defining performance, while Eleanor Parker ( The Sound of Music ) is deliciously wicked as Frankie’s seemingly hapless wife. Adapted from Nelson Algren’s uncompromising novel and featuring a groundbreaking jazz score by Elmer Bernstein, Preminger’s Oscar-nominated film – released without the Production Code seal of approval – remains a devastating character study laden with moral ambiguity.

#72Super Nature🎬 LB 3.53 长片
2025 · 82 分钟 · 纪录片 · 自然世界 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Ed Sayers · 英国
🏆 获奖
英文原文Sharing his vision was Oscar-winning filmmaker Asif Kapadia ( Amy ; Senna , MIFF 2011), who was so inspired by Sayers’s pitch that he came on board as executive producer.
这是一部2025年英国纪录片长片。导演：Ed Sayers。MIFF 信息：自然世界、澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、成长与青春、亲密关系、政治与社会现实、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Forget ultra-high-definition cameras, macro imagery and drone shots. Compiled exclusively from new super-8 footage shot on vintage cameras in 25 countries across five continents, Super Nature offers an unexpectedly rich, gloriously lo-fi view of the world, captured by 40 local volunteer cinematographers – including Australians Oliver Birt, Caitlin Henderson and Fraser Johnston – who filmed whatever caught their eye, providing commentary as they saw fit. From Welsh puffins and Patagonian whales to Italian mountain ranges and Indigenous Brazilian communities, Super Nature is a global love letter to nature, written in all the textures of the human heart. It’s a testament to Ed Sayers’s lifelong passion for super-8 that he could craft such a coherent narrative from these disparate vignettes, shot by super-8 aficionados as well as biologists, conservationists and environmental activists. Sharing his vision was Oscar-winning filmmaker Asif Kapadia ( Amy ; Senna , MIFF 2011), who was so inspired by Sayers’s pitch that he came on board as executive producer. Despite our planet’s obvious challenges, Super Nature is full of compassion and hope for its future, reconnecting us to our world through the nostalgic intimacy and vibrant immediacy of its format.
Letterboxd 3.53/5；纪录片 / 自然世界 / 澳洲首映。推荐理由：家庭关系、成长与青春、亲密关系、政治与社会现实、纪录片视角。奖项/展映线索：获奖

英文原文简介Best friends Minna and Flic are on a mission to graduate from their English boarding school and get into Oxbridge. Keenly aware that they’ll need to go the extra mile to increase their chances of selection, the girls set themselves an extracurricular assignment to become more “worldly”. Their goal: to fall in love with the first person they see … and that just happens to be their totally oblivious geography teacher, Miss Delavigne (Alice Englert, Bad Behaviour , MIFF 2023). With a punchy script penned by Miriam Battye and adapted from a short story by Rose Tremain, Extra Geography is a funny, bittersweet ode to teenage-girl friendship in the lineage of films like Ghost World , Clueless and Booksmart . BAFTA-winning TV director Molly Manners’s debut feature is led by remarkable performances from newcomers Galaxie Clear and Marni Duggan as Minna and Flic, whose convincingly cosy friendship is tested by the rocky terrain of adolescence, full of confusing hormones, co-dependency and competitiveness.

#74Decorado🎬 LB 3.51 长片
2025 · 95 分钟 · 动画 · 动画单元 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Alberto Vazquez · 西班牙
🏆 获奖
英文原文Unicorn Wars director Alberto Vázquez returns with another visionary, Goya Award–winning animated polemic. | ...s lauded short of the same name (MIFF 2016), Decorado swaps out the overt violence of his award-winning feature debut Unicorn Wars (MIFF 2022) for a seething sense of menace, capturing the paranoia that can come from being a...
这是一部2025年西班牙动画长片。导演：Alberto Vazquez。MIFF 信息：动画单元、澳洲首映。核心看点：成长与青春、亲密关系、政治与社会现实、恐怖 / 超自然。
英文原文简介Middle-aged mouse Arnold is unemployed, and his cartoonist wife María’s salary sometimes falls short when the bills arrive. As if these pressures weren’t bad enough, he’s also convinced that the town they live in is a theatre set (or decorado in Spanish). With the all-powerful Almighty Limitless Megacorporative Agency tightening its grip on the townsfolk, Arnold risks losing both his home and his marriage – so he enlists the ghost of his recently deceased best friend Ramiro and the outcast Mr. Mushroom, and sets out to reclaim what’s left of his life. Expanding on Alberto Vázquez’s lauded short of the same name (MIFF 2016), Decorado swaps out the overt violence of his award-winning feature debut Unicorn Wars (MIFF 2022) for a seething sense of menace, capturing the paranoia that can come from being a mere hamster (or mouse) on a wheel. Evoking The Truman Show , Nineteen Eighty-Four and classic Disney, the film is visually bold and narratively breathtaking, tapping into the existential, industrial and psychological crises of a present riddled with inequality and fake news. If all the world’s a stage, this dystopian work dares to ask, are we its actors obliged to keep the show going on?

🏆 圣丹斯、首映
英文原文Adapting Ursula Wills-Jones’s 2008 short story, this Sundance-premiering twist on a period love story – directed by Australian-born Eleanor Wilson and filmmaking (as well as real-life) partne...
这是一部2026年美国剧情、喜剧、Historical、奇幻长片。导演：Alex Huston Fischer, Eleanor Wilson。MIFF 信息：新锐视野、澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、亲密关系、音乐与表演。
英文原文简介In a seaside village lost to time, a fisherwoman delivers the food relied on by the townsfolk, who barely tolerate her cantankerous presence. Unexpectedly named the next to wed and sick of the disdain, she commissions the local basketmaker to weave her the perfect husband, and he goes above and beyond. When you’re married to the hottest and handiest man around, however, jealousies inevitably flare up. Adapting Ursula Wills-Jones’s 2008 short story, this Sundance-premiering twist on a period love story – directed by Australian-born Eleanor Wilson and filmmaking (as well as real-life) partner Alex Huston Fischer, and including MIFF Accelerator alum David Michôd among its producers – is at once ingenious and charmingly irreverent. But it’s no straw-man depiction of middle-aged sexual wish fulfilment: the film uses its whimsical premise to critique small-mindedness, superstition and overzealous conservatism. Olivia Colman goes all-in for a role that recalls her fiery turn in The Favourite , while Alexander Skarsgård ( Lee , MIFF 2024) is magnetic as a creature with more humanity than his human counterparts – testament to the practical effects by Joe Dunckley ( Avatar ) and WETA Workshop. Capped off with transportive cinematography by Oscar winner Lol Crawley ( The Brutalist ) and counting Peter Dinklage ( The Toxic Avenger , MIFF 2025), Richard E. Grant and Melbourne’s own Elizabeth Debicki ( The Tale , MIFF 2018) among its cast, Wicker is a fantasy romance that asks whether we truly know our heart’s desire.

英文原文...like Andrea Arnold’s Cow (MIFF 2021) and Jerzy Skolimowski’s EO (MIFF 2022) – or even the Oscar-winning animation Flow (MIFF 2024) – will adore this feathery fancy from György Pálfi ( Taxidermia , MIFF 2006)....
这是一部2025年德国、希腊、匈牙利剧情长片。导演：György Pálfi。MIFF 信息：欧洲与英国、维州首映。核心看点：导演表达与人物处境。
英文原文简介A poultry transport driver steals a factory-farmed hen, planning to put her in a tasty soup. When he stops his truck at a servo, she escapes, evading a hungry fox and braving a busy highway before getting cooped up in a run-down seaside restaurant. All she wants is to find a safe nest to brood her own chicks – but as she repeatedly strives to find out what becomes of her eggs, she encounters a world in which hens aren’t the only creatures to be exploited. Fans of animal-centred dramas like Andrea Arnold’s Cow (MIFF 2021) and Jerzy Skolimowski’s EO (MIFF 2022) – or even the Oscar-winning animation Flow (MIFF 2024) – will adore this feathery fancy from György Pálfi ( Taxidermia , MIFF 2006). Filmed vividly at chook’s-eye level, its allegory is compelling but never didactic, witty without being gimmicky. There are no animatronics or CGI – just thrilling action and set pieces that need to be seen to be believed, along with the genuine emotion that the inimitable Hungarian auteur draws from an all-star flock of trained birds.

#77Nuisance Bear🎬 LB 3.48 长片
2025 · 86 分钟 · 纪录片 · 自然世界 · 维州首映 · 导演 Gabriela Osio Vanden, Jack Weisman · 美国、英国、加拿大
🏆 有电影节展映/奖项线索
英文原文As animals and humans collide in the world’s “Polar Bear Capital”, this acclaimed doc pairs gorgeous photography with broader climate change questions. | Welcome to the snowy Canadian outpost of Churchill, Manitoba, the self-proclaimed “Polar Bear Capital of the World”.
这是一部2025年美国、英国、加拿大纪录片长片。导演：Gabriela Osio Vanden, Jack Weisman。MIFF 信息：自然世界、维州首映。核心看点：政治与社会现实、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Welcome to the snowy Canadian outpost of Churchill, Manitoba, the self-proclaimed “Polar Bear Capital of the World”. Driven towards urban developments by changing climate and the increasing encroachment of ‘civilisation’ into wilderness, the iconic animals arrive as both dangerous predators and photo-op fodder for tourists. As the bears forage for food and scrap for survival, indifferent to the circus that surrounds them, locals debate whether to welcome them, drive them away peacefully or follow a more traditional mode of coexistence informed by Indigenous practices. Adapted from Gabriela Osio Vanden and Jack Weisman’s award-winning 2021 short of the same name, this stirring and beautifully observational film won the U.S. Documentary Grand Jury Prize at Sundance. Blessed with stunning photography of bear and landscape, narrated by Inuit Elder Mike Tunalaaq Gibbons, and highlighted by a playful score from The White Lotus composer Cristóbal Tapia de Veer, this tragicomic portrait of one of the animal realm’s most regal creatures gives rise to bigger conversations about climate change, displacement, migration and the rights of habitation.
Letterboxd 3.48/5；纪录片 / 自然世界 / 维州首映。推荐理由：政治与社会现实、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。奖项/展映线索：有电影节展映/奖项线索

英文原文简介Having left her job in Delhi, 32-year-old Bishnu returns to the village in Sikkim where she grew up. She stays in the family home, joining three generations of women: her grandmother, who misses her Dubai-based son; her mother, who juggles domestic and communal pressures; and her pregnant older sister, who is avoiding her husband and in-laws. Bishnu knows she has to help them, but her progressive views clash with those of the townsfolk. Meanwhile, her fondness for local architect Gyan only complicates matters. Winning the Busan International Film Festival’s Songwon Vision and Taipei Film Commission awards, Tribeny Rai’s rousing feature debut tackles the conflict between tradition and modernity by way of one woman’s journey towards forging her own path. Set against breathtaking views of remote north-eastern India, the film recalls the works of Jia Zhang-ke in its dramatisation of how ‘progress’ – seen here through the prevalence of iPads, K-pop and karaoke – can reshape a culture. In her prodigious breakout role, optometrist-turned-actor Gaumaya Gurung injects Bishnu with complexity, playing her as both a maverick with a brattish disregard for custom and a firebrand unshackling herself from patriarchal strictures.

It’s a balancing act that director Sara Dosa already perfected in her breakout Fire of Love (MIFF 2022), which shone a new light on the work of pioneering volcanologist couple Katia and Maurice Krafft. Arriving at MIFF via Sundance, SXSW and CPH:DOX, Time and Water is a moving meditation on what once was, and what has already vanished.

However, an unexpected event not only drives a wedge between the pair but also destabilises the school’s social hierarchy. These disruptions go on to mark both boys in profound ways, through their adolescent years and well into adulthood. Bowing at Cannes Directors’ Fortnight, Kohei Kadowaki’s stunning and stirringly told directorial debut recalls Hirokazu Kore-eda’s Monster (MIFF 2023) in its preoccupation with the impacts of childhood cruelty and Akira Kurosawa’s Rashomon in its bisected structure representing each protagonist’s point of view, filling in gaps of memory and offering alternative perspectives on proceedings. Rendered using a dynamic, at times dreamlike blend of rotoscoped and hand-drawn 2D animation, We Are Aliens is a beautiful, bittersweet meditation on lost innocence and the internecine fractures that can complicate the experience of growing up.

这是一部2026年美国剧情、实验、悬疑长片。导演：Jack Auen, Kevin Walker。MIFF 信息：实验影像、维州首映。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、记忆与历史、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Béatrice Courte (played by real-life professor Anne Laure Sellier) is a polylingual academic with research interests in the darkest corners of philosophy. When she encounters a short paragraph on the Chronovisor – a device built in the 1950s that claimed to “photograph the past” as a kind of spectral, visual time machine – she soon becomes obsessed. Camping out at libraries, poring over pages and chasing up leads in four different languages, Béatrice is hot on the trail of the machine’s inventor: an eccentric real-life Benedictine monk named Father Pellegrino Ernetti. Is he still alive? Is his machine a hoax? And how is the Catholic Church involved? With its closing crawl listing a bunch of “creditors” including Jorge Luis Borges, Umberto Eco, Roberto Bolaño and Paul Auster, this hyper-literary work of sleuthing offers an experimental, lo-fi riff on reading-room conspiracy classics like The Ninth Gate (MIFF 2000), Neil LaBute’s Possession and even The Da Vinci Code . Neither strictly documentary nor fiction, the debut feature of directors and academics Kevin Walker and Jack Auen fashions an uncanny bricolage from largely authentic books, magazines, journals and degraded videos. Shot on 16mm in a host of shadowy, Gothic libraries, this is an atmospheric, slyly funny oddity that cast a spell on audiences at Rotterdam and New Directors/New Films.

英文原文简介Gianina is a live-in nanny for a wealthy family in Bordeaux. One of the many Romanians who go to France seeking better economic conditions, she keeps the extravagant home shipshape, cooks the family their favourite Thai meals and cares for their occasionally bratty young son. In the evenings, Gianina divides her time between rehearsals for a play – specifically, a bawdy, experimental adaptation of the titular 1900 Octave Mirbeau novel previously brought to screen by Jean Renoir and Luis Buñuel – and video-calling her daughter, who jealously pines for her back in their home village. Feted at Cannes, Radu Jude’s latest class satire operates in a realist, somewhat melancholic register closer to that of Kontinental ’25 (MIFF 2025) than to his anarchic Dracula . Anchored by excellent performances from Ana Dumitraşcu as Gianina and Mélanie Thierry and Vincent Macaigne ( Suspended Time , MIFF 2024) as her employers – as well as Ilinca Manolache, the irrepressible star of Jude’s 2023 opus Do Not Expect Too Much From the End of the World – this left-of-field literary riff is both deeply compassionate and merciless in dramatising the sometimes absurd, often humiliating, plight of migrant workers.

英文原文简介Resembling a pompadoured, older Robert Mitchum, Al Cook (born Alois Koch in Vienna, 1945) has lived in the same apartment all his life. In the basement, he maintains a humble recording studio – also the site of a shrine to his musical idols, Elvis chief among them. But Al’s building is under threat by developers; he is, in fact, the last remaining resident. Contemplating the upheaval to come, Al is drawn to the idea of finally visiting Memphis, the faraway, foreign city that gave birth to the music to which he’s dedicated his life. As in their previous films Vera , Mister Universo and La Pivellina (MIFF 2010), directors Tizza Covi and Rainer Frimmel centre a 16mm character study on a non-professional actor whom they’ve invited to enact a version of themselves for their camera – in this case, a minor celebrity in his home country who is possessed of a mellowed, graceful swagger. Pricked with the dry humour of Aki Kaurismäki, this Berlinale Competition selection is a laconic, bittersweet portrait of a man who is beautifully – and, in some ways, tragically – out of sync with his time.

#91Flesh and Fuel🎬 LB 3.63 长片
2026 · 90 分钟 · 剧情、爱情 · 欧洲与英国 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Pierre Le Gall · 法国、波兰
🏆 获奖、戛纳
英文原文Awarded the inaugural Queer Palm Revelation award at Cannes, this swooning feature debut trails the deepening romantic spark that forms between two long-haul truckers.
这是一部2026年法国、波兰剧情、爱情长片。导演：Pierre Le Gall。MIFF 信息：欧洲与英国、澳洲首映。核心看点：亲密关系、政治与社会现实。
英文原文简介Due to the nature of their work, Étienne and Bartosz are ships – or semitrailers – in the night. And while the Frenchman and the Pole both drive trucks carrying all manner of goods across Europe, they couldn’t be more different: whereas reticent Étienne has been hardened by his experiences, gregarious Bartosz retains his zest for life despite its hardships. What was meant to be a one-off hook-up by the side of the road transforms into a profound, continent-spanning romance. There’s no dearth of works tackling the difficult pursuit of queer love, but Pierre Le Gall’s indelible answer to God’s Own Country (MIFF 2017) and Brief Encounter enriches its tale of unexpected connection by implicating clashes of culture and economy and exploring questions of self-acceptance, ambition and blue-collar alienation. Bolstered by Antoine Cormier’s sensitive lensing and Paul Sabin’s affecting score, actors Alexis Manenti and Julian Świeżewski enthral as the film’s central couple, magnetically portraying their chemistry and their distinct responses to this tricky relationship. Flesh and Fuel shows how love can bloom in the most unlikely of places, so long as we’re willing to take a different route.

🏆 柏林电影节
英文原文An enigmatic woman with no name books herself a one-way trip in order to drink her way through West Berlin in Ulrike Ottinger’s most revered film. | Setting off on a curious odyssey through Berlin’s bourgeois and bohemian drinking establishments, she invites a woman of very different means (Christine Lutze) to join her for a...
这是一部1979年West Germany剧情、实验长片。导演：Ulrike Ottinger。MIFF 信息：Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels。核心看点：家庭关系、亲密关系、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Dressed to the neuns, Tabea Blumenschein (known only here as “she”) arrives at Tegel Airport with one thing on her mind: alcohol. Setting off on a curious odyssey through Berlin’s bourgeois and bohemian drinking establishments, she invites a woman of very different means (Christine Lutze) to join her for a cognac or 10, and together they rub shoulders – at an aloof distance – with the city’s outré inhabitants (played by an eclectic cast including Nina Hagen, Eddie Constantine and Martin Kippenberger). Intent on her own oblivion, she pays no attention to the Greek chorus following her all the while: three sociologists in houndstooth suits whose conversation revolves around moral judgements and facts about gendered alcoholism. Director Joanna Hogg ( The Eternal Daughter , MIFF 2023; The Souvenir , MIFF 2019) has said that this film had a “decisive influence” on her desire to become a filmmaker, having seen it at age 19 and likening it to her love of the work of both Derek Jarman and Powell and Pressburger. Frequent Ottinger collaborator Blumenschein (star of Madame X: An Absolute Ruler and co-director of The Enchantment of the Blue Sailors ) is dazzling in this “portrait of a drinker” (as the original German title translates to), bringing a doomed charisma to a mostly wordless performance. She also designed the glamorously clamorous costumes, and appears briefly in drag.
Letterboxd 3.73/5；剧情、实验 / Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels。推荐理由：家庭关系、亲密关系、纪录片视角。奖项/展映线索：柏林电影节

英文原文简介Sylvie, a reclusive and irascible novelist living in squalor in Paris, struggles to get the creative juices flowing. To address this, she decides to train her telescope on the apartment across the street, where she spies two men and a woman fumbling around with sound recording equipment. Fascinated, she conjures up a melodramatic backstory for the threesome and starts typing. But when a stranger enters her orbit, the lines between fantasy, fabrication and fixation begin to blur. Asghar Farhadi’s follow-up to the Cannes Grand Prix–awarded A Hero (MIFF 2021) and Oscar winners The Salesman (MIFF 2016) and A Separation (MIFF 2011) is a suspenseful meta-thriller loosely based on the episode of Krzysztof Kieślowski’s Decalogue (MIFF 1990) that became A Short Film About Love . Co-written by Farhadi and his brother Saeed, the film evokes Hitchcock and Coppola but deploys its own psychologically complex provocation on truth, intention and interpersonal obsession. Elevated by Guillaume Deffontaines’s sumptuous cinematography and Zbigniew Preisner’s haunting score, the performances from Vincent Cassel ( The Shrouds , MIFF 2024), Virginie Efira ( A Private Life , MIFF 2025), Pierre Niney ( The Count of Monte Cristo ) and Adam Bessa ( Ghost Trail , MIFF 2024) – along with screen legend Catherine Deneuve in cameo – are superb, while lead Isabelle Huppert shines as an ill-tempered artist desperate to cling on to fading relevance.

#94迷魂記 Vertigo🎬 LB 4.22 长片
1958 · 128 分钟 · 剧情、惊悚 · Kim Novak: Hollywood Heretic · 导演 Alfred Hitchcock · 美国
这是一部1958年美国剧情、惊悚长片。导演：Alfred Hitchcock。MIFF 信息：Kim Novak: Hollywood Heretic。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、失去与哀悼、悬疑 / 犯罪张力。
英文原文简介Former San Francisco detective John “Scottie” Ferguson (James Stewart) is hired by an old college acquaintance to trail his wife, Madeleine Elster (Kim Novak), claiming she might be possessed and suicidal. It’s not long before Scottie is deeply infatuated with his enigmatic mark, then shattered at her untimely death. In the grip of obsession, he meets a woman on the street, Judy Barton, whom he proceeds to make over in order to resurrect Madeleine as he remembers her – leading once again to tragedy. Initially, Alfred Hitchcock wanted Vera Miles for the dual role of Madeleine and Judy in Vertigo . When she became unavailable, he instead hired Novak, at that time a darling of the American moviegoing public. Though she was only 24 at the time of the film’s production, her performance is that of a much wiser and more experienced actor: while the genius of Hitchcock is undeniably central to the film’s construction and Novak’s presentation within the frame, it’s the latter’s own complexity that brings nuance to the two distinct women she plays. The palpable chemistry between her and Stewart (again on display in Bell, Book and Candle , released the same year) makes the tragedy that unfolds in Vertigo all the more keenly felt.

#95Gabin🎬 LB 3.60 长片

🏆 戛纳
英文原文Gracefully condensing a decade’s worth of footage, this tender nonfiction gem out of Cannes chronicles the adolescence of a boy in northern France.
这是一部2026年法国、德国、瑞士纪录片长片。导演：Maxence Voiseux。MIFF 信息：纪录片单元、国际首映。核心看点：家庭关系、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Young Gabin Jourdel lives in Artois, an agricultural region in economic decline. His mother, Patricia, is a cattle farmer; his father, Dominique, a butcher. Dominique intends for Gabin to one day take over his business, but even at the age of eight, the boy has reservations; demonstrably less at ease with his peers than with the Brown Swiss cows tended to by his mother, he would prefer to work with “living animals”. Over 10 years, as he grows up in front of director Maxence Voiseux’s camera, Gabin negotiates not only the burdens of familial expectation but also the limitations of his rural environment. Voiseux achieves a seamless, effortlessly intimate vérité style that suggests immense trust on the part of the Jourdel family, who first appeared in the director’s 2016 mid-length film The Heirs (this earlier documentary focusing on Dominique, his two brothers and their own cattle dealer father). Recalling both Richard Linklater’s Boyhood (MIFF 2014) and the beloved Up series (MIFF 1986), Gabin , with its quietly grand scope, is a poignant, truly impressive feature-length debut.

英文原文Winner of four AFI Awards, Sarah Watt’s prismatic and improbably funny tale of looming tragedy is independent Australian cinema at its off-kilter best. | This auspicious live-action debut by Sydney-born, Melbourne-schooled animator and filmmaker Sarah Watt premiered in 2005, when it screened at MIFF alongside a retrospective of her animated shorts.
这是一部2005年澳大利亚剧情、喜剧长片。导演：Sarah Watts。MIFF 信息：Director in Focus: Sarah Watt。核心看点：家庭关系、成长与青春、亲密关系、政治与社会现实、失去与哀悼、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介An Adelaide artist who earns her crust as a painter of sympathy card seascapes, Meryl – played by Justine Clarke, stepping out from Play School ’s square window – is prone to morbidly nightmarish fantasies, lovingly rendered in hand-drawn animations. On her way home from her father’s funeral, Meryl has a genuine run-in with the reaper when she witnesses the death of a pedestrian in a train accident. This tragedy becomes the unlikely basis for a fraught whirlwind romance with a photojournalist (William McInnes) dealing with demons of his own, as well as the fulcrum of the film’s multiple interlocking portraits of grief. This auspicious live-action debut by Sydney-born, Melbourne-schooled animator and filmmaker Sarah Watt premiered in 2005, when it screened at MIFF alongside a retrospective of her animated shorts. In addition to sweeping that year’s AFI Awards, Watt also picked up the Toronto International Film Festival’s Discovery Award. Two decades on, Look Both Ways stands as a prime and, against all odds, uplifting example of the breezily black humour that has characterised a number of the nation’s most iconic films.

英文原文简介Argentinian designer Catalina has just won a prestigious award in Geneva, but something within her has clearly come unmoored. She drifts aimlessly through city streets in her turquoise coat, then casually throws herself off a bridge into the river below. Though she survives the attempt, back home in Buenos Aires she can’t shake a new, debilitating fear of water, which she’s too ashamed to share with her husband Pedro and small daughter Sofia. Her hair becomes increasingly bedraggled – one of the few visible signs of an inner turbulence that buffets Catalina between mental agony, dissociation and an almost sublime sensitivity. Bowing in TIFF’s Platform strand, The Currents went on to win San Sebastián’s RTVE – Another Look Award for the work at the festival best capturing “subjects related to the female world”. Immersing us in Catalina’s experience, director Milagros Mumenthaler’s deeply observational storytelling invites comparisons to her compatriot Lucrecia Martel ( Zama , MIFF 2018), submerging Catalina’s traumas in metaphor through a flow of light and textures.

Living alone in an isolated corner of a rural property, he rarely sees other people, and barely says a word when he does. Working as a woodcutter, he chops trees, shaves them down and loads them for transport. In quieter moments, he smokes, takes a shit or lies in the sun. And at the end of the day, he kills, prepares and barbecues his dinner: a classic woodcutter’s meal of roasted armadillo.

#100Joybubbles🎬 LB 3.57 长片

这是一部2026年美国纪录片长片。导演：Rachael J. Morrison。MIFF 信息：纪录片单元、维州首映。核心看点：家庭关系、记忆与历史、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Before internet hackers popularised the concept of scrambling technology, the analog pioneers known as ‘phone phreaks’ discovered that they could manipulate landlines simply by whistling at certain frequencies. Born Josef Engressia in 1949 before adopting his cheerful mononym in 1991, Joybubbles was one such phreaker. From the tender age of four he was obsessed with the telephone, and he first discovered he could perform the magical 2600-hertz whistle aged just seven. As a whiz-kid, he was drawn to experiment with technology, but it also represented a kind of lifeline: born blind, Joybubbles used the phone to forge connections with people – and to help others connect, too. Though he died in 2007, Joybubbles can narrate his own story thanks to filmmaker Rachael J. Morrison, who uncovered a treasure trove of his audio recordings. In chronicling its singular subject’s life, underpinned by trauma but still overflowng with kindness, this loving and suitably uplifting Sundance-premiering documentary – produced by Sarah Winshall, who also produced By Design (MIFF 2025) and served as a consulting producer on Maddie’s Secret (MIFF 2026) – takes viewers back to a pre-internet era via its wealth of archival material, spotlighting a sidelined but fascinating chapter of hacking history.

英文原文Swiss filmmaker Tobias Nölle has found acclaim for his experimental, eerie narrative features, from 2016 Berlinale stand-out Aloys to 2024 sci-fi parable Preparations for a Miracle .
这是一部2026年瑞士纪录片、剧情长片。导演：Loran Bonnardot, Tobias Nölle。MIFF 信息：纪录片单元、维州首映。核心看点：亲密关系、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Tristan da Cunha is the most remote place of human habitation in the world. A volcanic speck in the South Atlantic, midway between Argentina and South Africa, it’s visited by only six to eight boats per year, its 230-odd inhabitants vastly outnumbered by penguins. Loran Bonnardot, a jaded Parisian physician with a lifetime serving in Médecins Sans Frontières, has spent 30 years visiting Tristan; now, he’s hoping to permanently relocate there to escape the hectic nature of 21st-century living. As Bonnardot explores the island’s wilderness and tries to integrate into its community, he awaits approval for permanent residency. Swiss filmmaker Tobias Nölle has found acclaim for his experimental, eerie narrative features, from 2016 Berlinale stand-out Aloys to 2024 sci-fi parable Preparations for a Miracle . Here, directing in collaboration with Bonnardot, Nölle mounts a dreamlike, meditative film that blurs lines between ethnography, documentary and fantasy. With cinematography that evocatively brings Tristan da Cunha’s landscape to life, this is a quiet, contemplative study in both the pleasures and the perils of isolation – the perfect film for anyone with a love of exploration or a desire to escape.

英文原文简介When The Critics, as they call themselves, first formed, its members were not even teenagers. Though the Nigerian cinema emerging from the Nollywood hub of Lagos is famously prolific, the collective’s members live hundreds of kilometres away in the northern city of Kaduna (also known as Croc City). The films that truly inspire these young adults – predominantly sci-fi blockbusters – were made not in Nollywood but in Hollywood. Hand-sewn green screen, makeshift tripods, borrowed iPhones: schooling themselves via Wikipedia and YouTube tutorials, The Critics use whatever’s on hand to furnish their playful but grand moviemaking visions. In the process, they attract thousands of fans online, including Star Trek director J.J. Abrams. New Zealand director Pietra Brettkelly ( Yellow Is Forbidden , MIFF 2018) worked with behind-the-scenes footage – shot over more than a decade by The Critics themselves – to co-author an account of their story to date. Tracing the group’s burgeoning political consciousness alongside their creative development and launching its international festival run at this year’s Berlinale, Crocodile reveals the tensions that arise between members as well as the harsh realities that their love of cinema has enabled them to transcend.

英文原文简介Elliot starts working for debauched artist Erika Tracy, who foxed the fine-art world into intellectualising her giant papier-mâché phalluses and labial canvases. She immediately grooms her wide-eyed young assistant as her submissive muse, awakening his nascent appetites. Dazzled by the pleasures of pegging, handcuffs, ball gags and pig masks, Elliot shares all the steamy tea with his horny gay co-worker and his repressed housemate. But nine-and-a-half weeks of candy-coloured erotic mayhem later, Elliot’s in pink lingerie and in trouble with the law … Queer punk provocateur Gregg Araki ( Mysterious Skin , MIFF 2005) titillated Sundance 2026 with his first big-screen outing since 2014: a delirious dom-com that’s a raunchy blast for everyone, teasing Gen Z with the fun they’re missing while also satirising the Teen Apocalypse Trilogy auteur’s own permissive cultural sphere. Delightful as the down-for-anything Elliot, Cooper Hoffman ( Licorice Pizza ) sparks with Olivia Wilde ( Don’t Worry Darling ; Drinking Buddies , MIFF 2013), whose Erika is a hilariously unhinged mix of Norma Desmond, Miranda Priestly and Maude Lebowski. #104Tangles🎬 LB 4.05 长片
2026 · 103 分钟 · 动画 · 动画单元 · 维州首映 · 导演 Leah Nelson · 美国
这是一部2026年美国动画长片。导演：Leah Nelson。MIFF 信息：动画单元、维州首映。核心看点：家庭关系、亲密关系。
英文原文简介Sarah is in her twenties and embracing life in San Francisco, where she has a job she loves at a queer magazine and a new girlfriend she adores even more. It’s 1999, and the future looks bright. But on a trip back home to the conservative Maine town she only recently escaped, she notices something’s not quite right with her mum, Midge. When the diagnosis comes – early-onset Alzheimer’s disease – Sarah finds herself caught between two worlds, juggling the life she was just beginning with the one she thought she’d left behind. Working closely with Sarah Leavitt, the author of the graphic novel Tangles: A Story about Alzheimer’s, My Mother and Me, debut director Leah Nelson has created an exceptionally moving tribute – not only to the source material, but also to everyone touched by the ruthless tangles of Alzheimer’s. The gorgeous, mostly black-and-white, hand-drawn animation pays homage to the book while not replicating it, and weaves seamlessly from authenticity to surreal fantasy as the story dictates. Featuring a voice cast that includes Abbi Jacobson, Julia-Louis Dreyfus, Bryan Cranston, Seth Rogen, Samira Wiley, Beanie Feldstein, Pamela Adlon, Sarah Silverman, Bowen Yang and Wanda Sykes, Tangles is a playful, sweet and achingly honest film about family, love and the brutal truths of a cruel disease. Bring tissues.

#105Liverpool🎬 LB 3.61 长片
2008 · 84 分钟 · 剧情 · Lisandro Alonso · 法国、德国、西班牙、荷兰、阿根廷
🏆 戛纳
英文原文Lisandro Alonso’s fourth feature – which, like its predecessors, bowed at Cannes – marshals a larger budget to follow another of his lonely men across a vivid landscape.
这是一部2008年法国、德国、西班牙、荷兰、阿根廷剧情长片。MIFF 信息：Lisandro Alonso。核心看点：家庭关系。
英文原文简介Farrel (Juan Fernández) is a merchant seaman, toiling away below deck on long-haul shipping routes. When his ship is forced to dock at Ushuaia, southern Argentina’s gateway to Antarctica, he requests permission to go ashore to find out if his ailing mother is still alive. Downing drinks as he goes, the permanently soused sailor eventually manages to hitch a ride on a logging truck headed for his old hometown, to the place and the people he left behind. There, he discovers that his mother is still alive, but barely – and that she’s living with Farrel’s own daughter, Analía, whom he abandoned prior to her birth. Lisandro Alonso’s fourth feature – which, like its predecessors, bowed at Cannes – marshals a larger budget to follow another of his lonely men across a vivid landscape. Shot amid the icy surrounds of Tierra del Fuego, it’s a sensorial work aswirl with wind and snow, aching with isolation both environmental and emotional. Though armed with more traditional narrative elements than Alonso’s first three movies, Liverpool is another work in which so much story – and backstory – is conveyed silently, perceptible only to engaged viewers.

🏆 柏林电影节、首映
英文原文Premiering in Berlinale’s Panorama section, her empathetic drama refuses to reinterrogate Roya through the camera’s objectifying gaze.
这是一部2026年德国、伊朗、Luxembourg、Czechia剧情、惊悚长片。导演：Mahnaz Mohammadi。MIFF 信息：非洲与中东、维州首映。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、记忆与历史。
英文原文简介Iranian teacher Roya (Melisa Sözen, Winter Sleep ) is a political prisoner, detained and humiliatingly tortured after her students burned their hijabs. The regime offers her two options: make a televised confession falsely denouncing her beliefs; or face indefinite solitary confinement in her tiny prison cell. But for Roya, choice and coercion blur as she drifts between memories, interrogators’ lies and isolation-driven hallucinations. Is her family really at risk if she doesn’t confess? Is her silence resilience, or will it only confirm her guilt? Will confessing end the terror, or bring it inside forever? Director Mahnaz Mohammadi has been repeatedly arrested for defending Iranian women’s rights; like her protagonist, she spent months in Tehran’s notorious Evin prison. Premiering in Berlinale’s Panorama section, her empathetic drama refuses to reinterrogate Roya through the camera’s objectifying gaze. Instead, visceral point-of-view sequences and dreamlike voyages into Roya’s defiant past and bruised present honour the dissident mind’s struggle against authoritarian power.

#109Freak Orlando🎬 LB 3.57 长片
1981 · 128 分钟 · 剧情、实验、奇幻 · Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels · 导演 Ulrike Ottinger · West Germany
🏆 柏林电影节
英文原文...by way of Tod Browning’s infamous 1932 horror Freaks , this is the second in Ottinger’s ‘Berlin Trilogy’, wedged between Ticket of No Return and Dorian Gray in the Mirror of the Yellow Press ....
这是一部1981年West Germany剧情、实验、奇幻长片。导演：Ulrike Ottinger。MIFF 信息：Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels。核心看点：家庭关系、记忆与历史、恐怖 / 超自然。
英文原文简介Across five sweeping, nonlinear adventures, the multi-named, gender-fluid and barely ageing Orlando (played by avant-garde New German Cinema star Magdalena Montezuma) explores the history of civilisation. From a modern department store in Freak City to medieval times, and from the Spanish Inquisition to a carnival sideshow, Orlando ultimately lands in Northern Italy for a competition crowning “The Ugliest Person of the Year”. A punk shapeshifter, our hero jostles with a wild cast of acrobats and performers with a diverse array of bodies and identities – including self-flagellating leather boys, the “Freak Orlando bunnies”, and conjoined twins memorably played by legendary French New Wave figure Jackie Raynal and frequent Ulrike Ottinger collaborator Delphine Seyrig (who appears throughout in multiple roles). A loose adaptation of Virginia Woolf’s epic 1928 novel Orlando: A Biography by way of Tod Browning’s infamous 1932 horror Freaks , this is the second in Ottinger’s ‘Berlin Trilogy’, wedged between Ticket of No Return and Dorian Gray in the Mirror of the Yellow Press . Described by Ottinger as a “ histoire du monde ”, or “small theatre of the world”, Freak Orlando is perhaps her most unclassifiable film. A cinematic fever dream, it challenges idealised norms of beauty, gender and sexuality through pageantry – an assemblage of irreverent tableaux vivants in lush colour and extravagant costuming.
Letterboxd 3.57/5；剧情、实验、奇幻 / Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels。推荐理由：家庭关系、记忆与历史、恐怖 / 超自然。奖项/展映线索：柏林电影节

When the studio can’t afford to pay his salary, he’s gifted a VR headset instead. Zha soon grows obsessed with the virtual realm, and the borders between reality and illusion begin to blur. Moving between hand-drawn animation and digital live action in its VR sequences, Light Pillar offers a remarkably refreshing blend of romance, sci-fi and drama. Blessed with both a sense of Ghibli-esque whimsy and a cultural critique of modernisation-mad China that’s reminiscent of the works of Jia Zhang-ke, the film is at once an achingly sad portrait of loneliness, an epitaph for the glory days of cinema and a smart critique of people turning to technology to solve their problems. 🏆 戛纳、导演双周、首映
英文原文Produced by Apichatpong Weerasethakul, on whose own films Sompot regularly worked as an assistant, and premiering at Cannes Directors’ Fortnight, 9 Temples to Heaven is a sensitive, involving saga.
这是一部2026年泰国、法国、新加坡、挪威剧情长片。导演：Sompot Chidgasornpongse。MIFF 信息：亚太单元、维州首映。核心看点：家庭关系、亲密关系、政治与社会现实、失去与哀悼、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介When Sakol hears an unsettling, weirdly specific prophecy about his ageing mother’s imminent death, he springs into action. Knowing that nine is a fortuitous number in Thai culture, he bundles the same amount of family members into a mini-van to visit nine temples in one day. It’s an ambitious attempt to cultivate enough karma for “Grandma” to find a peaceful afterlife, but things don’t go as planned. As three generations of family members squabble over religion and personal responsibility, and they encounter a mix of genuinely kind and commercially opportunistic monks, Sakol’s grand plan starts to feel like a futile undertaking. As the day comes to an end, will his faith finally be rewarded? Sompot Chidgasornpongse’s debut, the documentary Railway Sleepers (MIFF 2017), bunked down with passengers taking long-distance train rides across Thailand. His second feature – and first venture into fiction – is a beautifully observed portrait of the relationship between religious tradition and capitalist society, drawing from personal experiences of his own family pilgrimages to Buddhist temples. Produced by Apichatpong Weerasethakul, on whose own films Sompot regularly worked as an assistant, and premiering at Cannes Directors’ Fortnight, 9 Temples to Heaven is a sensitive, involving saga.

One day, he catches a glimpse of a boy on TV raving about finding fame in Buenos Aires. This sparks a flame in Milo, who decides to escape his provincial existence by way of a city-bound train. But Milo quickly discovers that the journey and the destination are so much more than he could have ever imagined. Lorenzo Ferro and Lucas A. Vignale’s Berlinale-premiering feature debut is a sublime, magic-realist coming-of-age tale that blurs the factual and fantastical elements of Milo’s journey to striking effect. As the film unpacks its depictions of duality – between childhood and growing up, creative rigour and rebellion, the safety and stagnation of home – breakout actor Milo Barría skilfully embodies the protagonist’s wide-eyed hunger for adventure. Intimate and inventive, The River Train captures the ever-difficult question of whether to continue to dream or face the reality of waking life.

When a tragic accident tears their friendship apart just before the start of senior year, Minnie embarks on a close friendship with Callie’s elegant mother, Helen – a complicated dynamic that causes friction between Minnie and her own perpetually frazzled working mother, Barbara. The third feature collaboration from husband-and-wife duo Kelly O’Sullivan and Alex Thompson ( Saint Frances ; Ghostlight ), Mouse is a heartfelt and deeply humanistic portrayal of the complexities of navigating loss at any age. 英文原文简介Misael is content with his spartan life in a remote corner of Argentina’s picturesque La Pampa province. Dwelling in a shack, he spends his days cutting down trees, treating the wood and dealing with local traders. Soon, however, an unexpected responsibility upends his life, and the logic of his days fades away in a place where human reason holds no meaning. Lisandro Alonso returns 25 years later to the protagonist of his debut feature, 2001’s simple, soft-spoken landmark of slow cinema La libertad . This latest feature, whose title – in Spanish, La libertad doble – directly calls back to its predecessor, reunites Alonso with the same nonprofessional lead, Misael Saavedra, along with cinematographer Cobi Migliora, once again shooting on 35mm. Through this mirroring, the director reflects on how life in Argentina has grown more precarious over the past quarter-century, for lumberjacks and filmmakers alike.

#116Marc by Sofia🎬 LB 3.35 长片
2025 · 87 分钟 · 纪录片 · 纪录片单元 · 维州首映 · 导演 Sofia Coppola · 美国
🏆 威尼斯、首映
英文原文...plate, Coppola’s disinterest in both industry drama and didactic biography separates this Venice-premiering A24 documentary from more conventional couturier profiles; her fascination with the evanescent is instead perfectly su...
这是一部2025年美国纪录片长片。导演：Sofia Coppola。MIFF 信息：纪录片单元、维州首映。核心看点：政治与社会现实、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Filmmaker Sofia Coppola met fashion designer Marc Jacobs in 1993, when her downtown New York minimalism intrigued the upstart who’d just brought grunge to the Perry Ellis runway. They shared a taste for poised perfectionism, as well as an unusually self-effacing temperament among the big egos in their respective professions. Thirty years on, as Marc’s spring 2024 show approaches, his one-time muse hangs out in his studio, watching him plan the staging as meticulously as the clothes. “In another life I really want to be a theatre director,” sighs the 60-year-old as he enthuses about a creative practice they both know intimately. Jacobs and Coppola both intuitively gravitate towards the playful and attainable rather than confronting or luxuriating in wealth. Despite its familiar ‘prepping for the big show’ template, Coppola’s disinterest in both industry drama and didactic biography separates this Venice-premiering A24 documentary from more conventional couturier profiles; her fascination with the evanescent is instead perfectly suited to tracing the wandering pathways of creative inspiration and influence that guide her subject’s creative sensibility. Fans of Coppola’s fiction work will appreciate these generous conversations and associative flurries of archival montage alike.
Letterboxd 3.35/5；纪录片 / 纪录片单元 / 维州首映。推荐理由：政治与社会现实、纪录片视角。奖项/展映线索：威尼斯、首映

#117Strawberries🎬 LB 3.35 长片
2026 · 103 分钟 · 剧情 · 欧洲与英国 · 维州首映 · 导演 Laïla Marrakchi · 法国、比利时、西班牙、Morocco
🏆 戛纳、一种关注、首映
英文原文In this Cannes Un Certain Regard–premiering political drama, two Moroccan women doing seasonal work in Spain struggle against dire labour conditions.
这是一部2026年法国、比利时、西班牙、Morocco剧情长片。导演：Laïla Marrakchi。MIFF 信息：欧洲与英国、维州首映。核心看点：亲密关系、政治与社会现实。
英文原文简介Hoping to make ends meet, tetchy Hasna and timid Meriem set sail for the Spanish province of Huelva, where they will earn 35 euros per day as strawberry pickers. The work is onerous, and their difficult circumstances – the language barrier, the oppressive conditions, the distance from loved ones in Morocco – are ameliorated only by their camaraderie with their female colleagues. When acts of extortion and sexual assault throw a wrench into those relationships, however, Hasna and Meriem must decide whether to protect their livelihoods or their dignity. Co-written by Delphine Agut ( The Story of Souleymane , MIFF 2024; Inshallah a Boy , MIFF 2023) and based on real-world cases, Laïla Marrakchi’s bracing third feature depicts the insidious systems that enable migrant and gender-based exploitation across the Mediterranean. Timely and eye-opening, Strawberries sheds light not just on the toxic feedback loop between desperation and oppression, but also on the oblivious privilege of the First World societies that rely on this workforce. Nisrin Erradi ( Adam , MIFF 2019) is formidable as Hasna: a compelling yet flawed heroine whose combative spirit jars with her instinct to prioritise self-preservation.

英文原文简介December 1995: riding high on her hit comedy Billy Madison and numerous celebrated music videos, Tamra Davis ( Jean-Michel Basquiat: The Radiant Child , MIFF 2010) brought her Sony Hi8 camcorder to Australia on tour with her new husband, Mike D of the Beastie Boys. At Summersault, an upstart festival hoping to outshine the Big Day Out, Davis recorded electric live sets from the Beasties and pals Pavement, Sonic Youth, Dave Grohl’s new band Foo Fighters and Kim Deal’s Breeders-hiatus project The Amps. And as Bikini Kill’s Kathleen Hanna playfully interviewed other musos backstage, Davis unknowingly documented the riot grrrl icon falling for future husband Adam ‘Ad-Rock’ Horovitz. Thirty years later, Davis found a shoebox of old 8mm videotapes while evacuating her home during the Los Angeles Palisades wildfire. This precious time capsule – a last hurrah of scrappy underground camaraderie before landmark albums and arena superstardom – formed the basis for this wistful feature-length window into another era. Summersault didn’t last, but its young promoter Steve Pavlovic went on to found cult label Modular Recordings, decisively shaping Australian indie music. “It was such a different time,” Davis told the crowd at the film’s 2026 Sundance premiere – and this shaggy hangout travelogue will take you right back there.

Reuniting with Koh Jia Ler and Yeo Yann Yann – who both starred in Ilo Ilo (MIFF 2013) and Wet Season (MIFF 2020), the earlier entries in the director’s ‘Growing Up’ trilogy – Anthony Chen again dissects the intricacies of human relationships, this time also critiquing a Singapore where consumerism and class foment divisions. Twin interdisciplinary choreographers Hsieh Hsiao-Ting and Hsieh Hsiao-Wei invite you, too, to watch without moving. Poetic, abstract dance evokes ALS patients’ rich, heightened consciousness as everyday objects dissolve under the weight of illness: a motionless wheelchair; drifting curtains; a dining table for two; a fish in its bowl. 英文原文简介Slow-cinema legend Tsai Ming-liang accompanies actor Anong Houngheuangsy ( Days , MIFF 2021) back to his hometown, a rural Lao village situated amid rice paddies. Armed with only a Leica camera and a Canon camcorder, Tsai undertakes a minimalist meditation on the power of place. More drawn to the surrounding environment than the reunion between Anong and his family, Tsai’s ever-patient camera gazes on dogs, cats, cows, goats and house plants. For the Buddhist filmmaker, these lives are just as interesting as those of family members, farmers selling their wares at markets and stonemasons carving statues of Buddha. Tsai calls this film, shot over two weeks, a work of “handcrafted cinema”. Premiering at Venice, Back Home offers another still, quiet study for those attuned to Tsai’s filmmaking approach, and particularly the entries in his ongoing Walking series ( Abiding Nowhere , MIFF 2021; Journey to the West , MIFF 2014). Tsai first graced Melbourne screens with his sumptuous Vive l’amour in 1995; each new outing for cinema’s Zen master is a humble treasure to behold.

英文原文简介In 1972, groundbreaking Black filmmaker William Greaves – maker of the reality-bending 1968 vérité masterpiece Symbiopsychotaxiplasm: Take One (MIFF 2023) – issued an invitation to the surviving figureheads of the cultural boom that emanated from Harlem in the 1920s and 30s: to come together once again. The likes of Broadway pioneers Noble Sissle and Eubie Blake, artist Aaron Douglas and activist Louise Thompson Patterson convened one summer evening at the stately home of Duke Ellington, where the drinks and reminiscences flowed, crystallised by time. Behind the camera at this historic gathering was William’s son, David Greaves. With the elder Greaves having passed in 2014, it fell to David to ensure that this remarkable footage could at last be seen and celebrated. In Once Upon a Time in Harlem , he skilfully blends roving scenes from the party with sit-down interviews, also filmed onsite, to create an inviting, immersive atmosphere that positively crackles with the revolutionary verve and commentary of its subjects.

英文原文简介When his father suffers a stroke, Melbourne-based filmmaker Vee Shi returns to his hometown, Longtian, Fuqing, in south-eastern China, a small rural community that he left behind when he was 13. As the family’s proud, stubborn patriarch struggles with his compromised health and need for care, his estranged wife and daughter – who, due to China’s one-child policy, was given up for adoption prior to the director’s birth – are suddenly entrusted with the duty, and burden, of looking after a man who has often treated them badly. These strained family dynamics evoke a bigger-picture portrait of changing Chinese society and social values, where the once-total dedication to family is falling away. This unique hybrid documentary, initially conceived of as a scripted film wherein Shi’s family would play themselves, is an at times shockingly intimate portrait of familial love, duty and trauma. The MIFF Accelerator alum’s previous short Jia (MIFF 2023) was a drama inspired by his relationship with his mother, as well as the familial and cultural estrangement of living in a different country in another hemisphere. The Visions du Réel–selected Time and Tide – the first film ever to be shot in Longtian, and only the second to feature the disappearing Fuqing dialect – profoundly and often painfully extends that inquiry to the contested space of a fractured family home.

英文原文简介New York, late 1980s. He is loved, of course, despite his mercurial ego: by Dennis, his devoted partner, and by Brenda, his sister. Following Peter Hujar’s Day (MIFF 2025), Ira Sachs crafts another stirring time capsule of queer New York; The Man I Love also recalls his immediately previous work, Passages (MIFF 2023), in featuring a love triangle, but here the focus is less on erotic foibles than on the impetuousness of living on borrowed time. Working from a script from Sachs and his regular co-writer Mauricio Zacharias, and acting alongside a formidable Tom Sturridge, Rami Malek brilliantly incarnates Jimmy’s unapologetic audacity and the yearning fragility beneath his bravado. More than an AIDS drama, The Man I Love is a story of perseverance and performativity – about the shows we put on despite the obstacles of health and the heart.

这是一部1967年美国纪录片长片。导演：Shirley Clarke。MIFF 信息：锋利现实。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Holding court over a long, boozy December night at New York’s Hotel Chelsea, Jason Holliday serves up wild anecdotes of a life lived on the city’s margins, including working the streets as a hustler, doing time on Riker’s Island and even befriending Miles Davis – fraught, flamboyant tales that become profound reflections on race, class and sexuality. Meanwhile, the offscreen prompts from director Shirley Clarke ( Ornette: Made in America , MIFF 1987), a pioneering figure in documentary’s avant-garde, add to the film’s air of electric, off-the-cuff vérité. Just how much of Jason’s studied fabulousness, in which the self is nested within endless layers of performance, is an elaborate shield against a hostile world, including the provocations of his director? And to what extent might Clarke, whose antagonism stokes the film’s irresistible frisson, be said to be exploiting him? Both an exquisite study in character and a fascinating look at the ethics behind capturing performance in documentary, Portrait of Jason – like its subject – is a slippery, shapeshifting work, as exhilarating as it is unsettling.
Letterboxd 3.83/5；纪录片 / 锋利现实。推荐理由：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、纪录片视角。奖项/展映线索：暂无明确获奖信息，主要按评分、题材和导演风格推荐

#131Memory🎬 LB 3.72 长片
2025 · 98 分钟 · 纪录片 · 线上放映 · 维州首映 · 导演 Vladena Sandu · 法国、荷兰
这是一部2025年法国、荷兰纪录片长片。导演：Vladena Sandu。MIFF 信息：线上放映、维州首映。核心看点：家庭关系、成长与青春、政治与社会现实、记忆与历史、悬疑 / 犯罪张力、纪录片视角、恐怖 / 超自然。
英文原文简介In the late 1980s, six-year-old Vladlena Sandu was sent from Crimea to Grozny, Chechnya, to live with her grandparents. Little did she, or her family, know that the horrors of war would be right on their doorstep over the following decades through the fall of the Soviet Union and the ensuing Russo-Chechen Wars. In this poetic, autobiographical hybrid documentary, Sandu revisits her traumatic childhood memories, confronting the ways in which geopolitical conflict impacts children, and asking what can be done to break these generational cycles of violence. The influence of Andrei Tarkovsky, Pier Paolo Pasolini and Sergei Parajanov looms large in the evocative and lyrical imagery that makes up Memory , which incorporates live-action re-enactment, puppetry, animation, archival material and surreal vignettes shot on 16mm film. Nevertheless, this staggering, unique cinematic tapestry is thoroughly Sandu’s own. Depicting her tumultuous past with breathtaking intimacy and artistry, she also bears singular witness to the children whose lives are being threatened today by wars and conflict the world over.
Letterboxd 3.72/5；纪录片 / 线上放映 / 维州首映。推荐理由：家庭关系、成长与青春、政治与社会现实、记忆与历史、悬疑 / 犯罪张力、纪录片视角、恐怖 / 超自然。奖项/展映线索：暂无明确获奖信息，主要按评分、题材和导演风格推荐

#132愛之哨 Whistle🎬 LB 3.71 长片
2025 · 84 分钟 · 纪录片、喜剧 · 澳洲电影 · 维州首映 · 导演 Christopher Nelius · 日本、美国、澳大利亚、西班牙
这是一部2025年日本、美国、澳大利亚、西班牙纪录片、喜剧长片。导演：Christopher Nelius。MIFF 信息：澳洲电影、维州首映。核心看点：家庭关系、音乐与表演。
英文原文简介The Masters of Musical Whistling is an international competition that celebrates, well, whistling – at an elite level. Every two years, dedicated and supremely talented whistlers converge on Hollywood to showcase their art and, hopefully, whistle up a coveted trophy. The 2023 competitors include global whistling superstar Molly Lewis, who features on the Barbie soundtrack; Spaniard Ayna, who’s inherited her circus-performing parent’s charismatic stage presence; and Yuki, a Japanese whistling prodigy sick of being the runner-up. They’re all here because Carole Anne Kaufman, founder of the Masters and two-time world champion, wants to change how the world thinks about whistling. Thanks to Australian director Christopher Nelius, she just might. With genuine affection and care, Nelius ( Girls Can’t Surf ; Buoy , MIFF 2017) documents high and low notes for Kaufman and her competitors, on and offstage. Nelius clearly understands the visual language of the mockumentary; but while many of his subjects wouldn’t be out of place in a Christopher Guest film, there’s no mockery here. Instead, he respectfully centres this community’s incredible artistry through all the tears, bruised egos, heartaches and soaring joys. Funny, poignant and wonderfully weird, Whistle is a treat from start to finish – and, perhaps, just what the world needs right now.
Letterboxd 3.71/5；纪录片、喜剧 / 澳洲电影 / 维州首映。推荐理由：家庭关系、音乐与表演。奖项/展映线索：暂无明确获奖信息，主要按评分、题材和导演风格推荐

英文原文...zu Kore-eda’s earlier works Broker (MIFF 2022), Like Father, Like Son (MIFF 2013) and the Palme d’Or–winning Shoplifters (MIFF 2018)....
这是一部2026年日本剧情、科幻长片。导演：Hirokazu Kore-eda。MIFF 信息：主打佳片、维州首映。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、失去与哀悼。
英文原文简介In a near-future Japan of delivery drones and diet-monitoring fridges, REbirth has devised the ultimate remedy for grieving parents: a ‘replacement’ in the form of an anthropomorphic robot. Two years prior, an accident took architect Otone and carpenter Kensuke’s son Kakeru; when REbirth offers them a free trial, Otone doesn’t hesitate. While she becomes enamoured of the revived Kakeru, Kensuke is sceptical: “It’s a Tamagotchi. It’s a Roomba.” Gradually, they learn that making do is not the same as moving on. Despite its sci-fi trappings, Sheep in the Box is, more accurately, a study of complicated families, building on director Hirokazu Kore-eda’s earlier works Broker (MIFF 2022), Like Father, Like Son (MIFF 2013) and the Palme d’Or–winning Shoplifters (MIFF 2018). Inspired by an illustration from The Little Prince and evoking Pinocchio with its (not so) ‘real boy’, the film raises questions about humanity, loss and the ways technology can both help and harm. Actors Haruka Ayase ( Our Little Sister , MIFF 2015) and Daigo movingly portray Otone’s technophilia and Kensuke’s neo-Luddism as synecdoche for coping, while Rimu Kuwaki precociously imbues the robotic Kakeru with an affecting emotional depth.

英文原文简介In 2011, ambitious young music critic Grace plans a summer sabbatical in Montreal, sick of getting exploited by her Toronto alt-weekly editor and snubbed by chin-stroking bro colleagues. Moving in with chic DJ Madeleine and drummer Hugo, Grace starts promoting Hugo’s band Bone Patrol to impress its vain frontman Chevy, “the worst guy in Montreal” – though something slower and sweeter simmers with floppy-haired guitarist Archie. Things go off the frets as Grace’s planned 33 ⅓ book on Alanis Morissette’s Jagged Little Pill falls by the wayside, her funds run perilously low and past traumas resurface as bad choices. Writer/director Chandler Levack (Netflix’s Roommates ) based her sophomore feature on her own youth in Montreal’s alt trenches. Her affectionate but bittersweet romantic dramedy – more Reality Bites than Almost Famous – premiered at TIFF and toured to Vancouver, Stockholm and SXSW. As Grace, Barbie Ferreira ( Bob Trevino Likes It , MIFF 2024) brings fierce empathy to an impulsive, sometimes exasperating but easily recognisable protagonist, while Bone Patrol’s personnel include members of real-life Montreal band TOPS.

#136Strangers When We Meet🎬 LB 3.77 长片
1960 · 117 分钟 · 剧情、爱情 · Kim Novak: Hollywood Heretic · 导演 Richard Quine · 美国
这是一部1960年美国剧情、爱情长片。导演：Richard Quine。MIFF 信息：Kim Novak: Hollywood Heretic。核心看点：家庭关系、成长与青春、亲密关系。
英文原文简介Margaret “Maggie” Gault (Kim Novak) is listless, persisting in a stable but passionless marriage to a conservative prude. Kirk Douglas is Larry Coe, an architect in a happy but comfortable marriage who has just taken on a new project to design a house for a successful writer played by Ernie Kovacs ( Bell, Book and Candle , MIFF 2026). After a meet-cute at school pick-up and a follow-up at the local grocery store, Maggie and Larry embark on a tender, deeply felt affair, sharing a connection they haven’t previously enjoyed with anyone else – one in which they can be their authentic selves. But when nosy neighbour Felix (Walter Matthau, The Odd Couple ) discovers the dalliance, he makes a sinister play for Larry’s wife. Adapted from a novel by Evan Hunter, Strangers When We Meet is a gorgeously rendered melodrama that fields a mature viewpoint on adult relationships, layered with shades of grey. The film boasts an exceptional supporting cast: Matthau revels in his sleazy role as a smug spanner in the works; while Barbara Rush is also wonderful, exuding quiet wisdom and grace as Larry’s pragmatic and perceptive wife – her rebuff of Felix’s unwanted advances is a scene-stealer. The house that Larry constructs, meanwhile, was purpose-built for the film, designed by legendary Hollywood art directors Carl Anderson and Ross Bellah.

On his release, seemingly ill at ease with his newfound freedom, he sets out on a journey into the Argentine jungle armed with his trusty machete. 英文原文简介A filmmaker’s approach to chemistry experiments produces dazzlingly psychedelic results in this spectacular, scientifically illuminating Australian debut. When thinking about the world’s natural wonders, it’s likely the big stuff – the mountains, the canyons, the oceans – that first spring to mind. But what about those things you can’t see, such as light, gravity and quantum energy? Using a high-powered camera and absolutely no AI, Melbourne-based filmmaker Josef Gatti makes brilliantly manifest those intangible building blocks of our universe. Across 10 chapters, each dedicated to a single scientific concept, kaleidoscopic Petri dish displays are augmented by tracks from Nils Frahm and British electronic musician Rival Consoles. It’s nature, but like you’ve never seen it before.

The prisoners panic, pointing the finger at Dimas, but one clairvoyant inmate is adamant that there’s a sinister supernatural entity behind the killings. He warns the others that they’d better keep their auras clean through art, prayer and dance, lest they become the ghost’s next victim. The 12th feature by Indonesian genre master Joko Anwar ( Satan’s Slaves ), this action-packed horror-comedy has a lot on its mind. Smuggled in between the film’s visually imaginative gore and twisted sense of humour is an astute commentary on systemic inequality and corruption, using the prison setting and its ensemble of colourful characters as a microcosm of society at large – with a few dance battles thrown in for good measure.

#144故土 Fatherland🎬 LB 3.59 长片
2026 · 82 分钟 · 剧情、Historical · 主打佳片 · 维州首映 · 导演 Paweł Pawlikowski · 法国、德国、波兰、意大利
这是一部2026年法国、德国、波兰、意大利剧情、Historical长片。导演：Paweł Pawlikowski。MIFF 信息：主打佳片、维州首映。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、记忆与历史。
英文原文简介In 1949, ageing German Nobel laureate Thomas Mann breaks his long exile from his homeland to honour Johann Wolfgang von Goethe’s 200th anniversary in the latter’s birthplace of Frankfurt, West Germany. Next, he plans to visit the city where the literary giant died: Weimar, now in the communist East. Chauffeured by his resentful actor/writer daughter Erika, Thomas crosses a country he barely recognises, even as he waxes poetic about its heritage. Meanwhile, Erika notices in person – as her beloved, tormented brother Klaus does in his fiction – how two divergent but equally compromised regimes are being installed atop the still-festering wounds of Nazism. The country they grew up in is a fading memory; but can this intellectual family even feel at home with one another? Paweł Pawlikowski’s drama is the third in a thematic triptych of European postwar reverberations – filmed, like its predecessors Ida and Cold War (MIFF 2018), in luminous black-and-white. Pawlikowski’s immaculate road trip through Germany’s cultural crossroads follows a crisp yet elliptical map of details: disgusted looks at parties; silences in half-empty restaurants; dryly ironic new uses for old infrastructure. Meanwhile, the Manns’ repressed tensions emerge gradually in masterful lead performances by Hanns Zischler ( Kings of the Road , MIFF 1976) and Sandra Hüller ( Rose , MIFF 2026; Anatomy of a Fall , MIFF 2023), whose brilliantly understated turn as Erika captures a breadth of emotions lurking just below the surface.

英文原文简介Margot (Mara Taquin, Zero Fucks Given ) has worked hard to land her first job as a doctor in France’s most prestigious emergency department. But even in this life-and-death medical field, Charles Boyau Hospital is a brutal pressure cooker: the relentless competition among colleagues and merciless production-line pace set by her boss Hélène (Karin Viard, Polisse , MIFF 2011) have Margot so stressed that she’s literally sweating blood. She recalls treating similar unexplained symptoms in patients her own age: young professionals in French workplaces are brutally lashing out, seeming somehow to be … changing. Is this extreme burnout, a novel virus or a transformative environmental adaptation? Premiering in the Cannes Midnight Screenings section, Marion Le Corroller’s brash debut feature shares a blood type with her body- horreur compatriots Coralie Fargeat ( The Substance , MIFF 2024) and Julia Ducournau ( Titane , MIFF 2021). But Species delivers its critique of ‘rise-and-grind’ productivity culture with an axe, not a scalpel: every frame is a gonzo frenzy, captured expressionistically by cinematographer Guillaume Schiffman at tilted angles and through fish-eye lenses, all set to a pulsating electronic score by ROB. Imagine Philip Brophy’s Body Melt (MIFF 1994) infecting The Pitt and you might at least have the right genus … but Species is a breed all its own.

英文原文简介At the turn of 2021, 13 of the world’s 14 highest mountains had been summitted in winter. The exception? The second-highest mountain on Earth, K2, a notoriously perilous western Himalayan peak towering 8600 metres above sea level. In the northern winter of late 2020, in the depths of the COVID pandemic and with violent snowstorms on the way, Icelandic alpinist John Snorri Sigurjónsson and Pakistani father and son Ali and Sajid Sadpara – all veteran mountaineers – prepare their bid to enter the record books; without warning, they’re joined at base camp by throngs of others vying to be the first, including Nepalese mountaineering rock star Nirmal Purja and commercial climbing tourists of varying experience. As ego, capitalism and the deep scars of colonialism clash with ethics, physics and the indifference of howling winds and infinitesimally icy temperatures, the stage is set for an epic and catastrophic competition. Bringing together stunning big-screen visuals courtesy of influencer GoPros and professional film crews who accompanied the would-be summiteers, director Amir Bar-Lev ( Long Strange Trip , MIFF 2017) masterfully layers a gripping, heartbreaking and nuanced picture of the moral and philosophical conundrums at the heart of extreme achievement.

英文原文简介Jess (Judy Greer, Lemon , MIFF 2017), a lawyer in a nondescript Midwestern town, is struggling. Her problems seem to be solved when, at local fast food joint Blake Junior’s, she finds a finger in her chilli con carne bowl and a damage-controlling franchise executive offers her a $100,000 settlement on the spot. But when the restaurant’s owner and namesake (John Goodman) hears of the payout, he smells something fishy, and puts his shady yet trusted friend Dave (Bryan Cranston) on the case. Based (very loosely) on a true story that took place in California in 2005, this tar-black crime comedy evokes the early works of the Coen brothers but determinedly follows its own spicy path. Blessed with a cast of incredible character actors all having a ball, Chili Finger is headlined by an electric Greer. It all adds up to a wild, hilarious ride of bad decisions and worse consequences.

英文原文简介In a rural England somewhere between the late 19th century and a Technicolor dream, headstrong nature girl Hazel Woodus – played by a swooning, windswept Jennifer Jones ( The Song of Bernadette ) – lives a carefree existence communing with the animals and fairies of the untamed country. Like the foxes with whom she shares a spiritual kinship, Hazel finds herself hunted by both a dark, dashing squire (David Farrar, Black Narcissus ) and a straitlaced clergyman (Cyril Cusack), two men to whom she refuses to be shackled. Steeped in mysticism and eerie folklore – and serving as vivid inspiration for Kate Bush’s Hounds of Love – this expressionistic romance from the legendary Michael Powell and Emeric Pressburger ( The Red Shoes ; A Matter of Life and Death ) was the British filmmakers’ lone foray into Hollywood, in part due to co-producer (and Jones’s husband) David O. Selznick later bowdlerising the film for its US release as The Wild Heart . Presented here in its original version – and on a vibrant 35mm print, courtesy of Martin Scorsese’s personal collection – the film is a haunting tale of doomed love and the liberating power of nature, led by Jones’s foxy, ferocious performance.

Despite the press cycle’s familiar beats, epiphanies emerge from both the conversations and the reflective silences in between. The MIFF program would almost feel incomplete without a film from treasured festival fixture Hong Sang-soo, a master of minimalist, conversational works that mine true poetry from everyday exchanges. In his 34th feature – anchored by a beguiling turn from regular collaborator Song Seon-mi ( Walk Up , MIFF 2023) – Hong interrogates the various modes of performance: not only the craft of acting, but also the ways in which we modify our self-presentation for different contexts.

英文原文简介Edinburgh, 1810: wealthy aristocrat Lady Cumming Gordon arrives at a new girls’ boarding school, wishing to enrol her illegitimate teenage granddaughter Jane. When Jane – born to an Indian mother – is bullied by her peers for her dark skin, progressive teachers Miss Pirie and Miss Woods take her under their wings. But the close bond that develops leads to complicated feelings of jealousy, and a shift in the trio’s dynamic instigates an accusation by Jane that will alter the course of the teachers’ lives. This dramatisation of the true story that inspired Lillian Hellman's famous play The Children's Hour – which in turn was adapted into the 1961 William Wyler film of the same name starring Audrey Hepburn and Shirley MacLaine – deals frankly with the layers of intersectional power that impacted the real-life events behind it. Up-and-comer Mia Tharia (also starring in Taika Waititi’s upcoming adaptation of Kazuo Ishiguro’s Klara and the Sun ) gives a deftly nuanced performance as Jane, while Fiona Shaw is in typically fine form as the acerbic and haughty Lady Cumming Gordon. Aftersun (MIFF 2022) fans will also be delighted to spot Frankie Corio in a supporting role.

The Sun Never Sets marks the first full-length feature in nearly a decade by Joe Swanberg ( Drinking Buddies , MIFF 2013), an auteur who helped to forge the mumblecore lexicon – and launch the acting career of Greta Gerwig – with such heavily improvised and incredibly frank flicks as Hannah Takes the Stairs and Nights and Weekends . Now a political exile, she resides in the United States, while her parents still live in the house that she grew up in, which her architect father designed. Longing to somehow bridge the distance, Maryam – herself unseen in the film – has surveillance cameras installed in their home: together with super-8 home videos and archival materials, this dialogue-free footage of her ageing parents, moving around the house or at times performing for the camera, illustrates her reflective voiceover. Past Future Continuous , however, gradually reveals itself to be something more complex than straight documentary, provocatively slipping between historical fact and narrative fabrication – in the process, gesturing towards the tragic broader relevance of Maryam’s story of displacement to families in today’s Iran.

Newly arrived at HQ, Scottish meteorologist Captain James Stagg (Andrew Scott, Blue Moon , MIFF 2025) begs for a delay. His pioneering real-time weather observations are predicting heavy rain and high winds that will swamp boats or drive them calamitously off course. Ebullient US weatherman Irving P. Krick (Chris Messina, Call Jane , MIFF 2022), on the other hand, says Stagg’s just doomcasting, and that historical barometric charts indicate it’ll be positively balmy – which is just what arrogant British commander Bernard “Monty” Montgomery (Damian Lewis, Homeland ) wants to hear. Australian director Anthony Maras ( Hotel Mumbai ) dramatises this underappreciated historical turning point with moment-by-moment urgency, co-writing a grippingly cinematic adaptation of David Haig’s 2014 stage play. The always-subtle Scott mesmerises as a decent, plain-speaking expert caught up in the high pressure system of a long-planned military operation. Meanwhile, rain-soaked carnage on beach battlefields and weather-buffeted balloons over Newfoundland reveal the elemental, existential stakes compelling one man to dissuade his complacent colleagues from disaster.

Informed by her own experience of developing feelings for a chatbot, VCA grad Chouwa Liang’s jointly Australian-produced feature directorial debut expands her short documentary My AI Lover to offer a timely social portrait about technology, fantasy and connection. #157Shades of Silk🎬 LB 3.50 长片

英文原文简介Lysanne and Marlène (the latter played by writer/director Mary Stephen herself) were best friends in high school; perhaps, even then, their bond was underpinned by a desire for and fear of greater intimacy. Time has since separated the two women – both originally from Shanghai, Lysanne is now living in Paris and Marlène in Massachusetts, where she’s studying at Wellesley – but they pine for one another still, each in their own way and to tragic ends. Stephen’s darkly dreamy and remarkably assured debut – made when she was just 24 years old – was conceived as a loving counterpoint to Marguerite Duras’s India Song , with her similar cross-cultural narrative instead unfolding from an Asian woman’s perspective. For decades, the Hong Kong–born Stephen has primarily been known for her work as an editor, but the 2025 restoration of this 1978 treasure has stirred up overdue appreciation for her directorial oeuvre, spanning fiction and documentary and characterised by an exploration of colonial identity and cultural memory.

#158The Only Living Pickpocket in New York🎬 LB 3.50 长片
2025 · 88 分钟 · 剧情、犯罪 · 北美单元 · 维州首映 · 导演 Noah Segan · 美国
这是一部2025年美国剧情、犯罪长片。导演：Noah Segan。MIFF 信息：北美单元、维州首映。核心看点：家庭关系、成长与青春、悬疑 / 犯罪张力。
英文原文简介Harry is a veteran fingersmith with a heart of pilfered gold, and equally collegial relationships with his long-time fence Ben (Steve Buscemi) and NYPD detective Allan (Giancarlo Esposito). By day, he nimbly relieves unsuspecting New Yorkers of their valuables; by night, he cares for his ailing wife Rosie in their modest Bronx apartment. Fatefully, Harry picks the wrong mark: the random data card he’s swiped is a crypto wallet belonging to petulant crime family scion Dylan Diamond, whose goons threaten Rosie while Harry scours all five boroughs for the lost trinket. Can his bone-deep bond with his city survive the crude transactions of digital crime, or is New York about to have no living pickpockets? Actor-turned-director Noah Segan’s charming old-fashioned crime drama steals its vibe from the pockets of cinema’s 1970s and 1980s New York storytellers: the perfectly cast John Turturro roams the New York of John Cassavetes and Spike Lee, Robert Altman and Elaine May. The subtle, charismatic veteran of the screen owns this elegiac film, which doesn’t resist progress or ridicule digital natives but rather celebrates the evergreen value in human connections and well-honed skills.
Letterboxd 3.50/5；剧情、犯罪 / 北美单元 / 维州首映。推荐理由：家庭关系、成长与青春、悬疑 / 犯罪张力。奖项/展映线索：暂无明确获奖信息，主要按评分、题材和导演风格推荐
