#161I Shot Andy Warhol🎬 LB 3.48 长片
1996 · 103 分钟 · 剧情、喜剧、惊悚 · 经典修复 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Mary Harron · 美国
🏆 首映
英文原文In its Australian-premiering 4K restoration, Mary Harron’s fictionalised portrait of radical-feminist avenger Valerie Solanas still aims truly at manufactured cool and exploitative notoriety.
这是一部1996年美国剧情、喜剧、惊悚长片。导演：Mary Harron。MIFF 信息：经典修复、澳洲首映。核心看点：政治与社会现实、记忆与历史、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介On 3 June 1968, writer Valerie Solanas (Lili Taylor) walks into Andy Warhol’s Factory, points a handgun at the art superstar and fires three times. Previously, Valerie has been introduced – along with her notorious man-hating polemic, the SCUM Manifesto – to the Factory demimonde. She sees fellow iconoclasts; Warhol sees satirical performance art; Olympia Press publisher Maurice Girodias sees profitable controversy. But Valerie’s abusive past has made her both urgently ambitious and hyper-alert to exploitation, and she suspects that Girodias has been conspiring against her with Warhol – who becomes, in her eyes, a valid target for her rage. Many debates about gender and celebrity have raged since Mary Harron’s astonishing debut feature screened at MIFF 1996, but the complex agency the film grants its protagonist still blows most biopics away. Harron meticulously researched Warhol’s Factory in consultation with its key living figures; but rather than further mythologising its glamour, she emphasises the hollowness of its artifice – a theme she’d revisit in her stylish American Psycho (MIFF 2000). Featuring a score by avant-garde legend John Cale and a stunning cast including Jared Harris, Martha Plimpton and Michael Imperioli – as well as indie band Yo La Tengo standing in for The Velvet Underground – I Shot Andy Warhol returns after a long absence from screens as a vivid, timely provocation.

#162Rose of Nevada🎬 LB 3.48 长片

英文原文简介Thirty years ago, fishing trawler the Rose of Nevada vanished off the coast of Cornwall, taking its crew with it. Their village has been in decline ever since. When the boat suddenly reappears out of the fog one day, many townsfolk regard it as a good omen. A new crew is hired and heads out to sea. After a few days, they return with a full catch … but their home isn’t quite as they remember it. After the folk-horror stylings of Enys Men (MIFF 2022), Mark Jenkin’s Rose of Nevada returns audiences to the social realism of the Cornish fishing diaspora so evocatively portrayed in his debut Bait (MIFF 2019), albeit with a preternatural twist. Shooting in 16mm on vintage Bolex cameras, Jenkin uses visual and aural textures as storytelling devices, immersing viewers in deliberately uncanny realities and time loops. George MacKay and Callum Turner lend star power, but the film remains distinctly Jenkin’s vision: a cinematic artefact that looks like an oil painting come to life and unfolds like a 1970s ghost story.

#163Broken English🎬 LB 3.46 长片
2025 · 99 分钟 · 纪录片、音乐 · 音乐电影 · 维州首映 · 导演 Iain Forsyth, Jane Pollard · 英国
这是一部2025年英国纪录片、音乐长片。导演：Iain Forsyth, Jane Pollard。MIFF 信息：音乐电影、维州首映。核心看点：亲密关系、政治与社会现实、记忆与历史、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Plucked from obscurity by the manager of The Rolling Stones, Marianne Faithfull had her first hit in 1964 with ‘ As Tears Go By ’. She was 17. Hers would be a monumental career spanning six decades, punctuated by both high-profile love affairs and highly publicised struggles with drug abuse, anorexia and homelessness. But, for all its wealth of archival materials, Broken English is no conventional rock doc. Here, in a playful but sincere twist, the husky-voiced chanteuse is interviewed by a record keeper (George MacKay, Rose of Nevada , MIFF 2026) at the fictional Ministry of Not Forgetting – a bureaucratic institution overseen by none other than Tilda Swinton – while luminaries such as Courtney Love and Beth Orton chime in with their own reflections. Directors Iain Forsyth and Jane Pollard have specialised in immersive, form-defying documentaries built around musicians, from Nick Cave in 20,000 Days on Earth (MIFF 2014) to Emiliana Torrini in The Extraordinary Miss Flower (MIFF 2025). This inventive portrait of a legendary singer-songwriter is suffused with a particular, unanticipated pathos: Faithfull died in January 2025 while the film was still in production, making the rendition we see of her 2018 track ‘ Misunderstanding ’ – accompanied by Cave and Warren Ellis – her final recorded performance.

#164Knife: The Attempted Murder of Salman Rushdie🎬 LB 3.44 长片
2025 · 107 分钟 · 纪录片 · 纪录片单元 · 维州首映 · 导演 Alex Gibney · 美国
这是一部2025年美国纪录片长片。导演：Alex Gibney。MIFF 信息：纪录片单元、维州首映。核心看点：亲密关系、政治与社会现实、失去与哀悼、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介In 1989, an Iranian fatwa called for author Salman Rushdie’s death over his theologically provocative novel The Satanic Verses . Booksellers were firebombed and international publishers and translators attacked, even killed. Rushdie went into hiding … but his eventual assailant hadn’t yet been born. In 2022, with more than three decades having passed and the danger seemingly over, the 75-year-old author was speaking on exiled artists’ safety in a relaxed, informal event in upstate New York when a young Shia extremist invaded the stage and stabbed him repeatedly. Despite the horrendous, life-changing injuries he endured, Rushdie refused to become a tragic symbol of ideological violence. Now, doubling down on his commitment to free expression, he documents his own survival. Acclaimed documentarian Alex Gibney ( Zero Days , MIFF 2016) has profiled plenty of creative mavericks, political dissidents and repressive institutions. Here, he allows his subject’s clever, poetic voice to lead an unexpectedly meditative and allusive film that offers deep archival context for the home-video footage of the attack’s aftermath and the arduous recovery that followed, captured with unflinching love by the author’s poet wife Rachel Eliza Griffiths. Physically weakened and spiritually fragile, Rushdie nonetheless takes back his narrative, showing that resistance against authoritarian censorship is sharpened by wit, imagination and a defiantly imperfect humanity.

#165Fantasma🎬 LB 3.43 长片
2006 · 63 分钟 · 剧情 · Lisandro Alonso · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Lisandro Alonso · 阿根廷
这是一部2006年阿根廷剧情长片。导演：Lisandro Alonso。MIFF 信息：Lisandro Alonso、澳洲首映。核心看点：悬疑 / 犯罪张力、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Argentino Vargas, the star of Los muertos , has arrived in Buenos Aires to attend a retrospective screening of the film at the grand Teatro General San Martín. Out of place and uneasy in the city, he soon gets lost within the cinema — a movie palace that, having fallen into disarray, is full of shadows and secrets. As he drifts through the labyrinthine building, he crosses paths with Misael Saavedra, the central figure of La libertad . Here, the two solitary subjects at the centre of Lisandro Alonso’s first two films are together yet apart, unable to find their place within the cinema. Alonso calls his first three movies his ‘Lonely Men Trilogy’. Inspired by Tsai Ming-liang’s Goodbye, Dragon Inn (MIFF 2004), this unifying conclusion to the triptych is a self-reflexive exploration of the filmmaker’s own work, and particularly on how he took these rural non-actors and turned them into cinematic subjects. With little dialogue or narrative, Fantasma is built from evocative tracking shots and ultra-detailed sound design, full of strange elements such as the unexplained presence of a barking dog. As always, there is mystery in the film’s intention and its title. Is this a portrait of being haunted by the spectre of cinema itself? Or are each of these lonely men lost spirits, fated to forever live on in Alonso’s movies?

Dr Lisa Jones-Engel is a passionate primatologist who reflects, with a mix of sadness and horror, on her past work at the Laboratory for Experimental Medicine and Surgery in Primates. It was enough to turn her from animal tester to animal welfare advocate, as contemporary and archival footage – both personal and professional – relates. Through the perspectives of other frontline scientists discussing the fraught balance of human needs and animal rights, one compelling fact emerges: animal testing does psychological harm not just to its physical victims, but also to its human practitioners.

When her dad, Count Dracula, dies from a nasty case of stake-in-the-heart, Nadja finally has a chance to emerge from her father’s long, overbearing shadow. But before she can make a fresh start, a twist of fate romantically entangles Nadja with Lucy – an extended relative of her father’s murderer, Van Helsing. Owing as much to André Breton’s 1928 novel of the same name as it does to 1936 horror classic Dracula’s Daughter, this magnetically cool black comedy by Michael Almereyda ( Marjorie Prime , MIFF 2017) is shot on luminous monochrome 35mm with shimmering vampire POV sequences captured by a toy Pixelvision camcorder. The soundtrack, featuring My Bloody Valentine, Portishead and The Verve, is an education in 90s shoegaze; while the cast includes Hal Hartley regulars Elina Löwensohn and Martin Donovan, Peter Fonda as Van Helsing, and even the late, great David Lynch (one of the film’s key financiers) making a cameo as a morgue attendant, naturally.

Beneath its charm and whimsy, Bell, Book and Candle offers a sly meditation on conformity, desire and the vulnerability required to truly connect with another person.

One evening, she meets Mitsutsuka, a soft-spoken physics lecturer who’s just as reticent and fastidious as she is. Soon, they start taking walks together, sitting in cafés and talking the night away – two lonely satellites briefly, tenderly brought into shared orbit. But can their relationship survive the cold light of day? Adapting the book of the same name by Mieko Kawakami (author of the hit novel Breasts and Eggs ), Yukiko Sode takes on a gentle, beautiful story grounded in interior experience, delicately hinting at the difficulty of connecting with others – and the preciousness of the rare moments when it occurs. Starring prolific big- and small-screen Japanese actors Yukino Kishii and Tadanobu Asano (here taking on a relatively subdued role), this lovely two-hander is a film that dwells on conversation and the spaces lurking between the words we say to one another.

#175The Enchantment of the Blue Sailors🎬 LB 3.40 长片
1975 · 49 分钟 · 实验 · Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels · 导演 Ulrike Ottinger · West Germany
这是一部1975年West Germany实验长片。导演：Ulrike Ottinger。MIFF 信息：Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels。核心看点：导演表达与人物处境。
英文原文简介An exotic sea laps upon the sands of a distant beach, and a woman in an extravagant red gown and matching headdress crosses the dunes, singing. Gay sailors in classic white-and-blue uniforms kiss (years before French artists Pierre et Gilles made such imagery iconic). A woman in a leopard-print party dress fringed with pink, cake-like layers settles in for a solo picnic, while another woman in full-feathered bird regalia prowls nearby, her tinselled wings shimmering in the light. Scantily clad characters cavort and canoodle with bacchanalian pleasure. An assemblage of vivid imagery, The Enchantment of the Blue Sailors was Ulrike Ottinger’s second mid-length experimental film, following Laocoon & Sons: The Story of the Transformation of Esmeralda del Rio (1972/73), and her first in riotous colour. Notably, it is the only work in Ottinger’s filmography that she shares a directorial credit on: joining her at the helm here is her partner and frequent collaborator Tabea Blumenschein, who also oversaw the film’s costumes and make-up. Both women appear onscreen, with Ottinger playing the “Nymph of German Romanticism” alongside influential queer filmmaker Rosa von Praunheim ( It Is Not the Homosexual Who Is Perverse, but the Society in Which He Lives ) as one of the titular sailors.

英文原文简介After her husband unceremoniously leaves her one morning, Zee heads out to wander the streets of the Upper West Side in a daze, muttering to herself about what she could have done differently. When she stops at Café Central to eat her feelings with a big bowl of chocolate ice cream, Zee’s loud sobs are noticed by Eli, a fellow divorcee, sitting at the next table. Before long, the two strangers develop a distinctly neurotic New York–style case of amour fou , philosophising, bickering and engaging in a courtship characterised by acts of mutual wallowing. This dryly funny romance from iconoclastic American independent filmmaker Henry Jaglom (who died just last September) is an invaluable time capsule of 1980s New York. Filmed on the streets among real pedestrians, its freewheeling style lends the film a refreshing spontaneity, enhanced by the wonderfully quirky central performances by Karen Black ( Five Easy Pieces ) and the director’s brother Michael Emil ( Insignificance , MIFF 1985), as well as memorable cameos from Carol Kane, a young Larry David and Orson Welles – Jaglom’s friend and business partner – as a movie magician.

While investigating, he hooks up with hot bartender and sex worker Cody (Tom Rodgers) – a chance encounter that also gets him embroiled in the machinations of drag mob boss Fat Frankie (Paul Capsis, Head On , MIFF 1998). Caught up in drug deals, shootouts, a deadly heist and more, Aiden must find a way out before he loses himself in this sinister web. Lastly, amid the Amazon gold rush of 1970s Brazil, two young men from a remote tribe fight over a girl – and one of them ends up dead. Courtesy of an inner demon she calls “Fred”, the impulsive carnage that’s always followed in Winifred’s wake doesn’t take long to pop up gruesomely again. Given the Poundses’ own depraved lineage, has Winifred finally found her people? What are they learning from their super-callous, pugilistic, exterminatory governess?

#184Madame X: An Absolute Ruler🎬 LB 3.29 长片
1977 · 145 分钟 · 剧情、实验、奇幻 · Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels · 导演 Ulrike Ottinger · West Germany
这是一部1977年West Germany剧情、实验、奇幻长片。导演：Ulrike Ottinger。MIFF 信息：Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels。核心看点：亲密关系。
英文原文简介The most successful and cruellest pirate on the Far Eastern Seas, Madame X (Tabea Blumenschein) rules her junk Orlando with a gloved iron fist from which extends a long spike, having lost her real hand to a deadly jellyfish years ago while attempting to save her lover (played by Ulrike Ottinger herself in flashback). Now in desire of “total domination”, she sends out a signal to women across the globe – including an Australian bush pilot with a wildly shorn haircut and Yvonne Rainer in a green visor and rollerskates – inviting them to join her for a life of excitement. Journeying from all corners, they leave their ordinary lives behind in search of something new; but no-one expects the tyranny that awaits. Shot on 16mm, Ottinger’s first scripted feature is a swashbuckling sadomasochistic reverie that caused much controversy for its brightly coloured, often humorous, depictions of queer violence. With its fetishistic costuming designed by Blumenschein (the director’s romantic partner and collaborator at the time) and wild aesthetic, Madame X was a call to arms for a new avant-garde; yet it still pays homage to its queer predecessors, with references to Virginia Woolf and a Sapphic take on the Shangri-Las’ 1964 pop hit ‘Leader of the Pack’ .

#188Aro berria🎬 LB 3.07 长片
2025 · 102 分钟 · 剧情、实验 · 实验影像 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Irati Gorostidi Agirretxe · 西班牙
这是一部2025年西班牙剧情、实验长片。导演：Irati Gorostidi Agirretxe。MIFF 信息：实验影像、澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、失去与哀悼、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介It’s 1978, and Spanish society is struggling to find a post-dictatorship identity in the wake of Franco’s death. A host of activist workers from a Basque factory, disillusioned by the seeming inevitability of capitalism, attempt a complete rebellion, setting out to join a commune in rural Navarre. Eme (played by a magnetic Maite Mugerza Ronse) wants to believe that Arco Iris offers a new way of living, but she soon learns it’s just as political as a picket line: the commune is riddled with personality clashes and ideological disagreements, and its sexual practices are underpinned by patriarchal power imbalances. Despite what the thousands of pilgrims who flock to its large-scale spiritual rituals might think, this rainbow family isn’t particularly harmonious. Irati Gorostidi Agirretxe has been building to this debut feature through her short films, chronicling life within an intentional community in both documentary (2021’s San Simón 62 ) and fiction (2023’s Contadores ). The connection is personal: Gorostidi Agirretxe’s own parents lived in a new-age commune before she was born. Boasting a wryly comic cameo from the charismatic Oliver Laxe (director of MIFF 2025 stand-out Sirāt ) as a seedy tantric sex guru, her debut feature is a slippery film sitting at the intersection of sincerity and scepticism. Evoking both the daily routines of Direct Action (MIFF 2024) and the ecstatic rituals of The Testament of Ann Lee , Aro berria introduces a vital new voice in Basque cinema.

#190Nagi Notes🎬 LB 3.06 长片
2026 · 110 分钟 · 剧情 · 亚太单元 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Koji Fukada · 日本、菲律宾、法国、新加坡
这是一部2026年日本、菲律宾、法国、新加坡剧情长片。导演：Koji Fukada。MIFF 信息：亚太单元、澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、亲密关系、音乐与表演。
英文原文简介Yuri, an architect from Tokyo, arrives in regional Nagi, a small town that’s home to both a magnificent art museum and an active military base. She’s there to visit her ex-husband’s sister, Yoriko, a sculptor who wants Yuri to sit for her. Staging sessions in a workshop barn on her dairy farm, Yoriko chips away at a block of camphorwood and at Yuri’s guardedness, their conversation turning personal. Two boys who attend Yoriko’s art classes and workshops, Keita and Haruki, are fascinated by this outsider, unsure of what the relationship between the two women is. As the quartet try to make sense of one another, much is left unsaid. Reminiscent of the films of Éric Rohmer and Ryusuke Hamaguchi ( All of a Sudden , MIFF 2026), and having earnt comparisons to Kelly Reichardt’s Showing Up (MIFF 2023) for its gentle depiction of artistry, this latest work from Koji Fukada ( Harmonium , MIFF 2016) adapts Oriza Hirata’s 1994 theatrical production Tokyo Notes (which itself drew from Yasujirō Ozu’s masterpiece Tokyo Story , MIFF 2016). Nagi Notes is a keenly observed character study with no real explosions – save for the sound of military munitions drills that periodically ring out through the town. Pondering the nature of creativity, queer identity and the challenges of finding belonging amid the social strictures of Japanese society, this is a thoughtful, low-key conversation piece that’s perfect for those who like their dramas intimate and deeply human.
Letterboxd 3.06/5；剧情 / 亚太单元 / 澳洲首映。推荐理由：家庭关系、亲密关系、音乐与表演。奖项/展映线索：暂无明确获奖信息，主要按评分、题材和导演风格推荐

#191The Legend of Lylah Clare🎬 LB 3.14 长片
1968 · 130 分钟 · 剧情 · Kim Novak: Hollywood Heretic · 导演 Robert Aldrich · 美国
这是一部1968年美国剧情长片。导演：Robert Aldrich。MIFF 信息：Kim Novak: Hollywood Heretic。核心看点：失去与哀悼、悬疑 / 犯罪张力。
英文原文简介Lylah Clare is a mythical movie star whose death has long been shrouded in mystery. When unknown ingenue Elsa Brinkman (Kim Novak) is cast in the principal role in a biopic about the doomed thespian, she is almost immediately seduced by the heady Hollywood lifestyle, not to mention by tyrannical director Lewis Zarken (Peter Finch, Network ); she quickly assumes Lylah’s previous status on his arm, in his film and in his bed. Soon, the lines between reality and delusion begin to blur: the spirit of Lylah herself lays claim to Elsa, at times taking hold just long enough to deliver blistering take-downs of her adversaries. With echoes of her iconic role in Vertigo and references to her own transformation at the behest of Columbia Pictures head Harry Cohn, she plays the role with trademark empathy while embracing the inspired chaos of the piece. Robert Aldrich ( Kiss Me Deadly , MIFF 1998) directs with feverish intensity, transforming sound stages, mirrors and camera lenses into sites of psychological entrapment, while Novak delivers a haunting dual performance that blends innocence (quickly lost) and bravado. The Legend of Lylah Clare remains a savage, self-reflexive meditation on Hollywood’s capacity to consume the women it immortalises. Largely dismissed on release, it has since been reclaimed as a camp cult classic.

英文原文简介As the world faces a probable super El Niño event in 2026/27, with wildfire conditions that may exceed those of 2019/20, picturing these unprecedented fires defies imagination. Using the latest scientific data, a custom machine-learning model and the Unreal Engine 3D-creation platform, Firestorm allows audiences to visualise historical Australian bushfires and then interactively adjust weather conditions to see how they would dramatically change under escalating global warming scenarios. Presented at the VCA, University of Melbourne, in a world-first conversion of an LED volume into a stereoscopic cinema, Firestorm fully immerses audiences in a panoramic fire landscape, allowing them to viscerally experience the look and feel of these possible futures firsthand.

Meanwhile, Vénéranda has just learned with dismay that her daughter Tina is unexpectedly pregnant, news that complicates her commitment to healing and deepens her own reckoning with the past. A decade in the making, Marie-Clémentine Dusabejambo’s debut film is a humanist portrait of the legacy of genocide and the challenges of reconciliation. Working largely with non-professional actors and drawing deeply from interviews with victims and recorded Gacaca testimonies, it deftly evokes the difficulty of moving on as individuals and communities. Blessed with an incandescent turn from Isabelle Kabano as the seething Suzanne, this is a profoundly intimate story of a nation still reckoning with its past

#204Rehearsals for a RevolutionLB N/A 长片
2026 · 95 分钟 · 纪录片 · 纪录片单元 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Pegah Ahangarani · 西班牙、Czechia
🏆 获奖、戛纳
英文原文Receiving the highest documentary prize at Cannes, this inspired essay movie channels the tumult of Iranian history into a personal account of loss. | Winning the 2026 L’Œil d’or at Cannes, this documentary vividly interrogates what it means – and costs – to resist.
这是一部2026年西班牙、Czechia纪录片长片。导演：Pegah Ahangarani。MIFF 信息：纪录片单元、澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、记忆与历史、失去与哀悼、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Living in exile in the UK, actor/director Pegah Ahangarani ( I Am Trying to Remember , MIFF 2022) wants to make a film about Iranian history, as a way to understand how the country ended up where it is today. Fashioning home movies, archival imagery, news footage, animated sequences and sobering statistics into a singular cinematic essay, she chronicles conflict and rebellion across the decades, from 1979’s Islamic Revolution to the 2026 massacre of protesters and war with Israel and the United States. Ahangarani stages this history lesson in five chapters, each dedicated to a friend or family member she lost along the way, poignantly situating her film at the intersection of the personal and the political. Born in 1984 to filmmakers Manijeh Hekmat ( Bandar Band , MIFF 2021) and Jamshid Ahangarani, Pegah Ahangarani grew up intertwined with cinema and the post-revolution history of her homeland. Rehearsals for a Revolution is steeped in both, drawing on clips from her father’s old movies and mobile phone footage captured on the front lines of the 2009 Green Wave protests; but it also dwells in the here and now, intimately capturing scenes from Ahangarani’s current life in London with her newborn daughter. Winning the 2026 L’Œil d’or at Cannes, this documentary vividly interrogates what it means – and costs – to resist.

🏆 获奖、圣丹斯、首映
英文原文Both a charismatic hangout movie and a courageous act of dissent, this Sundance winner spends quality time with two young women trying to make art in Iran. | Shot in secret and smuggled out of Iran to make its Sundance premiere, the film went on to receive the festival’s U.S.
这是一部2026年美国、伊朗剧情长片。导演：Hossein Keshavarz, Maryam Ataei。MIFF 信息：新锐视野、澳洲首映。核心看点：政治与社会现实、音乐与表演。
英文原文简介Hanna (Hana Mana) is a contemporary dancer who posts videos of her work online, while playwright Pari (Mahshad Bahram) stages experimental theatre productions. In Iran, both of these acts are illegal. Thick-as-thieves besties and housemates who participate in Tehran’s underground art communities, they live their lives – as artists, feminists and unwed women – in defiance of an authoritarian government that is openly hostile to everything they do. Armed with their friendship, their ideologies and a serious streak of rebellion, Hanna and Pari try to make art and make it through another day. Nearly four decades after Iranian cinema legend Abbas Kiarostami’s breakout 1987 film posed the eternal question Where Is the Friend’s House? , Hossein Keshavarz and Maryam Ataei deliver a playful answer. Inspired by classic Iranian art movies, Jean-Luc Godard’s political films of the 1960s and the US indie mumblecore movement, The Friend’s House Is Here is a movie about how to live your best, most creative life under a repressive regime. Shot in secret and smuggled out of Iran to make its Sundance premiere, the film went on to receive the festival’s U.S. Dramatic Special Jury Award for Ensemble Cast – a just reward for the non-professional actors (many themselves working artists) who appear in this film.

#206律法 TilaïLB N/A 长片
1990 · 81 分钟 · 剧情 · 经典修复 · 国际首映 · 导演 Idrissa Ouedraogo · Burkina Faso

英文原文An adulterous love affair brings tragedy to a traditional village in Burkina Faso in Idrissa Ouedraogo’s masterful, Cannes-awarded fable, now restored in 4K. | Having originally screened in 1990 at both MIFF and Cannes, where it shared the Grand Jury Prize, Tilaï returns newly restored, its modernist take on a story steeped in patriarchal traditi...
这是一部1990年Burkina Faso剧情长片。导演：Idrissa Ouedraogo。MIFF 信息：经典修复、国际首映。核心看点：家庭关系、亲密关系、政治与社会现实。
英文原文简介When Saga returns home after an absence of two years, he’s dismayed to learn that his fiancée, Nogma, has married someone else – his father. Her feelings for Saga haven’t waned, she reassures him, but she had no choice in the matter. Reunited, they find temptation too great to resist: in the straw hut where Saga is staying, just outside the village, he and his would-have-been bride discreetly consummate their courtship. But this transgression is discovered – per tribal law, treated as not just adultery but also incest – fracturing both family bonds and the broader community. Like Idrissa Ouedraogo’s two earlier features, Yam Daabo and Yaaba (MIFF 1990), Tilaï features non-professional actors selected from among his family and friends; the film also offers a potent distillation of complex social dynamics set against a backdrop of expansive plains – the filmmaker’s native lands looming mythically in stark compositions – and ancient moral codes. Having originally screened in 1990 at both MIFF and Cannes, where it shared the Grand Jury Prize, Tilaï returns newly restored, its modernist take on a story steeped in patriarchal tradition as striking today as it was decades ago.
暂无 Letterboxd 评分；剧情 / 经典修复 / 国际首映。推荐理由：家庭关系、亲密关系、政治与社会现实。奖项/展映线索：评审团奖、获奖、戛纳

英文原文简介In Lebanon’s Bekaa Valley, Bedouin tribes still live according to the dictates of ancient customs, even as Israeli missile strikes sound in the distance and civil war in Syria lurks just over the mountains. The connection to family, culture and land is strong, but – despite the open expanses of valley surrounding them – can often feel oppressive for the women of this community. Shot without a script and performed by a non-professional cast, Palestinian filmmaker Rakan Mayasi’s Cannes-premiering first feature follows a run of acclaimed shorts (including the award-winning Trumpets in the Sky , MIFF 2022) and training from global cinema titans Abbas Kiarostami and Béla Tarr. In Yesterday the Eye Didn’t Sleep , Mayasi draws from his own grandmother’s accounts of being forced into marriage at just 14 to document and interrogate tribal custom, ritual and entrenched patriarchy. Showcasing sublime photography and thrumming with political subtext, this evocative work shows a filmmaker engaged with both landscape and people, alive to a sense of place and the interior lives of those who dwell there.

Their accidentally avant-garde album made its way onto the internet, however, where it developed a life of its own. Two decades later, having long since settled into the routines and responsibilities of work and family, the now-adult quartet were astonished to find that their childhood experiment had developed a fan base on music forums – and, inspired by the discovery, set to work rekindling their friendship and creating new music together. Winning the Grand Jury Award in SXSW’s Documentary Feature Competition, Ayden Mayeri’s autobiographical documentary doesn’t merely settle for Y2K nostalgia or outsider-music obsessions; rather, it’s an unexpectedly honest, introspective tale about four women reconnecting with fearless creativity and reckoning with their most authentic selves.

Boosted by a game cast including acclaimed stand-up Ivan Aristeguieta, up-and-coming comic performer Florence Noble, and veteran character actors David Fane ( Eagle vs Shark , MIFF 2007) and Francis Greenslade, Yesterday Island is a film you’ll want to revisit over and over again.

For this special presentation, Michael “CAVS” Cavanagh of King Gizzard & the Lizard Wizard reimagines the film with an all-new live score, performing solo across multiple drum kits and a suite of electronic instruments. Part film screening, part live concert, Hear My Eyes has spent over a decade creating immersive cinema experiences, building a loyal following through collaborations including Terminator 2: Judgment Day with Peter Van Hoesen and Robin Fox, Chopper with Springtime and Mick Harvey, Wake in Fright with Surprise Chef, and Pan’s Labyrinth with Sleep D. For Nolan devotees and anyone who loves cinema that takes risks, this is a chance to revisit a cult classic, live and reimagined.

这是一部2025年美国纪录片长片。导演：Robert Gordon。MIFF 信息：音乐电影。核心看点：政治与社会现实、记忆与历史、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介There are many interpretations of the heckling at the Newport Folk Festival that accompanied Bob Dylan plugging in for the first time, but one thing remains clear: it represented a key turning point in the history of American music. In Newport & the Great Folk Dream, that moment is treated as a starting point for investigating the broader phenomenon of Newport, and how the countercultural event became one of the most iconic of its kind. Mining the archives of previously unseen footage shot over four successive years by Murray Lerner for his 1967 Oscar-nominated documentary Festival, director Robert Gordon (Best of Enemies, MIFF 2015) has assembled an ecstatic account of the Newport Folk Festival in its formative years. Featuring illuminating performances from Johnny Cash, Joan Baez, John Lee Hooker, Muddy Waters, Howlin’ Wolf, Taj Mahal, Buffy Sainte-Marie, The Staple Singers and many others, alongside contemporary interviews with those who were there, it’s a historical document par excellence. Placing this precious footage within its social and political context, Newport & the Great Folk Dream is an extraordinarily raw and energising music documentary.
暂无 Letterboxd 评分；纪录片 / 音乐电影。推荐理由：政治与社会现实、记忆与历史、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。奖项/展映线索：提名

#221A to ALB N/A 短片

英文原文Winner of a short film award at the 2011 Viennale.

英文原文简介Demonstrating the playful qualities that once saw him dubbed the enfant terrible of experimental film, Johann Lurf filmed this absurdist 2011 short from a sputtering Vespa as it circled – and circled and circled and circled – 100 different roundabouts in his homeland, Austria. Full of mediocre landscapes, shoddy architecture and novelty sculpture, it’s an endearing homage to human achievement at its least wondrous. Winner of a short film award at the 2011 Viennale.

#229The Airport ChaplainLB N/A
2026 · 75 分钟 · 澳洲电影 · 世界首映 · 导演 Bonnie Moir · 澳大利亚
🏆 获奖
英文原文Multi-award-winning screenwriter Elise McCredie ( Stateless ; Ride Like a Girl ) based this much-anticipated new drama series, commissioned b...
这是一部2026年澳大利亚影片。导演：Bonnie Moir。MIFF 信息：澳洲电影、世界首映。核心看点：政治与社会现实、记忆与历史、失去与哀悼、恐怖 / 超自然。
英文原文简介At a bustling international airport, lost people seek missed connections, while others carry heavy personal baggage. Tobias Wallace (Hugo Weaving, The Rooster , MIFF 2023) shepherds them all. Scruffy and benevolent in his hi-vis “Chaplain”-printed vest and always on call, he’ll bend rules to help passengers and workers alike – that includes Asha, a young woman hiding in the prayer room whose murky history stirs Tobias’s own deeply buried traumas. Not everybody is a fan of his methods, however: ambitious new terminal manager Mira (Shabana Azeez, The Pitt ; Lesbian Space Princess , MIFF 2025) has liability nightmare Tobias marked for redundancy. But as crises appear everywhere – overworked baggage handlers, security breaches, families torn apart and grief-stricken relatives – maybe this infuriating chaplain could be Mira’s salvation. Multi-award-winning screenwriter Elise McCredie ( Stateless ; Ride Like a Girl ) based this much-anticipated new drama series, commissioned by SBS, on co-creator and Wooden Horse producer Jude Troy’s ( The Clearing ) encounter with a Melbourne Airport chaplain who helped her recover a lost handbag – and her identity. In this world premiere of the first three episodes, director Bonnie Moir ( Not Dark Yet , MIFF 2022) warmly illuminates a morally complex protagonist, while his multicultural, multigenerational co-workers are portrayed by a fully booked flight of Aussie talent, from screen legend Claudia Karvan ( Bump ; The Big Steal , MIFF 2017) and Thomas Weatherall ( Heartbreak High ; Narrow Road to the Deep North ) to Kavitha Anandasivam ( The Hunting ) and Erroll Shand ( Wolfram ).
暂无 Letterboxd 评分；澳洲电影 / 世界首映。推荐理由：政治与社会现实、记忆与历史、失去与哀悼、恐怖 / 超自然。奖项/展映线索：获奖

#236FilipiñanaLB N/A 长片
2026 · 100 分钟 · 剧情 · 亚太单元 · 维州首映 · 导演 Rafael Manuel · 菲律宾
🏆 获奖、圣丹斯
英文原文In this Sundance-lauded debut, a young Filipina learns that subjugation and silence are par for the course at the golf club where she finds employment. | Executive-produced by Jia Zhang-ke and receiving a Special Jury Award at Sundance, Rafael Manuel’s scathing and contemplative feature debut escalates with menace despite its languid, sun-drenched set...
这是一部2026年菲律宾剧情长片。导演：Rafael Manuel。MIFF 信息：亚太单元、维州首映。核心看点：政治与社会现实、音乐与表演。
英文原文简介Having left rural Ilocos for Manila’s greener pastures, 17-year-old Isabel ends up on a different kind of green: working as a ‘tee girl’ for a country club. She quickly adopts a new routine teeing up balls for wealthy golfers, joining the staff to eat morsels of rice and fish while the clientele feast, and gradually growing infatuated with the wealthy doctor who runs the club. But as she discovers more about her patron and the institution to which he owes his fortune, Isabel finds herself drawn into a web of exploitation, displacement and unseen, sanitised violence. Executive-produced by Jia Zhang-ke and receiving a Special Jury Award at Sundance, Rafael Manuel’s scathing and contemplative feature debut escalates with menace despite its languid, sun-drenched setting, whose sheen conceals the gendered dynamics of power and how the extremely rich prey on the aspirational poor. Supported by Filipino screen mavens Angeli Bayani ( Ilo Ilo , MIFF 2013) and Ruby Ruiz ( First Light , MIFF 2025), Jorrybell Agoto lends an unsettled defiance to her portrayal of Isabel, propelling a sly satire of oppression entrenched through polished appearances.
暂无 Letterboxd 评分；剧情 / 亚太单元 / 维州首映。推荐理由：政治与社会现实、音乐与表演。奖项/展映线索：获奖、圣丹斯

MIFF 信息：对谈活动。核心看点：亲密关系、政治与社会现实、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介To celebrate the work of screen icon Kim Novak and the six films screening in the Kim Novak: Hollywood Heretic strand, the panel will share some of their personal favourite performances and iconic moments from her life through clips and commentary. They’ll also look back at her storied career, diving into her early appearance in The Man With the Golden Arm , legendary performances in Vertigo and Bell, Book and Candle opposite James Stewart in the same year, through to lesser-known but no less stunning roles in Middle of the Night , Strangers When We Meet and The Legend of Lylah Clare . They’ll look at the struggles Novak faced coming up in the studio system: fighting to keep her name, protesting at being underpaid, her position among peers and her uneasy relationship with her craft. Come learn about her filmography before meeting the woman herself in the documentary Kim Novak’s Vertigo . Kate Fitzpatrick is a film programmer and general doer of no good. At MIFF, she programs new features, retrospectives and XR, and curates the MIFF Schools section of the program.

#238Kings of VeniceLB N/A 长片
2026 · 95 分钟 · 纪录片 · 纪录片单元 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 S.D. Saltarelli, Sveinn Ingimundarson · 美国
🏆 威尼斯
英文原文Amid all the colour and chaos of Venice Beach, (ultra-)competitive paddle tennis players are a band apart. | In the Los Angeles neighbourhood of Venice Beach, 11 paddle tennis courts are under threat from an encroaching enemy: pickleball.
这是一部2026年美国纪录片长片。导演：S.D. Saltarelli, Sveinn Ingimundarson。MIFF 信息：纪录片单元、澳洲首映。核心看点：政治与社会现实、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介In the Los Angeles neighbourhood of Venice Beach, 11 paddle tennis courts are under threat from an encroaching enemy: pickleball. The hugely popular monolith, like some ruthless developer, is taking up increasing space in its expansion, threatening to wipe out a small community playing an exceedingly similar sport. From Scott, the self-described GOAT of paddle tennis, to hot-tempered Italian model Ernesto, these misfits unite to stage a paddlers vs pickleballers tournament. Winner gets $50,000 – and the right to control these courts. “The Venice Beach paddle tennis world is sort of like a back-alley fistfight,” says one of the oddballs in this quirky, captivating doc. Chronicling a subculture, those who inhabit it and their sporting passions, it’s surely MIFF 2026’s only film to feature a scene where the cops get called on people for yelling at pickleballers. Having enthralled festival-goers at DOC NYC and Slamdance (where it won the Audience Award for Documentary Feature), Kings of Venice is a crowdpleasing delight: a serve of outsized personalities that wouldn’t be out of place in a Christopher Guest comedy.

#240Viva CarmenLB N/A 长片
2026 · 90 分钟 · 动画 · 动画单元 · 维州首映 · 导演 Sébastien Laudenbach · 法国
🏆 戛纳
英文原文This painterly, profound adaptation of Georges Bizet’s iconic opera – told from the perspective of children – wowed Cannes crowds with its incredible use of colour.
这是一部2026年法国动画长片。导演：Sébastien Laudenbach。MIFF 信息：动画单元、维州首映。核心看点：亲密关系、失去与哀悼。
英文原文简介Salva (voiced by Milo Machado-Graner, Goodbye, Cruel World , MIFF 2026), Belén, Piranha and La Bola are street kids scrapping for survival on the streets of 19th-century Seville. Salva works for the blind knife grinder Antonio, who foretells a mystical prophecy of the death of free-spirited young Romani woman Carmen, who will be killed by the soldier who loves her. When Salva leaps into action in the hope of saving Carmen from her fate, his actions instead set the prophesy into motion. From Jacques Feyder’s Carmen (MIFF 1981) and Jean-Luc Godard’s Prénom Carmen (MIFF 1985) through to Mark Dornford-May’s U-Carmen eKhayelitsha (MIFF 2005), Georges Bizet’s iconic opera has proved a fertile text for cinematic adaptations. Animator Sébastien Laudenbach ( The Girl Without Hands , MIFF 2016) offers a unique take on the classic text, turning the narrative away from the star-cross’d lovers at the centre of its tragedy and instead presenting it from the perspective of children watching fate unfold. Filled with expressive lines and evocative colours, this gorgeously hand-painted work is a sheer delight for those who treasure the animated artform.

But Mitchell’s fluid portrayal of love and identity remains a life-changing cult classic because it defiantly troubles categories of drag and trans, nonbinarity and androgyny.

这是一部2026年美国纪录片长片。导演：Amy Jenkins。MIFF 信息：纪录片单元、维州首映。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Adam Sieswerda always knew he was a boy, but the aspiring singer-songwriter feared his artistic prospects because he also knew his voice wouldn’t drop. At 15, with support from his parents, he received his first testosterone shot – and so began Adam’s journey to becoming his true self. As he embraces his growing identity as a fledgling young adult male, his mother, filmmaker Amy Jenkins, documents various milestones – psychologist appointments, university applications, a ‘boob funeral’ – with both curiosity and compassion. Screening at SXSW and CPH:DOX, Jenkins’s eight-years-in-the-making film chronicles Adam’s transformative experiences of gender-affirming care while giving glimpses into the logistical, physiological and emotional demands of the process. At times, she even lets Adam take the reins – her handheld footage and archival clips interwoven with his smartphone videos – lending further intimacy to a film already brimming with energetic honesty. Amid the threats to trans rights in their home country and around the world, Adam’s Apple is an urgent and undeniably touching testament to familial solidarity and trans affirmation.

#250Aniki-BóbóLB N/A 长片
1942 · 72 分钟 · 剧情 · 经典修复 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Manoel de Oliveira · 葡萄牙
这是一部1942年葡萄牙剧情长片。导演：Manoel de Oliveira。MIFF 信息：经典修复、澳洲首映。核心看点：导演表达与人物处境。
英文原文简介Young Carlitos’s heart beats a little faster for Terezinha; so does Eduardo’s. Terezinha, for her part, has eyes mainly for a doll in the window display of a shop, the latter of which has the tantalising and lightly ominous name Temptations. Hoping to win his crush’s admiration, Carlitos swipes the doll for her – and, in doing so, introduces a new tension and moral murkiness into the lives of this gang of Porto urchins. Working from a short story by José Joaquim Rodrigues de Freitas, Portuguese director Manoel de Oliveira ( The Strange Case of Angelica , MIFF 2010) anticipated the eruption of neorealism in Italy several years later by choosing to use nonprofessional actors and shoot on location in his home city. But while its greatness is now recognised, Aniki-Bóbó was largely dismissed in its day, and de Oliveira – the only filmmaker whose career stretched from the silent to the digital era, and one who remarkably continued directing beyond his 100th birthday – would not make another feature-length film for 21 years. In its spareness, the auteur’s first fiction film is an edifying counterpoint to his later, lavishly stylised works, and enchanting in its own right.
暂无 Letterboxd 评分；剧情 / 经典修复 / 澳洲首映。推荐理由：导演表达与人物处境。奖项/展映线索：暂无明确获奖信息，主要按评分、题材和导演风格推荐

英文原文简介In the hazy days between Christmas and the new school year, 14-year-old Sid Bookman has a chance to reinvent herself for the tourists who flock to her small New Zealand beach town of Ōmaha. She dabbles in all the rebellious teenage rites of passage – drinking, smoking weed, self-piercing and generally trying anything to impress the popular crowd – but also dips her toe into the tantalising and dangerous realms of the internet. As Sid encounters strangers in chat rooms, she flirts with the girl she has a crush on by impersonating her best friend’s brother on an instant-messaging app. Despite her desperate bids for acceptance, she captures the attention of her older sister’s friend Freya, who sees the real Sid underneath all the posturing. The debut feature from writer/director Paloma Schneideman ( Gate Crash , MIFF 2023), a former MIFF Accelerator Lab participant and graduate of Jane Campion’s film school program A Wave in the Ocean, Big Girls Don’t Cry is a sensitive, intimate and unflinchingly honest portrayal of queer adolescence. Ani Palmer’s remarkable debut performance steers the film, conveying Sid’s youthful angst, burgeoning sexual curiosity and uneasiness in her own skin with impressive restraint; while Noah Taylor ( Predestination , MIFF 2014) plays a key supporting role.

#252Chimney Town: Frozen in TimeLB N/A 长片

英文原文简介Though now hailed as the hero of Chimney Town, Lubicchi is struggling to move on after the departure of Poupelle, his magical friend made of garbage. When an accident transports him to a mythical world populated by talking animals and impish spirits, he is told by the realm’s rat queen that he can only return home if he manages to restart the land’s giant clock, which has been frozen at 11.59 for decades. With the help of Fluff, a large white cat with attitude, Lubicchi discovers that a grieving clockmaker and a plant spirit in human form are two figures who hold the key to his quest. The film adaptation of Poupelle of Chimney Town struck a chord in Japan and abroad when it emerged during the pandemic; Akihiro Nishino’s original picture book has since also been adapted into musicals, ballet and kabuki. Working from an original script by Nishino, this sequel is another grand family adventure dealing with big themes like grief and coming of age. Where Poupelle radiated steampunk vibes, however, Frozen in Time takes on a more fantastical, psychedelic style, constructing a visual world reminiscent of Hayao Miyazaki’s all-time classic Spirited Away .

The last-known footage of 16-year-old Krzysztof Dymiński – “Chris” to his friends – was captured in the early hours of the morning in May 2023 on CCTV: he is seen standing on a bridge overlooking Warsaw’s Vistula River; the camera pans away and back, and Chris is gone. One year on, little hope remains that Chris is still alive, but his father Daniel pours his immense grief into the task of at least filling in the narrative blanks. He trawls his son’s social media profiles and the river itself for clues, increasingly consumed by his search.

#254CorpusLB N/A 长片
2026 · 102 分钟 · 惊悚、恐怖 · 午夜 / 类型片 · 国际首映 · 导演 Corrin Evans · 美国
🏆 首映
英文原文Steaming into MIFF from its premiere at Montreal’s Fantasia International Film Festival, Corpus announces Evans as an exciting new voice in genre film.
这是一部2026年美国惊悚、恐怖长片。导演：Corrin Evans。MIFF 信息：午夜 / 类型片、国际首映。核心看点：音乐与表演、恐怖 / 超自然。
英文原文简介In the sultry New York summer of 1998, night-life photographer and small-time drug dealer Sayo (Jeff Wahlberg) reluctantly accepts a party invitation from rising movie star Vince (Brodie Townsend, Heartbreak High ), his long-time friend for whom he has complicated feelings. Their boisterous club buddy Ross is keen to tag along, so the three head upstate to an isolated mansion estate, ready to get rowdy. Instead, they find Billie, Wren and Cata – three mysterious women whose disturbing agenda draws them into a dark web of seduction and terror. Corpus is the feature directorial debut of Corrin Evans, whose interest in exploring eroticism onscreen led her to become an in-demand intimacy coordinator, who has plied her trade on such spicy fare as Ti West’s MaXXXine and Larry Charles’s Dicks: The Musical . She’s joined on this super-horny horror film by co-writer and producer Lily Cowles, who also takes centre stage onscreen as sinister photographer Billie. Steaming into MIFF from its premiere at Montreal’s Fantasia International Film Festival, Corpus announces Evans as an exciting new voice in genre film.

英文原文简介Drawing on thousands of films and TV shows about the Holocaust, this gripping, rigorously crafted supercut queries the ethics of representing atrocity. “Fiction is a transgression,” stated Claude Lanzmann, maker of the definitive Holocaust documentary, Shoah (MIFF 1987), in reference to Schindler’s List . “It is my belief that the depiction of certain things is prohibited.” And yet, World War II – and, at its core, the mass murder that was perpetrated by the Nazis – remains the most popular historical subject in cinema. Michal Kosakowski’s found-footage essay film takes Lanzmann’s famous statement as its provocative point of departure, assembling clips culled from a corpus of more than 3000 narrative works – from Rome, Open City to Inglourious Basterds – to reveal both the constants and the contradictions of this genre.

#265Kim Novak’s VertigoLB N/A 长片

英文原文简介People have rarely given Kim Novak the credit she deserves. She has been dismissed as a generic 1950s studio blonde; her slippery performance in 1958 psychological thriller Vertigo (MIFF 1984) is too often attributed only to director Alfred Hitchcock’s genius; and her long, fiercely private retirement is treated as the wreckage of Hollywood misogyny. All the while, however, Novak has been her own auteur. She fought Columbia Pictures boss Harry Cohn to keep her own surname, and went on strike for better pay. Now 93, she recalls Vertigo as a satisfyingly metatextual collaboration, reframing her life’s dizzying, spiralling narratives as “a big, beautiful circle”. In the prolific Alexandre O. Philippe, Novak finds an avid, erudite listener. His documentaries on cinema craft are frequently valentines to individual films: The Texas Chainsaw Massacre ( Chain Reactions , MIFF 2025), Alien ( Memory – The Origins of Alien , MIFF 2019) and Psycho ( 78/52 , MIFF 2017). Here, as in his William Shatner portrait You Can Call Me Bill (MIFF 2023), Philippe illuminates a complex person rather than worshipping a star. Kim Novak’s Vertigo celebrates an unforgettable movie through its subject’s refreshingly candid musings on the tensions between authenticity and mystique.

英文原文简介In 1994, at the age of 19, Jonah Lomu donned his first All Blacks jersey – the youngest ever to wear it. At the next year’s World Cup, the Tongan New Zealander winger’s jaw-dropping combination of power and agility redefined rugby union. Nearly 2 metres tall and 120 kilograms, Lomu could run 100 metres in 11 seconds and evade every tackle – former Wallaby Peter FitzSimons described him as “a freight train in ballet shoes”. Having grown up bilingual between Tonga and South Auckland, he used his cultural connection and Christian faith to transform the glaring spotlight of sporting glory into a torch to ignite cultural pride across the Pacific. But Lomu wasn’t superhuman. Privately, he battled nephrotic syndrome, a rare kidney disorder that would extinguish his stupendous, record-setting career. A humble, staunch Lomu emerges here in intimate interviews with his closest family, friends and coaches, along with archival footage and previously unseen family videos. Sensitively stewarding Lomu’s world-spanning legacy are Dublin native Gavin Fitzgerald, known for documentary profiles of Liam Gallagher and Conor McGregor, and Kiwi Tongan trailblazer Vea Mafile’o ( Lea Tupu’anga , MIFF 2024; For My Father’s Kingdom , MIFF 2019).

An underachieving millennial who still lives with her oversharing, open-minded-to-the-extreme single mother, Mary must now navigate dismissive doctors, a useless parenting partner and a whole host of discombobulating physical side effects if she is to reclaim autonomy over her body and her life. Expanding on their 2024 short, director duo Sean Wallace and Jordan Mark Windsor – aka THUNDERLIPS – bring an unmistakeably Kiwi self-deprecating humour to this outrageous comedy positively dripping in extraterrestrial bodily fluids. Hannah Lynch ( Petrol , MIFF 2022) shines as the unapologetically pissed-off Mary, and the visceral practical effects and tentacled prosthetics are a sight to behold.

#269My Life Without SteveLB N/A 长片
1986 · 53 分钟 · 纪录片 · 经典修复 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Gillian Leahy · 澳大利亚
🏆 获奖
英文原文...say film – shot on lush 35mm – was honoured at MIFF, the Sydney Film Festival and the AFI Awards on its release....
这是一部1986年澳大利亚纪录片长片。导演：Gillian Leahy。MIFF 信息：经典修复、澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实。
英文原文简介“After you left, I moved in here for a year, hoping that the view would pull me out of the misery.” Over a series of domestic tableaux – a copper kettle on the boil; a bulging vase stuffed with white daisies – a woman delivers a discursive monologue: the musings of a wounded heart, rich with intertextual references from Roland Barthes to Laurie Anderson and Bob Dylan. The speaker is Liz, a semi-fictive creation voiced by Jenny Vuletic but seen only fleetingly, as a night-time reflection in the window of her apartment overlooking Sydney’s bustling Blackwattle Bay. Inspired by the works of Chris Marker and Chantal Akerman and made during a notable period for women filmmakers in Australia, Gillian Leahy’s singular, sophisticated essay film – shot on lush 35mm – was honoured at MIFF, the Sydney Film Festival and the AFI Awards on its release. However, My Life Without Steve also ruffled feathers, with Liz’s exploratory and sometimes accusatory monologue critiqued by some as failing certain feminist ideals. Forty years later, in a culture attuned to prickly autofiction, the conversation seems to have finally caught up to Leahy.

#270MāramaLB N/A 长片
2025 · 89 分钟 · 剧情、惊悚、恐怖 · 午夜 / 类型片 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Taratoa Stappard · 英国
这是一部2025年英国剧情、惊悚、恐怖长片。导演：Taratoa Stappard。MIFF 信息：午夜 / 类型片、澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、记忆与历史、失去与哀悼、恐怖 / 超自然。
英文原文简介In 1859, Māori teacher Mary Stevens receives a mysterious letter summoning her from Aotearoa New Zealand to North Yorkshire, England, with the promise of revelations about her family history. Upon her arrival, lord of the local manor Nathaniel Cole offers Mary board and work as a governess for his niece. Nathaniel proudly shows off his collection of Māori artefacts and fluency in te reo Māori; he claims to have a deep affection for Mary’s culture and people. But the longer Mary stays in the windswept manor, the more she senses someone – or something – in the house is trying to communicate a grave warning. Taratoa Stappard’s striking debut feature is a chilling ghost story reckoning with the violence of British colonialism, taking the tropes and visual language of classic Victorian Gothic horror and redeploying them through a uniquely Māori lens. Ariāna Osborne runs the gamut from grief to righteous fury in her ferocious performance as Mary, while the lavish costume and production design combine with the tale to elevate Mārama to the pantheon of great ghost stories.

#271Nostalgia for the FutureLB N/A 长片
2026 · 75 分钟 · 纪录片 · 电影之梦 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Brecht Debackere · 比利时、意大利
这是一部2026年比利时、意大利纪录片长片。导演：Brecht Debackere。MIFF 信息：电影之梦、澳洲首映。核心看点：记忆与历史、失去与哀悼、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Chris Marker liked to describe himself as “the best-known author of unknown films”, but perhaps the opposite is true. Today, there is widespread reverence for works such as La Jetée , his fleet but haunting sci-fi almost entirely comprising still images (and that later formed the basis for Terry Gilliam’s 12 Monkeys ), and Sans Soleil (MIFF 1983), the existential travelogue that redefined the essay film. But Marker – one of numerous pseudonyms he used in his 91 years – very rarely gave interviews; averse to being photographed, he often used a drawing of his cat as an avatar. The director’s death in 2012 left behind 550 boxes of archival material. Together with excerpts from his groundbreaking body of work, these materials form the basis for Brecht Debackere’s probing but necessarily oblique portrait of the artist – as narrated by Charlotte Rampling ( Swimming Pool , MIFF 2003), the magisterial actor here personifying an archivist. In tune with Marker’s preoccupations, Nostalgia for the Future is a meditation on the slippery persistence of memory, personal as well as cultural: a precious souvenir for existing fans, and a beguiling introduction for anyone who wishes to peer behind his Cheshire grin.

#272Of WombLB N/A 长片
2025 · 90 分钟 · 剧情、实验、恐怖 · 午夜 / 类型片 · 世界首映 · 导演 Peter Firebrace · 澳大利亚
这是一部2025年澳大利亚剧情、实验、恐怖长片。导演：Peter Firebrace。MIFF 信息：午夜 / 类型片、世界首映。核心看点：家庭关系、亲密关系、政治与社会现实、记忆与历史、失去与哀悼、恐怖 / 超自然。
英文原文简介Three young women have been raised in innocence on a remote, dilapidated homestead, alone with their bedbound, intensely religious mother. Fuelled by a heady brew of existential terror, dogmatic belief and desire to dominate, The Eldest decides to hide Mother’s death from her siblings, telling them the Devil is lurking behind her closed bedroom door as sound and stench, ready to repay their curiosity with a terrible sickness. Among the paperbark trees, invented sacraments begin playfully but soon plunge the trio into a claustrophobic shared delirium, gasping towards a devastating collapse. Inspired by their own religious upbringing and fascination with European arthouse witch tropes, debutant West Australian director Peter Firebrace shot Of Womb with a tiny, close-knit cast and crew in a heritage-listed South Fremantle house with its own morbid history. Belying its micro-budget, this visually stunning psychological fever dream thrums with the ritual gestures of Dogtooth (MIFF 2009) and The Witch (MIFF 2015) and evokes the landscape-horror tradition of Picnic at Hanging Rock (MIFF 2018). The film’s own gripping simplicity, however, announces an exciting new voice in Australian cinema – one poised to disturb, provoke and captivate.

英文原文简介Sheri (Sara Thompson, One of Us Is Lying ) hasn’t been okay since her beloved grandma (Kerry Armstrong, Lantana , MIFF 2001) died. She’s over her annoying boyfriend Harry (Jordan Dulieu, The Serpent’s Skin ), and resents her astronomer dad Hank (Scott Major, Neighbours ) for avoidantly watching the skies. When a glowing green meteorite crash-lands near their small town and its passenger starts melding gruesomely with locals, humanity’s last hope is Sheri, her dad and her Scooby Gang of mates: Poppy (Annapurna Sriram, Fucktoys ), Ash (Karis Oka, The Deb ) and Finn (Jess McLeod, One of Us Is Lying ), whose run-down video store has become the alien’s lair. Prolific Aussie queer-horror phenom Alice Maio Mackay ( T Blockers ), directing her seventh feature at the age of 21, merges retro schlock and teen-culture cool with a sincere affection for chosen family. It’s the opposite of effed-up that Major – the 90s Heartbreak High OG himself – stars here, and that she’s casting North Americans as rural Aussie retail shitkickers. Meanwhile, Mackay is building her own enviable friend gang: Our Effed Up World is produced by Jane Schoenbrun ( I Saw the TV Glow , MIFF 2024), and it’s a joy to spot cameos from TV Glow star Jack Haven and Lesbian Space Princess (MIFF 2025) co-writer/director Leela Varghese.

英文原文简介Introduced languishing in a faded motel, the eponymous Phillip is a Brit and by trade a screenwriter, though he’s not doing much writing these days. He’s more interested in frittering his time away, pursuing flights of fantasy and intoxicating indulgences even as the line between the two grows ever fuzzier. In this, he’s aided and abetted by an aspiring actor with whom he’s enjoying a dalliance – though Phillip suspects the younger man might be mainly interested in his showbiz connections – and the drug dealer next door. The prolific and indefatigable Briggs has often worked closely with non-professional actors to craft narratives whose blends of fact and fiction are as riotous as they are discomforting; he previously garnered acclaim for his 2024 feature A Grand Mockery (co-directed with and starring Sam Dixon, who also appears in this film in a supporting role), which took out top honours at SXSW Sydney as well as the Best Director prize at Sitges. With Phillip Philadelphia , the Meanjin-born writer/director captures the garish, grubby beauty of the Gold Coast on 16mm, evoking Florida as seen through the lenses of Harmony Korine and Sean Baker yet also extending his own distinctively homegrown, eloquently vulgar style.

英文原文简介Jennifer Robinson, Amber Heard and Brittany Higgins have all experienced the full force of weaponised defamation laws – but these indomitable activists and survivors of gendered violence won’t keep quiet. In 2017, #MeToo replaced the social stigma of discussing gendered violence with public solidarity and support for victim-survivors. The re-silencing was swift, vicious … and legalistic. Alleged perpetrators now used defamation lawsuits as cudgels to punish survivors for speaking out, and to deter journalists from exposing prominent people to public scrutiny. As a barrister who famously stood up for Amber Heard in a long-running, all-too-public defamation case in the UK, Jennifer Robinson has dedicated her career to fighting against these attacks, witnessing firsthand how such actions drag survivors through emotionally, professionally and financially ruinous legal proceedings.

#277School for DefectorsLB N/A 长片
2026 · 93 分钟 · 纪录片 · 纪录片单元 · 国际首映 · 导演 Jeremy Workman · 美国、韩国
这是一部2026年美国、韩国纪录片长片。导演：Jeremy Workman。MIFF 信息：纪录片单元、国际首映。核心看点：家庭关系、成长与青春、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介In many respects, the pupils at Jangdaehyun School are like any other teens: they stress about exams and getting into college; they dance on TikTok; they joke and laugh with friends. And they dream about their futures – a radical act when you’re born in North Korea. But Jangdaehyun is in South Korea, and its 20 boarders are all children of defectors from across the 38th parallel. Surrounded by the overwhelming promise of cosmopolitan democracy and buffeted by the often-negative attitudes of their new neighbours, the school provides a haven where these kids are free to discover who they are and who they want to be. Over the course of a year, Jeremy Workman ( Secret Mall Apartment , MIFF 2024) embedded himself within the school with permission from the students, their parents and teachers, and filmed. The Jangdaehyun community became his collaborators, welcoming him and his crew into their day-to-day lives as well as sharing their harrowing memories, hopes and ambitions. In small moments and in defiant acts, School for Defectors gives empathetic voice to an unseen generation who refuse to let their pasts define them.

英文原文简介Walking home from grocery shopping one afternoon, roommates Ricky and Tepper stumble across a disturbing scene: six grown men lying on the ground, feverishly licking the pavement. From that moment on, everything changes for Ricky, Tepper and even Aura, the girl Ricky is newly dating. Time slips, space bends, reality morphs and little slimy minnows start to appear in Ricky’s pockets. The deeper Ricky investigates, the more he starts to believe that the three of them may be under the control of a mysterious entity known as “The Yellow Thing”. A stoner hangout movie with Lynchian stylings and an experimental spirit, Sour Minnows comes straight to MIFF following its world premiere at Montreal’s Fantasia International Film Festival, where it screened in competition. Directed, written, edited and shot by Harrison Atkins – who also edited Emily the Criminal (MIFF 2022) and Madeline’s Madeline (MIFF 2018) this film is his second feature after 2015’s Lace Crater , on which MIFF 2026 Bright Horizons juror Joe Swanberg served as a producer. Equal parts goofily funny and chillingly existential, this quintessentially LA trip is capably led by David Brown ( Jury Duty ), Chase Williamson ( John Dies at the End , MIFF 2013) and Suzanna Son ( Red Rocket ).

#279Sukundimi Walks Before MeLB N/A 长片
2026 · 93 分钟 · 纪录片 · 自然世界 · 维州首映 · 导演 Lachlan McLeod, Matasila Freshwater · 澳大利亚、新西兰、Papua New Guinea
这是一部2026年澳大利亚、新西兰、Papua New Guinea纪录片长片。导演：Lachlan McLeod, Matasila Freshwater。MIFF 信息：自然世界、维州首映。核心看点：政治与社会现实、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介When an Australian mining conglomerate announces plans to build a huge copper/gold mine and toxic-waste dam on Papua New Guinea’s Sepik River, local communities fear pollution and ecological degradation. The “Amazon of the Asia Pacific” snakes for over 1100 kilometres through virgin rainforest, and is one of the few remaining large rivers in the world whose water remains drinkable. It’s also home to tens of thousands, who’ve lived along the river for millennia, drawing on it for sustenance and spiritual lore. Led by the charismatic Emmanuel Peni, these communities begin to mobilise, coming together to fight the forces of old colonial power structures, extractive economic practices, multinational lobbying and the supposed inevitability of ‘progress’. At once an intimate study of community and a rousing work of cine-activism, this boots-on-the-ground – or canoes-on-the-water – documentary offers a regional David vs Goliath story with deep ecological repercussions. Melanesian New Zealander filmmaker Matasila Freshwater (one of the directors of Vai , MIFF 2019) and Australian documentarian Lachlan McLeod ( Clean , MIFF Closing Night 2022) collaborate with community members, their cameras invited to witness conversations, meetings and planning sessions. Filled with rich cinematography, Papuan folk songs and historical newsreels, Sukundimi Walks Before Me is a vivid portrait of virtuous defiance.

#280Summer TourLB N/A 长片
2025 · 80 分钟 · 纪录片、音乐 · 音乐电影 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Mischa Richter · 美国
这是一部2025年美国纪录片、音乐长片。导演：Mischa Richter。MIFF 信息：音乐电影、澳洲首映。核心看点：亲密关系、政治与社会现实、音乐与表演。
英文原文简介Jerry and Annie are young and in love – with each other, and with the music of the Grateful Dead. Setting out on the road to catch every show on successor band Dead & Company’s farewell tour in 2023, they journey across America and deep into the heart of Deadhead fandom. Meeting fans young and old and participating in the marketplaces and gatherings that sprout around the shows, they discover a true community, alternative ways of living and what the music means to a wideranging cross-section of Deadheads. Mischa Richter’s “love letter” to the communal roadshow of Grateful Dead tours is a deeply personal doc from a committed Dead devotee – as are two of the film’s producers, Chloë Sevigny ( Magic Farm , MIFF 2025) and Emily Mortimer ( The Party , MIFF 2017). Filmed on 16mm and from deep within the community of fans, Summer Tour isn’t about the band – who are never seen performing – but those who follow them. It adds up to a warm-hearted hymn to hippie culture that doubles as an exploration of how people find meaning, and belonging, in art.

这是一部2026年澳大利亚剧情长片。导演：Harvey Zielinski。MIFF 信息：澳洲电影、世界首映。核心看点：家庭关系、亲密关系、政治与社会现实。
英文原文简介City boy Jake is at a loose end. Unemployed, single and holed up in a granny flat behind his family home, he lives in the shadow of his cisgender twin brother, successful real estate agent Sam. On an impulse, he takes a trip to the remote country town of Sweet Milk, where his terminally ill, estranged father (Kieran Darcy-Smith) still lives, totally unaware that Jake has transitioned. When his dad mistakes him for Sam and Jake misses the moment to correct him, an unforeseen opportunity lands in his lap: to fit in as masculine in a place where nobody suspects he’s trans. Adopting Sam’s identity, he manages to connect with his father for the first time, while a budding romance with local Toby (Hunter Page-Lochard, Kid Snow , MIFF 2024) – himself an outsider in this macho setting – offers further reinvigoration. But the longer Jake spends in Sweet Milk, the more tangled the web he weaves. How long can he hold on to his secret, and what will happen if the truth gets out? Drawing on his own experiences, debut filmmaker Harvey Zielinski also stars in the dual roles of Jake and Sam in this fish-out-of-water dramedy supported by the MIFF Premiere Fund – a raw, sensitive tale about the long road to self-acceptance and the lies we feel we need to tell to fit in.

#282The FenceLB N/A 长片
2025 · 109 分钟 · 剧情 · 欧洲与英国 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Claire Denis · 法国
这是一部2025年法国剧情长片。导演：Claire Denis。MIFF 信息：欧洲与英国、澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、失去与哀悼、悬疑 / 犯罪张力。
英文原文简介Overseeing a major West African construction site, Horn (Matt Dillon) has a lot on his plate: the imminent transition to new Chinese financiers; the arrival of his much younger wife (Mia McKenna Bruce, How to Have Sex , MIFF 2023); a tetchy engineer (Tom Blyth, Benediction ); and, most pressingly, the on-the-job death of a local worker. As night falls, the deceased’s brother Alboury (Isaach de Bankolé, The Brutalist ) arrives like an apparition. He demands to take possession of his sibling’s body, and won’t accept “no” – or bribes, threats or delays – for an answer. One of the true living legends of art cinema, Claire Denis ( Stars at Noon , MIFF 2022) has made a host of films sensuously and dramatically interrogating the European footprint in postcolonial Africa, including her magnum opus, Beau Travail (MIFF 2000), and two previous collaborations with de Bankolé in 1988’s Chocolat (MIFF 2000) and 2009’s White Material . For this late-career work, she has adapted a 1979 play by Bernard-Marie Koltès, whose dialogue-rich scenes mount a surreal, uneasy examination of exploitation, power and posturing.

#283The LatcherLB N/A 长片
2025 · 80 分钟 · 剧情、惊悚、恐怖 · 澳洲电影 · 世界首映 · 导演 James Hunter · 澳大利亚
这是一部2025年澳大利亚剧情、惊悚、恐怖长片。导演：James Hunter。MIFF 信息：澳洲电影、世界首映。核心看点：家庭关系、亲密关系、政治与社会现实、失去与哀悼、悬疑 / 犯罪张力、恐怖 / 超自然。
英文原文简介American midwife Alice lives in an isolated house in rural Australia. Worn out by her job and wearied by an unspoken tragedy, she experiences waking nightmares and starts sensing an eerie presence creeping in from the shadowy bushland. As desolation overwhelms her, and with the threat inching closer, her only refuge is the very home where she lost everything. Can she vanquish her demons before they corrode what’s left of her sense of self? Inspired by horror classics Rosemary’s Baby and Don’t Look Now as well as fairytales and folklore, this startling, thematically complex feature debut uses atmosphere and symbolism to explore the repercussions of loss, silence and solitude. Informed by interviews with bereavement midwives and a mother who had lost her baby, director James Hunter ( Nest , MIFF 2021) prioritised visual and narrative restraint to create “an uncanny feeling of unease”; this laid the foundations for Lucy Lovegrove’s affecting lead performance, which brims with polished physicality and nuanced interiority. Gripping and full of gravitas, The Latcher portrays one woman’s unravelling and her eventual journey towards healing.

#284The Oligarch and the Art DealerLB N/A 长片
2026 · 120 分钟 · 纪录片 · 纪录片单元 · 维州首映 · 导演 Andreas Dalsgaard · 美国、法国、丹麦
这是一部2026年美国、法国、丹麦纪录片长片。导演：Andreas Dalsgaard。MIFF 信息：纪录片单元、维州首映。核心看点：亲密关系、政治与社会现实、悬疑 / 犯罪张力、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Unfolding like a Hollywood thriller, The Oligarch and the Art Dealer unpacks with exquisite precision all the shady details of the Bouvier Affair: a high-profile court case between Russian businessman Dmitry Rybolovlev, the notoriously private owner of the world’s most expensive art collection, and his former trusted art dealer and friend Yves Bouvier, a maestro of freeports – duty-free tax havens-cum-storage lockers for the ultra-wealthy’s Picassos, da Vincis, Klimts and Magrittes. It’s a case that shocked the world, not least because it forced Rybolovlev – a man without a phone number, email address or computer – into the open and shone a spotlight on the clandestine dealings and deliberate secrets of the global elite. In this engrossing documentary, Andreas Dalsgaard digs into the decade-long battle that began when Rybolovlev accused Bouvier of a billion-dollar scam, blowing up the once-symbiotic relationship that had helped both men to stratospheric financial echelons. Approaching the scandal with an exacting eye, The Oligarch and the Art Dealer allows each man to make his case – Bouvier directly; the elusive Rybolovlev through his lawyers – and the audience to draw their own conclusions. But when the stakes are this high, and the eye-watering sums behind them are even higher, can you trust anyone’s story?
暂无 Letterboxd 评分；纪录片 / 纪录片单元 / 维州首映。推荐理由：亲密关系、政治与社会现实、悬疑 / 犯罪张力、纪录片视角。奖项/展映线索：暂无明确获奖信息，主要按评分、题材和导演风格推荐

#285The Siege of ParadiseLB N/A 长片
2026 · 82 分钟 · 纪录片 · 纪录片单元 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Gar O'Rourke · 瑞士、爱尔兰
🏆 翠贝卡
英文原文Scoring a Special Jury Mention at Tribeca, this documentary turns its lens on overtourism in Italy’s Cinque Terre, dubbed “the most beautiful place in the world”. | Meanwhile, DOP Lukas Gut – recipient of Tribeca’s Special Jury Mention for Cinematography in a Documentary Feature – captures Cinque Terre’s painterly radiance, completing this...
这是一部2026年瑞士、爱尔兰纪录片长片。导演：Gar O'Rourke。MIFF 信息：纪录片单元、澳洲首映。核心看点：政治与社会现实、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介On the Italian Riviera lies Cinque Terre, whose centuries-old villages and postcard-perfect beaches attract around four million holiday-makers – including countless social media influencers – annually. It’s become one of the most photographed places in the world, but this fame also concerns the 4000 individuals who call it home. Some, like winemaker Bartalo and restaurateur Carmelo, have resigned themselves to this yearly influx that finances their region. Others, like fisherman Guido, lament its toll on tradition, while mediators like politician Fabrizia must weigh profitability against sustainability. Sanatorium (MIFF 2025) director Gar O’Rourke returns with another elegant exploration of culture and place, this time exploring tourism as a double-edged sword bringing both wealth and threats to residents’ way of life. Rather than cold statistics, the film grounds its investigation on compelling firsthand accounts from locals, along with two lifestyle influencers whose insights reveal Cinque Terre’s simultaneous value and expendability for visitors. Meanwhile, DOP Lukas Gut – recipient of Tribeca’s Special Jury Mention for Cinematography in a Documentary Feature – captures Cinque Terre’s painterly radiance, completing this robust, handsomely realised account of #travel’s true cost.

#286The Way We MoveLB N/A 长片
2026 · 94 分钟 · 纪录片 · 音乐电影 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Nicolas Davenel, Vanessa Joo Dumont · 美国、法国
这是一部2026年美国、法国纪录片长片。导演：Nicolas Davenel, Vanessa Joo Dumont。MIFF 信息：音乐电影、澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Amber Galloway specialises in live American Sign Language interpretation for music festivals and concerts. You might recognise her hip-hop swagger from viral online videos: she captures complex instrumentation and wordplay with her whole body, using facial expressions to evoke tones and moods. Now, this accessibility trailblazer is training new ASL music interpreters, including striving young Puerto Rican father Julian Ortiz and Angela “AV” Vilavong, a queer Laotian from Oakland. Can they master this complex skill in time to join Galloway onstage at Austin City Limits Music Festival? As her students wrestle with live interpreting’s complex cognitive demands and poetic creative choices, Galloway’s pedagogical flair is treated with due admiration by French directorial duo Vanessa Dumont and Nicolas Davenel. For their part, Ortiz’s and Vilavong’s gifts are also evident (the former went on to live-interpret Bad Bunny’s Super Bowl half-time show, while the latter has been onstage with Céline Dion and The Chemical Brothers). But this sensitive documentary deals with tough emotions, too: Galloway is grieving her son Elijah, who was himself a promising interpreter, as she tries to pull his surviving twin Joshua from a depressive spiral. Equally, we see how Galloway and her protégés’ proudly queer, ancestral and Deaf identities help them express music’s life-affirming power. Turns out the body doesn’t just keep the score; it keeps the beat.

#287Tina Arena: Unravel MeLB N/A 长片
2026 · 90 分钟 · 纪录片、音乐 · 音乐电影 · 世界首映 · 导演 Adrian Russell Wills · 澳大利亚
🏆 首映
英文原文This world-premiering documentary from Adrian Russell Wills ( Kindred , MIFF 2023) unravels her vulnerable yet tenacious private self in candid, dryly funny conversation.
这是一部2026年澳大利亚纪录片、音乐长片。导演：Adrian Russell Wills。MIFF 信息：音乐电影、世界首映。核心看点：家庭关系、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介Tina Arena has been in the music business for 50 years; after 25 albums, she’s had enough eras to make other pop stars envious. Born in suburban Melbourne to Sicilian parents, Filippina Arena became Australia’s darling in 1976, aged eight, on Channel Ten’s prime-time variety show Young Talent Time . Her breakout 1990 pop single ‘I Need Your Body’ raunchily repudiated “Tiny Tina”, and she went on to score a soaring run of 90s hits … but self-doubt, misogyny and tall-poppy syndrome drove her to reinvent herself repeatedly in the UK and France: taking to the stage; seeking adventurous collaborations; and singing in Italian, French and Spanish. Behind Tina the power balladeer and queer icon is the woman her family still calls Pina. This world-premiering documentary from Adrian Russell Wills ( Kindred , MIFF 2023) unravels her vulnerable yet tenacious private self in candid, dryly funny conversation. Also appearing in new and archival interviews are Tina’s two sisters; her mentor Johnny Young; and collaborators and admirers including Céline Dion, Marc Anthony, Ronan Keating, Jessica Mauboy, and Jessica and Lisa Origliasso of The Veronicas. In bringing herself undone, Tina movingly shows how music has made and mended her.
暂无 Letterboxd 评分；纪录片、音乐 / 音乐电影 / 世界首映。推荐理由：家庭关系、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。奖项/展映线索：首映

#288Tomorrow I’ll Be BraveLB N/A 长片
2025 · 80 分钟 · 剧情、喜剧 · 学校单元 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Bernd Sahling · 德国
这是一部2025年德国剧情、喜剧长片。导演：Bernd Sahling。MIFF 信息：学校单元、澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、成长与青春、亲密关系、音乐与表演。
英文原文简介Karl is 12, short, insecure … and totally in love. Does the much taller, literally out-of-reach Lea like him back? If so, how can he tell? And how is he going to deal with all the feelings that come with a crush in the meantime? An opportunity to understand these nascent feelings arrives when a teacher encourages Karl and his friends to make a nonfiction short film interviewing people about their first loves. While working on this project, Karl channels his longing into his own creative pursuits – taking photographs that he develops in his homemade darkroom, and composing a love song with his cooler older brother – in the hope of impressing Lea. A sweet take on a familiar summertime-coming-of-age narrative, this special film dares to regard the normal, everyday emotions of adolescents as meaningful and worthy of exploration, with director Bernd Sahling placing the camera at eye level with his pint-sized protagonist. Free from nostalgia and never melodramatic or preachy, Tomorrow I’ll Be Brave is perfectly attuned to tweenage feelings.

#289Vaka Moana: Ancestors of the FutureLB N/A 长片
2026 · 48 分钟 · 纪录片 · 世界首映 · 导演 Tom Murray · 澳大利亚
这是一部2026年澳大利亚纪录片长片。导演：Tom Murray。MIFF 信息：世界首映。核心看点：导演表达与人物处境。
英文原文简介Made in collaboration with Indigenous NGO Te Puna Marama Voyaging Foundation on location in the Cook Islands, Vaka Moana: Ancestors of the Future is a 48-minute immersive 360-degree experience that takes viewers on a journey to the remote atoll of Mangaia. We sail on a recreated version of the Vaka Moana (or ocean-going canoes) that a millennia ago brought the first people to the Polynesian Pacific – the very last stage of the great human migrations across planet Earth. On this journey, we sail with Pwo master Peia Patai, one of only 10 masters of traditional non-instrument navigation (guided by stars, swells, ecological signs). While visiting ancient celestial maps in limestone caves and journeying across the oldest island in Polynesia, we also learn about the Polynesian resource-management strategy of Ra‘ui: to only take what is needed in order to conserve our ecology for the future. Sailing a small boat across the precarious and finite planet Earth, we learn about this ancestral Indigenous sustainable practice that is urgently needed globally. This is an immersive experience with a deep message from Polynesian ancestors and knowledge-holders for the future of us all.
暂无 Letterboxd 评分；纪录片 / 世界首映。推荐理由：导演表达与人物处境。奖项/展映线索：暂无明确获奖信息，主要按评分、题材和导演风格推荐
