#290We Are The ShaggsLB N/A 长片
2026 · 100 分钟 · 纪录片、音乐 · 音乐电影 · 国际首映 · 导演 Ken Kwapis · 美国
这是一部2026年美国纪录片、音乐长片。导演：Ken Kwapis。MIFF 信息：音乐电影、国际首映。核心看点：家庭关系、成长与青春、音乐与表演。
英文原文简介Austin Wiggin’s mother had prophesied his daughters would become a famous band – so, in 1965, he decided to make it happen. He pulled Dot, Helen and Betty out of school; handed them instruments they couldn’t play; suggested they write songs without the first clue how; and named them The Shaggs. For years, they (occasionally accompanied by younger sister Rachel) endured weekly heckling at local gigs in Fremont, New Hampshire, before recording an album, 1969’s Philosophy of the World . When Austin died in 1975, the sisters could finally live regular lives … until the 90s, when they learned The Shaggs had become a cult band whose tastemaker fans included Frank Zappa, Patti Smith and Kurt Cobain. Their grandmother’s prediction had come true, in the most ironic way possible. One Shaggs evangelist is veteran comedy director Ken Kwapis ( Vibes , MIFF 2019; Malcolm in the Middle ). His film explores the strangeness of the sisters’ wildly out-of-tune guitars, eccentric rhythms and unorthodox chords, tracing their path from “the worst band ever” to outsider music stars, while music experts champion their intuitive brilliance. Meanwhile, gentle, bemused surviving Shaggs Dot and Betty muse on the phenomenon they’ve been caught up in.

#291WildernessLB N/A 长片
2026 · 101 分钟 · 剧情 · 澳洲电影 · 世界首映 · 导演 Martin McKenna · 澳大利亚
这是一部2026年澳大利亚剧情长片。导演：Martin McKenna。MIFF 信息：澳洲电影、世界首映。核心看点：家庭关系、成长与青春、亲密关系、记忆与历史、音乐与表演。
英文原文简介Allie’s life seems ideal from the outside: she’s a doctor, living with her teenage daughter and successful husband in an opulent modernist home. But she’s sleeping on the couch, hitting the wine hard, smoking again – prone to making bad decisions and picking fights with anyone who crosses her path. In the wake of a serious car accident, Allie runs. Hitting the road and hitting the booze, she sets off with her trusty dog Stanley and is by chance reunited along the way with her estranged friend Kaz, a sound recordist whose work chronicles environmental degradation. Travelling into increasingly remote stretches of alpine wilderness, her journey becomes primal, confronting the pain of the two women’s past and the unspoken realities of their relationship. Set in the picturesque surrounds of Victoria’s High Country, Wilderness is at once a midlife crisis movie about women behaving badly and a parable about listening to the environments that surround us. Built around a bold lead performance by Mirrah Foulkes ( Animal Kingdom ) and strong support from Yael Stone ( Blaze , MIFF 2022), Martin McKenna’s first film in over a decade is a thoughtful exploration of the balance between the personal and the ecological, and how urban landscapes can disconnect us from the planet and from ourselves.

#292YumburraLB N/A 长片
2026 · 86 分钟 · 纪录片 · 澳洲电影 · 维州首映 · 导演 Grace McKenzie · 澳大利亚
这是一部2026年澳大利亚纪录片长片。导演：Grace McKenzie。MIFF 信息：澳洲电影、维州首映。核心看点：亲密关系、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介In the wake of the success – and media furore – that greeted his landmark book Dark Emu , writer Bruce Pascoe retreated to his tract of land, a piece of Yuin Country in East Gippsland, near the Mallacoota Inlet and right by the New South Wales border. Seeking to put his teachings on First Peoples agriculture into practice, Pascoe and his partner Lyn Harwood set about building the infrastructure for sustainable farming, healing their strained relationship and deepening their connection to Country. Yumburra is shot in observational style by Grace McKenzie, who’s previously charted farming, landscape and community in the documentaries Audrey of the Alps and In the Land of Wolves (MIFF 2018). Following on from Allan Clarke’s 2023 documentary The Dark Emu Story and naturally intersecting with Pascoe and Harwood’s 2024 book Black Duck: A Year at Yumburra , it’s a film furthering explorations of Indigenous wisdom, traditional land management and the cultural conversations we need to have. At once a character study of one of Australia’s great writers – and great mavericks – and an unhurried depiction of life on the land, Yumburra makes a quiet, unassuming case for the lessons we can learn from elders and the environment alike.

#293Johanna d’Arc of MongoliaLB N/A 长片
1989 · 167 分钟 · 剧情、实验、奇幻 · Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels · 导演 Ulrike Ottinger · 德国
这是一部1989年德国剧情、实验、奇幻长片。导演：Ulrike Ottinger。MIFF 信息：Ulrike Ottinger: Radical Travels。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介The carriages of the Trans-Siberian Railway have never seen such a theatrical ensemble of strangers: the chic, high-society ethnologist Lady Windermere (Delphine Seyrig) can speak several languages; American Broadway star Fanny Ziegfeld (Gillian Scalici) is always threatening to break into song; Russian cabaret trio the Kalinka Sisters are always breaking into song; the reserved German schoolteacher Frau Müller-Vohwinkel (Irm Hermann) has a quiet but curious eye; and Giovanna (Inés Sastre) is a naive young woman with little else but a rucksack, a walkman and a yearning for adventure. After transferring to the Trans-Mongolian Railway, their fantastical train journey makes a sharp turn when a group of mounted Mongolian warriors under the command of Princess Ulun Iga (Xu Re Huar) take them as captives to their nomadic summer village. There, the women observe and attempt to adapt to the customs of their new society. Cast with Western actors and Mongolian non-professionals, Ulrike Ottinger’s 1989 epic was the first feature film permitted to be made in Inner Mongolia by a Western director. An ever-curious artist who would soon after return to film the people, environment and cultural customs of this land for her eight-hour 1992 documentary Taiga , Ottinger has stated that Johanna d’Arc of Mongolia “is not trying to create an exotic image, but to explore the issue of cultural transfer”. Depicting a dazzling clash of traditions and a stunning assemblage of colours and costumes against a vast landscape, this masterwork was frequent collaborator Seyrig’s final performance onscreen.

#294Rapid Eye MovementLB N/A 长片
2025 · 45 分钟 · Dance · 导演 Harry Yef, Bertie Sampson · 加拿大
这是一部2025年加拿大Dance长片。导演：Harry Yef, Bertie Sampson。核心看点：音乐与表演、恐怖 / 超自然。
英文原文简介Rapid Eye Movement invites audiences to explore dreamlike landscapes constructed from fragments captured in the physical world. Dreams are the raw material, while the human mind and body serve as the instruments. “Rapid eye movement” refers to the final phase of the five sleep cycles – the dream stage, just before waking – when elements from everyday life resurface and blend into a parallel reality. Ahead of the show, the artists launched an online form to collect dreams from the public. Anyone could contribute to the project, sharing dreams and nightmares, describing visions, or submitting images and sounds. Using these textual and visual elements, the artists have juxtaposed scenes and constructed intricate 3D architectures – abstract, stylised dream worlds that are at once familiar and surreal – combining creations and generative AI and merging music and live images. The resulting immersive performance blurs the boundaries between reality and the dream world in real time, accompanied by a film presenting key moments from the artists’ experimental process.
暂无 Letterboxd 评分；Dance。推荐理由：音乐与表演、恐怖 / 超自然。奖项/展映线索：暂无明确获奖信息，主要按评分、题材和导演风格推荐

#29529 Hour Long BirthdayLB N/A 短片
2022 · 6 分钟 · 纪录片、实验 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Mark Jenkin · 英国
这是一部2022年英国纪录片、实验短片。导演：Mark Jenkin。MIFF 信息：澳洲首映。核心看点：导演表达与人物处境。
英文原文简介While his breakout feature Enys Men (MIFF 2022) was wowing the international festival circuit, Mark Jenkin crafted this melancholic 2022 dispatch from his holiday in New York, a city whose familiar sights and sounds are rendered in the filmmaker’s signature super-8 style. Inspired by reminiscences of movies and punctuated with a spot of celebrity spotting, the film finds a city in the grip of sociopolitical chaos.

2026 · 13 分钟 · 剧情、惊悚 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 James Nolan · 英国、澳大利亚
这是一部2026年英国、澳大利亚剧情、惊悚短片。导演：James Nolan。MIFF 信息：澳洲首映。核心看点：悬疑 / 犯罪张力。
英文原文简介In this stylishly executed thriller set entirely within a London share house, a young Australian woman (Olivia Junkeer, Neighbours ; Why Are You Like This ) finds herself alone with the mysterious tenant staying in her friend’s room. Is he merely a perceived threat, or a very real danger? Playing with the familiar tropes of the domestic thriller, writer/director James Nolan strikes at the fears of anyone who’s found themselves in an uncomfortable renting situation with punchy, unnerving results.

#343Swing Swish SwayLB N/A 短片
2026 · 7 分钟 · 实验 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 TT Takemoto · 美国
这是一部2026年美国实验短片。导演：TT Takemoto。MIFF 信息：澳洲首映。核心看点：家庭关系、政治与社会现实、记忆与历史。
英文原文简介A brilliantly multilayered, textural homage to a pioneer of queer rights. Inspired by Filipina American paintbrush maker and queer rights activist Rosalie “Rose” Bamberger, this playful, reflective new work from queer Japanese American artist and scholar TT Takemoto uses an abstract collage of archival images to reanimate a forgotten chapter of history, in which the Daughters of Bilitis (of which Rose was a founding member) became the first US lesbian political rights organisation.

#344The Essential CornishmanLB N/A 短片
2016 · 6 分钟 · 纪录片、实验 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Mark Jenkin · 英国
这是一部2016年英国纪录片、实验短片。导演：Mark Jenkin。MIFF 信息：澳洲首映。核心看点：导演表达与人物处境。
英文原文简介Mark Jenkin’s 2016 vision of what may be a cove fisherman’s final voyage, shot on hand-processed super-8 reversal stock and sound-recorded to compact audiocassette, was entirely unedited in terms of writing, performance and visuals, and designed as a homage to the spontaneous prose that emerged from the Beat movement. In the filmmaker’s hands, the grizzly old fisherman is transformed into a mythical poet.

#345The Native PoliceLB N/A 短片
2025 · 11 分钟 · 剧情 · 维州首映 · 导演 Charles Perrurle Perkins · 澳大利亚
这是一部2025年澳大利亚剧情短片。导演：Charles Perrurle Perkins。MIFF 信息：维州首映。核心看点：政治与社会现实、记忆与历史、音乐与表演。

Tasked with escorting a young Arrernte girl, he is forced to reckon with the colonial-driven violence that is tearing his people apart.

#346The Story of Documentary Film (Part 1)LB N/A
2026 · 180 分钟 · 纪录片 · 电影之梦 · 维州首映 · 导演 Mark Cousins · 英国
这是一部2026年英国纪录片影片。导演：Mark Cousins。MIFF 信息：电影之梦、维州首映。核心看点：记忆与历史、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介The premier chronicler of all things cinematic returns with his latest plunge into film history – this time, shining a projectionist’s lamp on more than a century of reality-based storytelling. From 1895’s Workers Leaving the Lumière Factory through the cinematic achievements of Leni Riefenstahl, Agnès Varda, Frederick Wiseman and Abbas Kiarostami, the history of film can’t be told without documentary. Interrogating “observational films, campaigning movies, portrait docs, archive-based films, personal essays, music films, journey documentaries, experimental and animated non-fiction cinema”, passionate celluloid historian Mark Cousins ( Women Make Film: A New Road Movie Through Cinema , MIFF 2020) turns his lens on the vast corpus of documentary films. Fashioning unexpected connections and highlighting overlooked filmmakers, he reframes our ideas of truth, power and the pursuit of onscreen beauty.
暂无 Letterboxd 评分；纪录片 / 电影之梦 / 维州首映。推荐理由：记忆与历史、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。奖项/展映线索：暂无明确获奖信息，主要按评分、题材和导演风格推荐

#349Time Life Volume 9. Life ModelLB N/A 短片
2025 · 10 分钟 · 动画、实验 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Mungo Thomson · 美国

英文原文简介The mechanical gaze of a book scanner becomes a hyper-speed collage of anatomy. The latest in a hypnotic series of stop-motion montages from LA-based visual artist Mungo Thomson, this transformative work uses images from Time Life encyclopedias as raw material for an animated sequence of modelled postures and stances. Collage functions as choreography, and dance as a deceptively giddy refraction of modern life.

#350toward a fundamental theory of physicsLB N/A 短片
2025 · 13 分钟 · 实验 · 澳洲首映 · 导演 Victor Van Rossem · 比利时
这是一部2025年比利时实验短片。导演：Victor Van Rossem。MIFF 信息：澳洲首映。核心看点：导演表达与人物处境。
英文原文简介A uniquely tactile exploration of time and light, captured on 16mm film with hundreds of lenses. Using a handcrafted time slice camera equipped with 293 lenses, Belgian artist Victor Van Rossem resurrects a vintage photographic technique to create an incredibly immersive depiction of light on film, striking and almost spectral in its strange optical pull. In the film’s otherworldly space – its 3D tangle of colour and movement – light itself appears to become a physical object.

Captured immaculately on 16mm film with huge telephoto lenses, self-built jet-propelled cars hurtle through soupy mirages of blistering heat to a hypnotic soundtrack. A strangely ethereal silence radiates as everything but momentum falls away.

#360Consuming CultureLB N/A
60 分钟 · 对谈活动
MIFF 信息：对谈活动。核心看点：记忆与历史。
英文原文简介Each year at the Melbourne International Film Festival, a panel of guests gather to dissect the highs and lows of the zeitgeist. Host Michael Sun will be joined by two of MIFF’s visiting Critics Campus mentors – Los Angeles–based film programmer and critic Miriam Bale and writer and creator/curator of Black Film Archive Maya S. Cade, who originally hails from New Orleans – along with Melbourne’s own Harvey Zielinski, the writer, director and star of MIFF Bright Horizons Competition film Sweet Milk Lake . They’ll discuss the most overrated, underrated and personal–favourite moments in movies, TV, podcasts and books of the past 12 months. If all goes to plan, there’ll be hot takes, heated discussions and great recommendations to enjoy post-festival. Miriam Bale is a critic and film programmer. She has written for The New York Times , the New York Daily News , W Magazine , Gagosian Quarterly , The New Republic , Film Comment , IndieWire , Sight and Sound and many other publications. She was the artistic director of the Indie Memphis Film Festival in Tennessee, and has curated multiple repertory film programs worldwide.
暂无 Letterboxd 评分；对谈活动。推荐理由：记忆与历史。奖项/展映线索：暂无明确获奖信息，主要按评分、题材和导演风格推荐

#373The Story of Documentary Film (Part 2)LB N/A
2026 · 180 分钟 · 纪录片 · 电影之梦 · 导演 Mark Cousins · 英国
这是一部2026年英国纪录片影片。导演：Mark Cousins。MIFF 信息：电影之梦。核心看点：记忆与历史、音乐与表演、纪录片视角。
英文原文简介The premier chronicler of all things cinematic returns with his latest plunge into film history – this time, shining a projectionist’s lamp on more than a century of reality-based storytelling. From 1895’s Workers Leaving the Lumière Factory through the cinematic achievements of Leni Riefenstahl, Agnès Varda, Frederick Wiseman and Abbas Kiarostami, the history of film can’t be told without documentary. Interrogating “observational films, campaigning movies, portrait docs, archive-based films, personal essays, music films, journey documentaries, experimental and animated non-fiction cinema”, passionate celluloid historian Mark Cousins ( Women Make Film: A New Road Movie Through Cinema , MIFF 2020) turns his lens on the vast corpus of documentary films. Fashioning unexpected connections and highlighting overlooked filmmakers, he reframes our ideas of truth, power and the pursuit of onscreen beauty.

#375ÉcosystèmeLB N/A 短片
2022 · 37 分钟 · 实验 · 导演 Dylan Côté, Maxime Dangles · 加拿大
这是一部2022年加拿大实验短片。导演：Dylan Côté, Maxime Dangles。核心看点：音乐与表演。
英文原文简介The underwater world definitely isn’t quiet … and what we hear there tells a story. Through waves, boat engines, marine animals communicating, the icepack cracking or the sound of flowing water – proof of steady melting – this immersive film explores a little-known component of this ecosystem: its soundscape. Écosystème is the result of a long residency combining research and creation. The project originated from a team of marine ecology researchers who wanted to experiment with the links between art and science. Back from a polar mission, they called upon the talents of electronic music producer Maxime Dangles to create new musical material from their underwater sound recordings. To illustrate this sound journey, visual artist Dylan Cote set out to create a dark and enigmatic aquatic universe inhabited by synthetic and minimalist entities. The animated film dives into this world and explores its imaginary lands, guided by a narrative thread showing their progressive disturbance.
暂无 Letterboxd 评分；实验。推荐理由：音乐与表演。奖项/展映线索：暂无明确获奖信息，主要按评分、题材和导演风格推荐

A lonely botanist in early 20th-century Germany forms a mysterious connection with a rare plant, dragging him into a conflict between scientific ambition and human values. Torn between the pursuit of knowledge and personal redemption, he faces challenging moral decisions.
  • 著名导演伊尔迪科·恩伊迪以细腻诗意的镜头语言，营造出沉浸式历史氛围，展现科学探索下的孤独与欲望。

一名外来者在挪威峡湾小镇试图融入当地社区，却因文化差异和个人秘密陷入困境。主角面对外界压力与自我认同的冲突，逐步揭示人性与孤独的主题。
An outsider arrives in a Norwegian fjord town, struggling to fit into the close-knit community. Facing cultural differences and personal secrets, the protagonist grapples with pressure and identity, gradually revealing themes of loneliness and human nature.
  • 导演Cristian Mungiu以细腻现实主义手法描绘北欧冷峻环境下的情感隔阂与人性挣扎，氛围营造紧张。
  • Sebastian Stan与Renate Reinsve的对手戏极具张力，两人准确捕捉角色心理变化，表演层次丰富。
  • 摄影利用峡湾景观强化孤独感，画面构图极具美学价值。
  • Director Cristian Mungiu employs nuanced realism to portray emotional isolation and human struggle against the stark Nordic backdrop, crafting a tense atmosphere.
  • The performances by Sebastian Stan and Renate Reinsve are compelling, with layered depictions of psychological shifts.
  • Cinematography leverages the fjord landscape to intensify themes of solitude, offering visually striking compositions.
